BhG 2.1

saJNjaya uvAca
taM tathA kR^ipayAviShTam ashrupUrNAkulekShaNam |
viShIdantam idaM vAkyam uvAca madhusUdanaH ||1||

shrIdharaH : dvitIye shoka-saMtaptam arjunaM brahma-vidyayA | pratibodhya harish cakre sthita-praj~nasya lakShaNam | tataH kiM vR^ittam ity apekShAyAM sa¤jaya uvAca - taM tathety Adi | ashrubhiH pUrNe Akule IkShaNe yasya taM tathA, ukta-prakAreNa visam arjunaM prati madhusUdana idaM vAkyam uvAca ||1||

madhusUdanaH : ahiMsA paramo dharmo bhikShAshanaM cety evaM-lakShaNayA buddhyA yuddha-vaimukhyam arjunasya shrutvA svaputrANAM rAjyam apracalitam avadhArya svastha-hR^idayasya dhR^itarAShTrasya harSha-nimittAM tataH kiM vR^ittam ity AkAN^kShAm apaninIShuH saJNjayas taM pratyuktavAn ity Aha vaishampAyanaH |

kR^ipA mamaita iti vyAmoha-nimittaH sneha-visheShaH | tayAviShTaM svabhAva-siddhyA vyAptam | arjunasya karmatvaM kR^ipAyAsh ca kartR^itvaM vadatA tasyA AgantukatvaM vyudastam | ataeva viShIdantaM sneha-viShayI-bhUta-svajana-vicchedAshaN^kA-nimittaH shokApara-paryAyash citta-vyAkulI-bhAvo viShAdas taM prApnuvantam | atra viShAdasya karmatvenArjunasya kartR^itvena ca tasyAgantukatvaM sUcitam | 

ataeva kR^ipA-viShAda-vashAd ashrubhiH pUrNe Akule darshanAkShame cekShaNe yasya tam | evam ashru-pAta-vyAkulI-bhAvAkhya-kArya-dvaya-janakatayA paripoShaM gatAbhyAM kR^ipA-viShAdAbhyAm udvignaM tam arjunam idaM sopapattikaM vakShyamANaM vAkyam uvAca na tUpekShitavAn | madhusUdana iti | svayaM duShTa-nigraha-kartArjunaM praty api tathaiva vakShyatIti bhAvaH ||1||

vishvanAthaH : 
AtmAnAtma-vivekena shoka-moha-tamo nudan |
dvitIye kR^iShNa-candro 'tra proce muktasya lakShaNam ||1||

baladevaH : 
dvitIye jIva-yAthAtmya-j~nAnaM tat-sAdhanaM hariH |
niShkAma-karma ca proce sthita-praj~nasya lakShaNam ||

evam arjuna-vairAgyam upashrutya sva-putra-rAjyAbhraMshAshayA hR^iShyantaM dhR^itarAShTram AlakShya sa¤jaya uvAca taM tatheti | madhusUdana iti tasya shokam api madhuvan nihaniShyatIti bhAvaH ||1||

BhG 2.2

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca
kutas tvA kashmalam idaM viShame samupasthitam |
anArya-juShTam asvargyam akIrti-karam arjuna ||2||

shrIdharaH : tad eva vAkyam Aha shrI-bhagavAn uvAca kuta iti | kuto hetos tvA tvAM viShame saN^kaTe idaM kushalaM samupasthitam ayaM mohaH prAptaH, yata Aryair asevitam | asvargyam adharmyam ayashaskaraM ca ||2||

madhusUdanaH : tad eva bhagavato vAkyam avatArayati kutas tveti | 

aishvaryasya samagrasya dharmasya yashasaH shriyaH |
vairAgyasyAtha mokShasya ShaNNAM bhaga itIN^ganA || [ViP 6.74]

samagasyeti pratyekaM sambandhaH | mokShasyeti tat-sAdhanasya j~nAnasya | iN^ganA saJNj~nA | etAdR^ishaM samagramaishvaryAdikaM nityam apratibandhena yatra vartate sa bhagavAn | nitya-yoge matup | tathA-

utpattiM ca vinAshaM ca bhUtAnAm AgatiM gatim |
vetti vidyAm avidyAM ca sa vAcyo bhagavAn iti || [ViP 6.78]

atra bhUtAnAm iti pratyekaM sambadhyate | utpatti-vinAsha-shabdau tat-kAraNasyApy upalakShakau | Agati-gatI Agaminyau sampadApadau | etAdR^isho bhagavac-chabdArthaH shrI-vAsudeva eva paryavasita iti tathocyate | 

idaM svadharmAt parAÇmukhatvaM kR^ipA-vyAmohAshru-pAtAdi-puraH-saraM kashmalaM shiShTa-garhitatvena malinaM viShame sa-bhaye sthAne tvA tvAM sarva-kShatriya-pravaraM kuto hetoH samupasthitaM prAptam ? kiM mokShecchAtaH ? kiM vA svargecchAtaH ? iti kiM-shabdenAkShipyate | hetu-trayam api niShedhati tribhir vishesaNair uttarArdhena | Aryair mumukShubhir na juShTam asevitam | sva-dharmair Ashaya-shuddhi-dvArA moks icchadbhir apakva-kaShAyair mumukShubhiH kathaM sva-dharmas tyAjya ity arthaH | saMnyAsAdhikArI tu pakva-kaShAyo 'gre vakShyate | asvargyaM svarga-hetu-dharma-virodhitvAn na svargecchayA sevyam | akIrtikaraM kIrty-abhAva-karam apakIrtikaraM vA na kIrtIcchayA sevyam | tathA ca mokSha-kAmaiH svarga-kAmaiH kIrti-kAmaish ca varjanIyam | tat kAma eva tvaM sevasva ity aho anucitaM ceShTitaM taveti bhAvaH ||2||

vishvanAthaH : kashmalaM mohaH | viShame 'tra saN^grAma-saN^kaTe | kuto hetoH | upasthitaM tvAM prAptam abhUt | anArya-juShTaM supratiShThita-lokair asevitam | asvargyam akIrtikaram iti pAratrikaihika-sukha-pratikUlam ity arthaH ||2||

baladevaH : tad vAkyam anuvadati shrI-bhagavAn iti | 

aishvaryasya samagrasya dharmasya yashasaH shriyaH |
vairAgyasyAtha mokShasya ShaNNAM bhaga itIN^ganA || [ViP 6.74]

iti parAsharoktaishvaryAdibhiH ShaDbhir nityaM vishiShTaH | samagrasyety etat ShaTsu yojyam | he arjuna ! idaM sva-dharma-vaimukhyaM kashmalaM shiShTa-nindyatvAn malinaM kuto hetos tvAM kShatriya-cUDAmaNiM samupasthitam abhUt ? viShame yuddha-samaye | na ca mokShAya svargAya kIrtaye vaitad-yuddha-vairAgyam ity Aha anAryeti | Aryair mumukShubhir na juShTam sevitam | AryAH khalu hR^id-vishuddhaye svadharmAn Acaranti | asvargyaM svargopalambhaka-dharma-viruddham | akIrti-karaM kIrti-viplAvakam ||2||

BhG 2.3

klaibyaM mA sma gamaH pArtha naitat tvayy upapadyate |
kShudraM hR^idaya-daurbalyaM tyaktvottiShTha paraMtapa ||3||

shrIdharaH : klaibyaM mA sma gama iti | tasmAt he pArtha ! klaibyaM kAtaryaM mA sma gamaH | na prApnuhi | yatas tvayi etan nopapadyate yogyaM na bhavati | kShudraM tucchaM hR^idaya-daurbalyaM kAtaryaM yuddhAya uttiShTha, he parantapa shatru-tApana ! ||3||

madhusUdanaH : nanu bandhu-senAvekShaNa-jAtenAdhairyeNa dhanur api dhArayitum ashaknuvatA mayA kiM kartuM shakyam ity ata Aha klaibyam iti | klaibyaM klIb-bhAvam adhairyam ojas-teja-Adi-bhaN^ga-rUpaM mA sma gamo mA gA | he pArtha pR^ithA-tanaya! pR^ithayA deva-prasAda-labdhe tat-tanaya-mAtre vIryAtishayasya prasiddhatvAt pR^ithA-tanayatvena tvaM klaibyAyogya ity arthaH | arjunatvenApi tad-ayogyatvam Aha naitad iti | tvayi arjune sAkShAn-maheshvareNApi saha kR^itAhave prakhyAta-mahA-prabhAve nopapadyate na yujyata etat-klaibyam ity asAdhAraNyena tad-ayogyatva-nirdeshaH |

nanu na ca shaknomy avasthAtuM bhramatIva ca me manaH iti pUrvam eva mayoktam ity AshaN^kyAha kShudram iti | hR^idaya-daurbalyaM manaso bhramaNAdi-rUpam adhairyaM kShudratva-kAraNatvAt kShudraM sunirasanaM vA tyaktvA vivekenApanIyottiShTha yuddhAya sajjo bhava | he parantapa ! paraM shatruM tApayatIti tathA saMbodhyate hetu-garbham ||3||

vishvanAthaH : klaibyaM klIb-dharmaM kAtaryam | he pArtheti tvaM pR^ithA-putraH sann api gacchasi | tasmAn mA sma gamaH, mA prApnuhi, anyasmin kShatra-bandhau varam idam upapadyatAm, tvayi mat-sakhau tu nopayujyate | 

nanv idaM shauryAbhAva-lakShaNaM klaibyaM mA shaN^kiShThAH | kintu bhIShma-droNAdi-guruShu dharma-dR^iShTyA viveko 'yaM dhArtarAShTreShu tu durbaleShu mad-astrAghAtam AsAdya martum udyateShu dayaiveyam iti tatrAha kShudram iti | naite tava viveka-daye, kintu shoka-mohAv eva | tau ca manaso daurbalya-vya¤jakau | tasmAt hR^idaya-daurbalyam idaM tyaktvA uttiShTha | he parantapa ! parAn shatrUn tApayan yudhyasva ||3||

baladevaH : nanu bandhu-kShayAdhyavasAya-doShAt prakampitena mayA kiM bhAvyam iti cet tatrAha klaibyam iti | he pArtha ! devarAja-prasAdAt pR^ithAyAm utpanna ! klaibyaM kAtaryaM mA sma gamaH prApnuhi | tvayi vishva-vijetari mat-sakhe 'rjune kShatra-bandhAv ivaitad IdR^ishaM klaibyaM nopayujyate | 

nanu na me shauryAbhAva-rUpaM klaibyaM kintu bhIShmAdiShu pUjyeShu dharma-buddhyA viveko 'yaM duryodhanAdiShu bhrAtR^iShu mac-chastra-prahAreNa mariShyatsu kR^ipeyam iti cet tatrAha kShudram iti | naite tava viveka-kR^ipe, kintu kShudraM laghiShThaM hR^idaya-daurbalyam eva | tasmAt tat tyaktvA yuddhAyottiShTha sajjIbhava | he parantapa ! shatru-tApaneti shatru-hAsa-pAtratAM mA gAH ||3||

BhG 2.4

arjuna uvAca
kathaM bhIShmam ahaM saMkhye droNaM ca madhusUdana |
iShubhiH pratiyotsyAmi pUjArhAv arisUdana ||4||

shrIdharaH : nAhaM kAtaratvena yuddhAt uparato 'smi, kintu yuddhasya anyAyyatvAd adharmyatvAc cety Aha arjuna uvAca katham iti | bhIShma-droNau pUjArhau pUjAyAm arho yogyau tau prati katham ahaM yotsyAmi, tatrApi iShubhiH yatra vAcApi yotsyAmIti vaktum anucitaM tatra bANaiH kathaM yotsyAmIty arthaH | he ari-sUdana shatru-mardana ||4||

madhusUdanaH : nanu nAyaM svadharmasya tyAgaH shoka-mohAdi-vashAt kintu dharatvAbhAvAd adharmatvAc cAsya yuddhasya tyAgo mayA kriyata iti bhagavad-abhiprAyam apratipadyamAnasyArjunasyAbhiprAyam avatArayati katham iti | bhIShmaM pitAmahaM droNAm cAcAryaM saN^khye raNa iShubhiH sAyakaiH pratiyotsyAmi prahariShyAmi katham ? na kathaMcid apIty arthaH | yatas tau pUjArhau kusumAdibhir arcana-yogyau | pUjArhAbhyAM saha krIDA-sthAne 'pi vAcApi harSha-phalam api lIlA-yuddham anucitaM kiM punar yuddha-bhUmau sharaiH prANa-tyAga-phalakaM praharaNam ity arthaH |

madhusUdanArisUdaneti sambodhana-dvayaM shoka-vyAkulatvena pUrvApara-parAmarsha-vaikalyAt | ato na madhusUdanArisUdanety asyArthasya punar uktatvaM doShaH | yuddha-mAtram api yatra nocitaM dUre tatra vadha iti pratiyotsyAmIty anena sUcitam |

athavA pUjArhau kathaM pratiyotsyAmi | pUjArhayor eva vivaraNaM bhIShmaM droNaM ceti | dvau brAhmaNau bhojaya deva-dattaM yaj~na-dattaM cetivat sambandhaH | ayaM bhAvaH - duryodhanAdayo nApuraskR^itya bhIShma-droNau yuddhAya sajjIbhavanti | tatra tAbhyAM saha yuddhaM na tAvad dharmaH pUjAdivad avihitatvAt | na cAyam aniShiddhatvAd adharmo 'pi na bhavatIti vAcyam | guruM huN^kR^itya tvaMkR^itya ity AdinA shabda-mAtreNApi guru-droho yadAniShTa-phalatva-pradarshanena niShiddhas tadA kiM vAcyaM tAbhyAM saha saN^grAmasyAdharmatve niShiddhatve ceti ||4||

vishvanAthaH : nanu pratibadhnAti hi shreyaH pUjya-pUjA-vyatikramaH iti dharma-shAstram | ato 'haM yuddhAn nivarta ity Aha katham iti | pratiyotsyAmi pratiyotsye | nanv etau yudhyete tarhy anayoH pratiyoddhA bhavituM tvaM kiM na shaknoShi ? satyaM na shaknomy evety Aha pUjArhAv iti | anayosh caraNeShu bhaktyA kusumAny eva dAtum arhAmi na tu krodhena tIkShNa-sharAn iti bhAvaH | bho vayasya kR^iShNa tvam api shatrUn eva yuddhe haMsi, na tu sandIpaniM sva-guruM, nApi bandhUn yadUn ity Aha he madhusUdaneti | nanu mAdhavo yadava eva | tatrAha he arisUdana ! madhur nAma daityo yas tavArir iti bravImIti ||4||

baladevaH : nanu bhIShmAdiShu pratiyoddhR^iShu satsu tvayA kathaM na yoddhavyam | AhUto na nivarteta iti yuddha-vidhAnAc ca kShatriyasyeti cet tatrAha katham iti | bhIShmaM pitAmahaM droNaM ca vidyA-gurum | iShubhiH kathaM yotsye ? yad imau pUjArhau puShpAdibhir abhyarcyau, parihAsa-vAgbhir api yAbhyAM yuddhaM na yuktam | tAbhyAM saheShubhis tat kathaM yujyeta ? pratibadhnAti hi shreyaH pUjya- pUjya-pUjA-vyatikramaH iti smR^itesh ca | madhusUdanArisUdaneti sambodhana-punar-uktiH | shokAkulasya pUrvottarAnusandhi-virahAt | tad-bhAvash ca tvam api shatrUn eva yuddhe nihaMsi na tUgrasena-sAndIpany-AdIn pUjyAn iti ||4||

BhG 2.5

gurUn ahatvA hi mahAnubhAvA¤
shreyo bhoktuM bhaikShyam apIha loke |
hatvArtha-kAmAMs tu gurUn ihaiva
bhu¤jIya bhogAn rudhira-pradigdhAn ||5||

shrIdharaH : tarhi tAn ahatvA tava deha-yAtrApi na syAd iti cet, tatrAha gurUn iti | gurUn droNAcAryAdIn ahatvA para-loka-viruddhaM guru-vadham akR^itvA iha-loke bhaikShyaM bhikShAnnam api bhoktuM shreya ucitam | vipakShe tu na kevalaM paratra duHkhaM, kintu ihaiva ca naraka-duHkham anubhaveyam ity Aha hatveti | gurUn hatvA ihaiva tu rudhireNa pradigdhAn prakarSheNa liptAn artha-kAmAtmakAn bhogAn ahaM bhu¤jIya ashnIyAm | yad vA artha-kAmAn iti gurUNAM visheShaNam | artha-tR^iShNAkulatvAd ete tAvad yuddhAn na nivarteran tasmAd etad vadhaH prasajyetaivety arthaH | tathA ca yudhiShThiraM prati bhIShmeNoktaM -

arthasya puruSho dAso dAsas tv artho na kasyacit |
iti satyaM mahArAja baddho 'smy arthena kauravaiH || iti [MBh 6.41.36] ||5||

madhusUdanaH : nanu bhIShma-droNayoH pUjArhatvaM gurutvenaiva, evam anyeShAm api kR^ipAdInAM, na ca teShAM gurutvena svIkAraH sAmpratam ucitaH -

guror apy avaliptasya kAryAkAryam ajAnataH |
utpathapratipannasya parityAgo vidhIyate || [Mbh 5.178.24] 

iti smR^iteH | tasmAd eShAM yuddha-garveNAvaliptAnAm anyAya-rAjya-grahaNena shiShya-droheNa ca kAryAkArya-viveka-shUnyAnAm utpatha-niShThAnAM vadha eva shreyAn ity AshaN^kyAha gurUn iti | 

gurUn ahatvA para-lokas tAvad asty eva | asmiMs tu loke tair hR^ita-rAjyAnAM no nR^ipAdInAM niShiddhaM bhaikSham api bhoktuM shreyaH prashasyataram ucitaM na tu tad-vadhena rAjyam api shreya iti dharme 'pi yuddhe vR^itti-mAtra-phalatvaM gR^ihItvA pApam Aropya vrate |

nanv avaliptatvAdinA teShAM gurutvAbhAva ukta ity AshaN^kyAha mahAnubhAvAn iti | mahAnubhAvaH shrutAdhyayana-tapa-AcArAdi-nibandhanaH prabhAvo yeShAM tAn | tathA ca kAla-kAmAdayo 'pi yair vashIkR^itAs teShAM puNyAtishaya-shAlinAM nAvaliptatvAdi-kShudra-pApma-saMshleSha ity arthaH | himahAnubhAvAn ity ekaM vA padam | himaM jADyam apahantIti himahA Adityo 'gnir vA tasyaivAnubhAvaH sAmarthyaM yeShAM tAn | tathA cAtitejasvitvAt teShAm avaliptatvAdi-doSho nAsty eva |

dharma-vyatikramo dR^iShTa IshvarANAM ca sAhasam |
tejIyasAM na doShAya vahneH sarva-bhujo yathA || [BhP 10.33.30]

nanu yadArtha-lubdhAH santo yuddhe pravR^ittAs tadaiShAM vikrItAtmanAM kutastyaM pUrvoktaM mAhAtmyaM, tathA coktaM bhIShmeNa yudhiShThiraM prati -

arthasya puruSho dAso dAsas tv artho na kasyacit |
iti satyaM mahArAja baddho 'smy arthena kauravaiH || [MBh 6.41.36]

ity AshaN^kyAha hatveti | artha-lubdhA api te mad-apekShayA guravo bhavanty eveti punar guru-grahaNenoktam | tu-shabdo 'py arthe IdR^ishAn api gurUn hatvA bhogAn eva bhu¤jIya na tu mokShaM labheya | bhujyanta iti bhogA viShayAH karmaNi gha¤ | te ca bhogA ihaiva na para-loke | ihApi ca rudhira-pradigdhA ivApayasho-vyAptatvenAtyanta-jugupsitA ity arthaH | yadehApy evaM tadA para-loka-duHkhaM kiyad varNanIyam iti bhAvaH | 

athavA gurUn hatvArtha-kAmAtmakAn bhogAn eva bhu¤jIya na tu dharma-mokShAv ity artha-kAma-padasya bhoga-visheShaNatayA vyAkhyAnAntaraM draShTavyam ||5||

vishvanAthaH : nanv evaM te yadi svarAjye 'smin nAsti jighR^ikShA, tarhi kayA vR^ittyA jIviShyasIty atrAha gurUn ahatveti | guru-vadham akR^itvA bhaikShyaM kShatriyair vigItam api bhikShAnnam api bhoktuM shreyaH | aihika-duryasho-lAbhe 'pi pAratrikam amaN^galaM tu naiva syAd iti bhAvaH | na caiva guravo 'valiptAH kAryAkAryam ajAnantash cAdhArmika-duryodhanAdy-anugatAs tyAjyA eva | yad uktaM - 

guror apy avaliptasya kAryAkAryam ajAnataH |
utpatha-pratipannasya parityAgo vidhIyate || [Mbh 5.178.24] iti vAcyam |

ity Aha - mahAnubhAvAn iti | kAla-kAmAdayo 'pi yair vashIkR^itAs teShAM bhIShmAdInAM kutas tad-doSha-sambhava iti bhAvaH | nanu -

arthasya puruSho dAso dAsas tv artho na kasyacit |
iti satyaM mahArAja baddho 'smy arthena kauravaiH || [MBh 6.41.36]

iti yudhiShThiraM prati bhIShmeNaivoktam ataH sAmpratam artha-kAmatvAd eteShAM mahAnubhAvatvaM prAktanaM vigalitam ? satyam, tad apy etAn hatavato mama duHkham eva syAd ity Aha artha-kAmAnartha-lubdhAn apy etAn kurUn hatvAhaM bhogAn bhu¤jIya kintv eteShAM rudhireNa pradigdhAn praliptAn eva | ayam arthaH - eteShAm artha-lubdhatve 'pi mad-gurutvam asty eva, ataevaitad-vadhe sati guru-drohiNo mama khalu bhogo duShkR^iti-mishraH syAd iti ||5||

baladevaH : nanu svarAjye spR^ihA cet tava nAsti tarhi deha-yAtrA vA kathaM setsyatIti cet tatrAha gurUn iti | gurUn ahatvA guru-vadham akR^itvA sthitasya me bhaikShyAnnaM kShatriyANAM nindyam api bhoktuM shreyaH prashastataram | aihika-duryasho-hetutve 'pi para-lokAvighAtitvAt | 

nanv ete bhIShmAdayo guravo 'pi yuddha-garvAvalepAt chadmanA yuShmad-rAjyApahAraM yuShmad-drohaM ca kurvatAM duryodhanAdInAM saMsargeNa kAryAkArya-viveka-virahAc ca samprati tyAjyA eva- 

guror apy avaliptasya kAryAkAryam ajAnataH |
utpathapratipannasya parityAgo vidhIyate || [Mbh 5.178.24] iti smR^iteH |

iti cet tatrAha - mahAnubhAvAn iti | mahAn sarvotkR^iShTo 'nubhAvo vedAdhyayana-brahmacaryAdi-hetukaH prabhAvo yeShAM tAn | kAla-kAmAdayo 'pi yad-vashyAs teShAM tad-doSha-sambandho neti bhAvaH | 

nanu -
arthasya puruSho dAso dAsas tv artho na kasyacit |
iti satyaM mahArAja baddho 'smy arthena kauravaiH || [MBh 6.41.36]

iti bhIShmokter artha-lobhena vikrItAtmanAM teShAM kuto mahAnubhAvatA ? tato yuddhe hantavyAs te iti cet tatrAha hatvArtha-kAmAn iti | artha-kAmAn api gurUn hatvAham ihaiva loke bhogAn bhu¤jIya, na tu para-loke | tAMsh ca rudhira-pradigdhAn tad-rudhira-mishrAn eva, na tu shuddhAn bhu¤jIya tad-dhiMsayA tal-lAbhAt | tathA ca yuddha-garvAvalepAdi-mattve 'pi teShAM mad-gurutvam asty eveti punar guru-grahaNena sUcyate ||5||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.6

na caitad vidmaH kataran no garIyo
yad vA jayema yadi vA no jayeyuH |
yAn eva hatvA na jijIviShAmas
te 'vasthitAH pramukhe dhArtarAShTrAH ||6||

shrIdharaH : kiM ca yadyapy adharmam aN^gIkariShyAmaH tathApi kim asmAkaM jayaH parAjayo vA garIyAn bhaved iti na j~nAyata ity Aha na ced ity Adi | etad dvayor madhye no 'smAkaM katarat kiM nAma garIyo 'dhikataraM bhaviShyatIti na vidmaH | tad eva dvayaM darshayati | yad vA etAn vayaM jayema jeShyAmaH yadi vA no 'smAn ete jayeyuH jeShyantIti | jayo 'pi kiM cAsmAkaM katarat jaya-parAjayayor madhye kiM khalu garIyo 'dhikataraM bhaviShyati etan na vidmaH | tad eva pakSha-dvayaM darshayati etAn vayaM jayema, no 'smAn vA ete jayeyur iti | kiM ca jayo 'py asmAkaM phalataH parAjaya evety Aha yAn eveti ||6||

madhusUdanaH : nanu bhikShAshanasya kShatriyaM prati niShiddhatvAd yuddhasya ca vihitatvAt svadharmatvena yuddham eva tatra shreyaskaram ity AshaN^kyAha na caitad iti | etad api na jAnImo bhaikSha-yuddhayor madhye kataran no 'smAkaM garIyaH shreShTham | kiM bhaikShaM hiMsA-shUnyatvAd uta yuddhaM svadharmatvAd iti | idaM ca na vidma Arabdhe 'pi yuddhe yad vA vayaM jayemAtishayImahi yadi vA no 'smAn jayeyur dhArtarAShTrAH | ubhayoH sAmya-pakSho 'py arthAd boddhavyaH | 

kiM ca jAto 'pi jayo naH phalataH parAjaya eva | yato yAn bandhUn hatvA jIvitum api vayaM necchAmaH kiM punar viShayAnupabhoktum ? ta evAvasthitAH saMmukhe dhArtarAShTrA dhR^itarAShTra-sambandhino bhIShma-droNAdayaH sarve 'pi | tasmAd bhaikShAd yuddhasya shreShThatvaM na siddham ity arthaH | 

tad evaM prAktanena granthena saMsAra-doSha-nirUpaNAd adhikAri-visheShaNAny uktAni | tatra na ca shreyo 'nupashyAmi hatvA svajanam Ahave ity atra raNe hatasya parivrAT-samAna-yoga-kShematvokteH anyac chreyo 'nyad utaiva preyaH [KaThU 2.1] ity Adi-shruti-siddhaM shreyo mokShAkhyam upanyastam | arthAc ca tad itarad ashreya iti nityAnitya-vastu-viveko darshitaH, na kAN^kShe vijayaM kR^iShNety [GItA 1.32] atraihika-phala-virAgaH | api trailokya-rAjyasya [GItA 1.35] hetor ity atra pAralaukika-phala-virAgaH | narake niyataM vAsa [GItA 1.44] ity atra sthUla-dehAtirikta AtmA, kiM no rAjyena [GItA 1.32] iti vyAkhyAta-vartmanA shamaH | kiM bhogair [GItA 1.32] iti damaH | yadyapy ete na pashyanti [GItA 1.38] ity atra nirlobhatA | tan me kShemataraM bhaved [GItA 1.46] ity atra titikShA | iti prathamAdhyAyArthaH saMnyAsa-sAdhana-sUcanam | asmiMs tv adhyAye shreyo bhoktuM bhaikSham api [GItA 2.5] ity atra bhikShA-caryopalakShitaH saMnyAsaH pratipAditaH ||6||

vishvanAthaH : kiM ca guru-drohe pravR^ittasyApi mama jayaH parAjayo vA bhaved ity api na j~nAyata ity Aha na caitad ity Adi | tathApi no 'smAkaM katarat jaya-parAjayayor madhye kiM khalu garIyo 'dhikataraM bhaviShyati etan na vidmaH | tad eva pakSha-dvayaM darshayati -- etAn vayaM jayema, no 'smAn vA ete jayeyur iti | kiM ca jayo 'py asmAkaM phalataH parAjaya evety Aha yAn eveti ||6||

baladevaH : nanu bhaikSha-bhojanaM kShatriyasya vigarhitaM, yuddhaM ca sva-dharmaM vijAnann api vibhAShase iti cet tatrAha na caitad iti | etad vayaM na vidmaH | bhaikShya-yuddhayor madhye no 'smAkaM katarad garIyaH prashastataram | hiMsA-virahAd bhaikShaM garIyaH svadharmatvAd yuddhaM veti, etac ca na vidmaH | samArabdhe yuddhe vayaM dhArtarAShTrAn jayema te vA no 'smAn jayeyur iti |

nanu mahA-vikramiNAM dharmiShThAnAM ca bhavatAm eva vijayo bhAvIti cet tatrAha yAn eveti | yAn dhArtarAShTrAn bhIShmAdIn sarvAn | na jijIviShAmo jIvitum api necchAmaH kiM punar bhogAn bhoktum ity arthaH | tathA ca vijayo 'py asmAkaM phalataH parAjaya eveti | tasmAd yuddhasya bhaikShAd garIyas tvam aprasiddham iti | evam etAvatA granthena tasmAd evaMvic chAnta-dAnta uparatas titikShuH shraddhAnvito bhUtvAtmany evAtmAnaM pashyet iti shruti-prasiddham arjunasya j~nAnAdhikAritvaM darshitam | tatra kiM no rAjyena [GItA 1.32] iti shama-damau | api trailokya-rAjyasya [GItA 1.35] ity aihika-pAratrika-bhogopekShA-lakShaNA uparatiH | bhaikShaM bhoktuM shreya iti dvandva-sahiShNutva-lakShaNA titikShA | guru-vAkya-dR^iDha-vishvAsa-lakShaNA shraddhA tUttara-vAkye vyaktIbhaviShyati, na khalu shamAdi-shUnyasya j~nAne 'sty adhikAraH paN^gAder iva karmaNIti ||6||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.7

kArpaNya-doShopahata-svabhAvaH
pR^icchAmi tvAM dharma-saMmUDha-cetAH |
yac chreyaH syAn nishcitaM brUhi tan me
shiShyas te 'haM shAdhi mAM tvAM prapannam ||7||

shrIdharaH : upadesha-grahaNe svAdhikAraM sUcayati kArpaNyety Adi | arthAt kArpaNya-doShopahata-svabhAvaH etAn hatvA kathaM jIviShyAma iti kArpaNyaM dosash ca svakula-kShaya-kR^itaH, tAbhyAm upahato 'bhibhUtaH svabhAvaH shauryAdi-lakShaNo yasya so 'haM tvAM pR^icchAmi, tathA dharme saMmUDhaM ceto yasya saH | yuddhaM tyaktvA bhikShATanam api kShatriyasya dharmo 'dharmo veti sandigdha-cittaH sann ity arthaH | ato me yan nishcitaM shreyaH yuktaM syAt tad brUhi | kiM ca te 'haM shiShyaH shAsanArhaH | atas tvAM prapannaM sharaNAgataM mAM shAdhi shikShaya ||7||

madhusUdanaH : gurUpasadanam idAnIM pratipAdyate samadhigata-saMsAra-doSha-jAtasyAtitarAM nirviNNasya vidhivad gurum upasannasyaiva vidyA-grahaNe 'dhikArAt | tad evaM bhIShmAdi-saMkaTa-vashAt | vyutthAyAtha bhikShAcaryaM caranti [BAU 3.5.1] iti shruti-siddha-bhikShA-carye 'rjunasyAbhilAShaM pradarshya vidhivad gurUpasattim api tat-saN^kaTa-vyAjenaiva darshayati kArpaNyeti | 

yaH svalpAm api citta-kShatiM na kShamate sa kR^ipaNa iti loke prasiddhaH | tad-vidhatvAd akhilo 'nAtma-vid aprApta-puruShArthatayA kR^ipaNo bhavati | yo vA etad akSharam gArgy aviditvA asmAl lokAt praiti sa kR^ipaNa [BAU 3.8.10] iti shruteH | tasya bhAvaH kArpaNyam anAtmAdhyAsavattvaM tan-nimitto 'smin janmany eta eva madIyAs teShu hateShu kiM jIvitenety abhinivesha-rUpo mamatA-lakShaNo doShas tenopahatas tiraskR^itaH svabhAvaH kShAtro yuddhodyoga-lakShaNo yasya sa tathA | dharme viShaye nirNAyaka-pramANaAdarshanAt saMmUDhaM kim eteShAM vadho dharmaH kim etat-paripAlanaM dharmaH | tathA kiM pR^ithvI-paripAlanaM dharmaH kiM vA yathAvasthito 'raNya-nivAsa eva dharma ity Adi-saMshayair vyAptaM ceto yasya sa tathA | na caitad vidmaH kataran no garIya ity atra vyAkhyAtam etat | evaMvidhaH sann ahaM tvA tvAm idAnIM pR^icchAmi shreya ity anuShaN^gaH |

ato yan nishcitam aikAntikam AtyantikaM ca shreyaH parama-pumartha-bhUtaM phalaM syAt tan me mahyaM brUhi | sAdhanAnantaram avashyambhAvitvam aikAntikatavaM, jAtasyAvinAsha Atyantikatvam | yathA hy auShadhe kR^ite kadAcid roga-nivR^ittir na bhaved api jAtApi ca roga-nivR^ittiH punar api rogotpattyA vinAshyate | evaM kR^ite 'pi yAge pratibandha-vashAt svargo na bhaved api jAto 'pi svargo duHkhAkrAnto nashyati ceti naikAntikatvam AtyantikatvaM vA tayoH | tad uktam -

duHkha-trayAbhighAtAj jij~nAsA tad-apaghAtake hetau |
dR^iShTe sApArthA cen naikAntAtyantato 'bhAvAt || (Sa.K. 1) iti |
dR^iShTavad AnushravikaH sa hy avaishuddhi-kShayAtishaya-yuktaH |
tad-viparItaH shreyAn vyaktAvyaktaj~na-vij~nAnAt || (Sa.K. 1) iti |

nanu tvaM mama sakhA na tu shiShyo 'ta Aha shiShyas te 'ham iti | tvad-anushAsanayogyatvAd ahaM tava shiShya eva bhavAmi na sakhA nyUna-j~nAnatvAt | atas tvAM prapannaM sharaNAgataM mAM shAdhi shikShaya karuNayA na tv ashiShyatva-shaN^kayopekShaNIyo 'ham ity arthaH | etena - tad vij~nAnArthaM sa gurum evAbhigacchet samit-pANiH shrotriyaM brahma-niShTham [MuNDU 1.2.11], bhR^igur vai vAruNiH | varuNaM pitaram upasasAra | adhIhi bhagavo brahmeti [TaittU 3.1] ity Adi-gurUpasatti-pratipAdakaH shruty-artho darshitaH ||7||

vishvanAthaH : nanu tarhi sopapattikaM shAstrArthaM tvam eva bruvANaH kShatriyo bhUtvA bhikShATanaM nishcinoShi tarhy alaM mad-uktyeti tatrAha kArpaNyeti | svAbhAvikasya shauryasya tyAga eva me kArpaNyam | dharmasya sUkShmA gatir ity ato dharma-vyavasthAyAm apy ahaM mUDha-buddhir evAsmi | atas tvam eva nishcitya shreyo brUhi | 

nanu mad-vAcas tvaM paNData-mAnitvena khaNDayasi cet, kathaM brUyAm ? tatrAha shiShyas te 'ham asmi | nAtaM paraM vR^ithA khaNDayAmIti bhAvaH ||7||
baladevaH : atha tad vij~nAnArthaM sa gurum evAbhigacchet samit-pANiH shrotriyaM brahma-niShTham [MuNDU 1.2.11], AcAryavAn puruSho veda [ChA 6.14.2] ity Adi shruti-siddhAM gurUpasattiM darshayati kArpaNyeti | yo vA etad akSharam gArgy aviditvA asmAl lokAt praiti sa kR^ipaNa [BAU 3.8.10] iti shravaNAd abrahmavittvaM kArpaNyam | tena hetunA yo doSho yAn eva hatveti bandhu-vargam amatAlakShaNas tenopahata-svabhAvo yuddha-spR^ihA-lakShaNaH svadharmo yasya saH | dharme saMmUDhaM kShatriyasya me yuddhaM svadharmas tad vihAya bhikShATanaM vety evaM sandihAnaM ceto yasya saH | IdR^ishaH sann ahaM tvAm idAnIM pR^icchAmi - tasmAn nishcitaM ekAntikaM AtyantikaM yan me shreyaH syAt tat tvaM brUhi | sAdhanottaram avashyaMbhAvitvaM aikAntikatvaM, bhUtasyAvinAshitvaM Atyantikatvam | 

nanu sharaNAgatasyopadeshaH tad vij~nAnArthaM sa gurum evAbhigacchet ity Adi-shruteH | sakhAyaM tvAM katham upadishAmIti cet tatrAha shiShyas te 'ham iti | shAdhi shikShaya ||7||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.8

na hi prapashyAmi mamApanudyAd
yac chokam ucchoShaNam indriyANAm |
avApya bhUmAv asapatnam R^iddhaM
rAjyaM surANAm api cAdhipatyam ||8||

shrIdharaH : tvam eva vicArya yad yuktaM tat kurv iti cet, tatrAha na hi prapashyAmIti | indriyANAm ucchoShaNam atishoShaNa-karaM madIyaM shokaM yat karma apanudyAt apanayet tad ahaM na prapashyAmIti | yadyapi bhUmau niShkaNTakaM samR^iddhaM rAjyaM prApsyAmi | tathA surendratvam api yadi prApsyAmi evam abhIShTaM tat tat sarvam avApyApi shokApanodanopAyaM na prapashyAmIty anvayaH ||8||

madhusUdanaH : nanu svayam eva tvaM shreyo vicAraya shruta-sampanno 'si kiM para-shiShyatvenety ata Aha nahIti | yac-chreyaH prAptaM sat-kartR^i mama shokam apanudyAd apanuden nivArayet tan na pashyAmi hi yasmAt tasmAn mAM shAdhIti so 'haM bhagavaH shocAmi taM mA bhagavA¤ chokasya pAraM tArayatu [ChAU 7.1.3] iti shruty-artho darshitaH | shokAnapanode ko doSha ity AshaN^kya tad-visheShaNam Aha indriyANAm ucchoShaNam iti | sarvadA santApa-karam ity arthaH |

nanu yuddhe prayatamAnasya tava shoka-nivR^ittir bhaviShyati jeShyasi cet tadA rAjya-prAptyA dvAv etau puruShau loke ity Adi-dharma-shAstrAd ity AshaN^kyAha avApyety AdinA | shatru-varjitaM sasyAdi-sampannaM ca rAjyaM tathA surANAm AdhipatyaM hiraNyagarbhatva-paryantam aishvaryam avApya sthitasyApi mama yac chokam apanudyAt tan na pashyAmIty anvayaH | tad yatheha karma-jito lokaH kShIyata evam evAmutra puNya-jito lokaH kShIyate [ChA 8.1.6] iti shruteH | yat-kR^itakaM tad-anityam ity anumAnAt pratyakSheNApy aihikAnAM vinAsha-darshanAc ca naihika Amutriko vA bhogaH shoka-nivartakaH kintu sva-sattA-kAle 'pi bhoga-pAratantryAdinA vinAsha-kAle 'pi vicchedAc choka-janaka eveti na yuddhaM shoka-nivR^ittaye 'nuShTheyam ity arthaH | etenehAmutra-bhoga-virAgo 'dhikAri-visheShaNatvena darshitaH ||8||

vishvanAthaH : nanu mayi tava sakhya-bhAva eva, na tu gauravam | atas tvAM katham ahaM shiShyaM karomi ? tasmAd yatra tava gauravaM taM kam api dvaipAyanAdikaM prapadyasva ity ata Aha na hIti | mama shokam apanudyAt dUrIkuryAd evaM janaM na prakarSheNa pashyAmi trijagaty ekaM tvAM vinA | svasmAd adhika-buddhimantaM bR^ihaspatim api na jAnAmIty ataH shokArta eva khalu kaM prapadyeya iti bhAvaH | yad yataH shokAd indriyANAm ucchoShaNaM mahA-nidAghAt kShudra-sarasAm iva utkarSheNa shoSho bhavati |

nanu tarhi sAmprataM tvaM shokArta eva khalu yudhyasva | tatash caitAn jitvA rAjyaM prAtavatas tava rAjya-bhogAbhiniveshenaiva shoko 'payAsyatIty Aha avApyeti | bhUmau niShkaNTakaM rAjyaM svarge surANAm AdhipatyaM vA prApyApi sthitasya mamendriyANAm etad ucchoShaNam evety arthaH ||8||

baladevaH : nanu tvaM shAstraj~no 'si sva-hitaM vicAryAnutiShTha, sakhyur me shiShyaH kathaM bhaver iti cet tatrAha na hIti | yat karma mama shokam apanudyAd dUrIkuryAt tad ahaM na prapashyAmi | shokaM vishinaShTi - indriyANAm ucchoShaNam iti | tasmAc choka-vinAshAya tvAM prapanno 'smIti | itthaM ca so 'haM bhagavaH shocAmi taM mAM bhavAn shokasya pAraM tArayatu iti shruty-artho darshitaH | 

nanu tvam adhunA shokAkulaH prapadyase yuddhAt sukha-samR^iddhi-lAbhe vishoko bhaviShyasIti cet tatrAha avApyeti | yadi yuddhe vijayI syAM tadA bhUmAv asapatnaM niShkaNTakaM rAjyaM prApya yadi ca tatra hataH syAM tadA svarge surANAm AdhipatyaM prApya sthitasya me vishokatvaM na bhaved ity arthaH | tad yatheha karma-jito lokaH kShIyata evam evAmutra puNya-jito lokaH kShIyate [ChAU 8.1.6] iti shruter naihikaM pAratrikaM vA yuddha-labdhaM sukhaM shokApahaM tasmAt tAdR^isham eva shreyastvaM brUhIti na yuddhaM shoka-haram ||8||


__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.9

saJNjaya uvAca
evam uktvA hR^iShIkeshaM guDAkeshaH parantapaH |
na yotsya iti govindam uktvA tUShNIM babhUva ha ||9||

shrIdharaH : evam uktvArjunaH kiM kR^itavAn ity apekShAyAM sa¤jaya uvAca evam ity Adi | spaShTArthaH ||9||

madhusUdanaH : tad-anantaram arjunaH kiM kR^itavAn iti dhR^itarAShTrAkAN^kShAyAM sa¤jaya uvAca evam ity Adi | guDAkesho jitAlasyaH parantapaH shatru-tApano 'rjuno hR^iShIkeshaM sarvendriya-pravartakatvenAntaryAmiNaM govindaM gAM veda-lakShaNAM vANIM vindatIti vyutpattyA sarva-vedopAdAnatvena sarvaj~nam AdAv evaM kathaM bhIShmam ahaM saN^khya ity AdinA yuddha-svarUpAyogyatAm uktvA tad-anantaraM na yotsya iti yuddha-phalAbhAvaM coktvA tUShNIM babhUva bAhyendriya-vyApArasya yuddhArthaM pUrvaM kR^itasya nivR^ittyA nirvyApAro jAta ity arthaH | svabhAvato jitAlasye sarva-shatru-tApane ca tasminn Agantukam Alasyam atApakatvaM ca nAspadam AdhAsyatIti dyotayituM ha-shabdaH | govinda-hR^iShIkesha-padAbhyAM sarvaj~natva-sarva-shaktitva-sUcakAbhyAM bhagavatas tan-mohApanodanam anAyAsa-sAdhyam iti sUcitam ||9||

vishvanAthaH : Nothing.

baladevaH : tato 'rjunaH kim akarod ity apekShAyAM sa¤jaya uvAca evam uktvety Adi | guDAkesho hR^iShIkeshaM prati evaM na hi prapashyAmIty AdinA yuddhasya shokAnivartakatvam uktvA parantapo 'pi govindaM sarva-vedaj~naM prati na yotsye iti coktveti yojyam | tatra hR^iShIkeshatvAd buddhiM yuddhe pravartayiShyati | sarva-veda-vittvAd yuddhe sva-dharmatvaM grAhayiShyatIti vyajya dhR^itarAShTra-hR^idi saJNjAtA sva-putra-rAjyAshA nirasyate ||9||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.10

tam uvAca hR^iShIkeshaH prahasann iva bhArata |
senayor ubhayor madhye viShIdantam idaM vacaH ||10||

shrIdharaH : tataH kiM vR^ittam ity apekShAyAm Aha tam uvAceti | prahasann iva prasanna-mukhaH sann ity arthaH ||10||

madhusUdanaH : evaM yuddham upekShitavaty apy arjune bhagavAn nopekShitavAn iti dhR^itarAShTra-durAshA-nirAsAyA 'ha tam uvAceti | senayor ubhayor madhye yuddhodyamenAgatya tad-virodhinaM viShAdaM mohaM prApnuvantaM tam arjunaM prahasann ivAnucitAcAraNa-prakAshanena lajjAmbudhau majjayann iva hR^iShIkeshaH sarvAntaryAmI bhagavAn idaM vakShyamANam ashocyAn ity Adi vacaH parama-gambhIrArtham anucitAcaraNa-prakAshakam uktavAn na tûpekShitavAn ity arthaH | 

anucitAcaraNa-prakAshanena lajjotpAdanaM prahAsaH | lajjA ca duHkhAtmiketi dveSha-viShaya eva sa mukhyaH | arjunasya tu bhagavat-kR^ipA-viShayatvAd anucitAcaraNa-prakAshanasya ca vivekotpatti-hetutvAd eka-dalAbhAvena gauNa evAyaM prahAsa iti kathayitum iva-shabdaH | lajjAm utpAdayitum iva vivkam utpAdayitum arjunasyAnucitAcaraNaM bhagavatA prakAshyate | lajjotpattis tu nAntarIyakatayAstu mAstu veti na vivakShiteti bhAvaH | 

yadi hi yuddhArambhAt prAg eva sthito yuddham upekSheta tadA nAnucitaM kuryAt | mahatA saMrambheNa tu yuddha-bhUmAv Agatya tad-upekShaNam atIvAnucitam iti kathayituM senayor ity Adi-visheShaNam | etac cAshocyAnityAdau spaShTaM bhaviShyati ||10||

vishvanAthaH : aho tvApy etAvAn khalv aviveka iti sakhya-bhAvena taM prahasan anaucitya-prakAshena lajjAmbudhau nimajjayan iveti tadAnIM shiShya-bhAvaM prApte tasmin hAsyam anucitam ity adharoShTha-niku¤canena hAsyam AvR^iNvaMsh cety arthaH | hR^iShIkesha iti pUrvaM premAivArjuna-vAÇ-niyamyo 'pi sAmpratam arjuna-hita-kAritvAt premNaivArjuna-mano-niyantApi bhavatIti bhAvaH | senayor ubhayor madhe ity arjunasya viShAdo bhagavatA prabodhash ca ubhAbhyAM senAbhyAM sAmAnyato dR^iShTa eveti bhAvaH ||10||

baladevaH : vyaN^gam arthaM prakAshayann Aha tam uvAceti taM viShIdantam arjunaM prati hR^iShIkesho bhagavAn ashocyAn ity Adikam atigambhIrArthaM vacanam uvAca | ahotavApIdR^ig vivekaH iti sakhya-bhAvena prahasan | anaucitya-bhAShitvena trapA-sindhau nimajjayan ity arthaH | iveti tadaiva shiShyatAM prApte tasmin hAsAnaucityAdIShad adharollAsaM kurvann ity arthaH | arjunasya viShAdo bhagavatA tasyopadeshash ca sarva-sAkShika iti bodhayituM senayor ubhayor ity etat ||10||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.11

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca
ashocyAn anvashocas tvaM praj~nA-vAdAMsh ca bhAShase |
gatAsUn agatAsUMsh ca nAnushocanti paNDitAH ||11||

shrIdharaH : dehAtmanor avivekAd asyaivaM shoko bhavatIti tad-viveka-darshanArthaM shrI-bhagavAn uvAca ashocyAn ity Adi | shokasyAviShayI-bhUtAn eva bandhUn tvam anvashocaH anushocitavAn asi dR^iShTvemAn svajanAn kR^iShNa ity AdinA | tatra kutas tvA kashmalam idaM viShame samupasthitam ity AdinA mayA bodhito 'pi punash ca praj~nAvatAM paNDitAnAM vAdAn shabdAn kathaM bhIShmam ahaM saN^khye ity AdIn kevalaM bhAShase, na tu paNDito 'si, yataH gatAsUn gata-prANAn bandhUn agatAsUMsh ca jIvato 'pi, bandhu-hInA ete kathaM jIviShyantIti nAnushocanti paNDitA vivekinaH ||11||

madhusUdanaH : HERE

vishvanAthaH : bho arjuna ! tavAyaM bandha-vadha-hetukaH shoko bhrama-mUlaka eva, tathA kathaM bhIShmam ahaM saN^khye ity Adiko vivekash cApraj~nA-mUlaka evety Aha ashocyAn ity Adi | ashocyAn shokAnArhAn eva tvam anvashoco 'nushocitavAn asi | tathA tvAM prabodhayantaM mAM prati praj~nA-vAdAn praj~nAyAM satyAm eva ye vAdAH kathaM bhIShmam ahaM saN^khye ity AdIni vAkyAni tAn bhAShase, na tu tava kApi praj~nA vartate iti bhAvaH | yataH paNDitAH praj~nAvanto gatAsUn gatA niHsR^itA bhavanty asavo yebhyas tAn sthUla-dehAn na shocanti, teShAM nashvara-bhAvatvAd iti bhAvaH | agatAsUn aniHsR^ita-prANAn sUkShma-dehAn api na shocanti, te hi mukteH pUrvaM nashvarA eva | ubhayeShAm api tathA tathA svabhAvasya duShpariharatvAt | mUrkhAs tu pirtrAdi-dehebhyaH prANeShu niHsR^iteShv eva shocanti, sUkShma-dehAMs tu na, te prAyaH paricinvantyas atas tair alam | ete hi sarve bhIShmAdayaH sthUla-sUkShma-deha-sahitA AtmAna eva | AtmanAM tu ityatvAt teShu shoka-pravR^ittir eva nAstIty atas tvayA yat pUrvam artha-shAstrAt dharma-shAstraM balavad ity uktaM tatra mayA tu dharma-shAstrAd api j~nAna-shAstraM balavad ity ucyata iti bhAvaH ||11||

baladevaH : evaM arjune tUShNIM sthite tad-buddhim AkShipan bhagavAn Aha ashocyAn iti | he arjuna ! ashocyAn shocitum ayogyAn eva dhArtarAShTrAMs tvaM anvashocaH shocitavAn asi | tathA mAM prati praj~nA-vAdAn praj~nAvatAm iva vacanAni dR^iShTvemaM svajanam ity AdIni, kathaM bhIShmam ity AdIni ca bhAShase, na ca te praj~nA-lesho 'py astIti bhAvaH | ye tu praj~nAvantas te gatAsUn nirgata-prANAn sthUla-dehAn, agatAsUMsh cAnirgata-prANAn sUkShma-dehAMsh ca, shabdAd Atmanash ca na shocanti | ayam arthaH - shokaH sthUla-dehAnAM vinAshitvAt, nAntyaH sUkShma-dehAnAM mukteH prAg avainAshitvAt tadvatAm AtmanAM tu ShaD-bhAva-vikAra-varjitAnAM nityatvAn na shocyAteti | dehAtma-svabhAva-vidAM na ko 'pi shoka-hetuH | yad-artha-shAstrAd dharma-shAstrasya balavattvam ucyate | tat kila tato 'pi balavatA j~nAna-shAstreNa pratyucyate | tasmAd ashocye shocya-bhramaH pAmara-sAdhAraNaH paNDitasya te na yogya iti bhAvaH ||11||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.12

na tv evAhaM jAtu nAsaM na tvaM neme janAdhipAH |
na caiva na bhaviShyAmaH sarve vayam ataH param ||12||

shrIdharaH : ashocyatve hetum Aha na tv evAham iti | yathAhaM parameshvaro jAtu kadAcit lIlA-vigrahasyAvirbhAva-tirobhAvato nAsam iti tu naiva | api tv Asam eva anAditvAt | na ca tvaM nAsIH nAbhUH, api tv AsIr eva | ime vA janAdhipA nR^ipA nAsann iti na, api tu Asann eva mad-aMshatvAt | tathAtaH param ita upary api na bhaviShyAmo na sthAsyAma iti ca naiva, api tu sthAsyAma eveti janma-maraNa-shUnyatvAd ashocyA ity arthaH ||12||

madhusUdanaH :

vishvanAthaH : athavA sakhe tvAm aham evaM pR^icchAmi | kiM ca prItyAspadasya maraNe dR^iShTe sati shoko jAyate, tatreha prItyAspadam AtmA deho vA ? sarveShAm eva bhUtAnAM nR^ipa svAtmaiva vallabhaH [BhP 10.14.57] iti shukokter Atmaiva prIty-Aspadam iti cet tarhi jIveshvara-bhedena dvividhasyaivAtmano nityatvAd eva maraNAbhAvAd AtmA shokasya viShayo nety Aha na tv evAham iti | ahaM paramAtmA jAtu kadAcid api pUrvaM nAsam iti na, api tv Asam eva | tathA tvam api jIvAtmA AsIr eva | tatheme janAdhipA rAjAnash ca jIvAtmAna Asann eveti prAg-abhAvAbhAvo darshitaH | tathA sarve vayam ahaM tvam ime janAdhipAsh cAtaH paraM na bhaviShyAmo na sthAsyAma iti na, api tu sthAsyAma eveti dhvaMsAbhAvash ca darshita iti paramAtmano jIvAtmanAM ca nityatvAd AtmA na shoka-viShaya iti sAdhitam | atra shrutayaH - nityo nityAnAM cetanash cetanAnAm eko bahUnAM yo vidadhAti kAmAn [ÁvetU 6.13] ity AdyAH ||12||

baladevaH : evam asthAna-shocitvAd apANDityam arjunasyApAdya tattva-jij~nAsuM niyojitA¤jaliM taM prati sarveshvaro bhagavAn nityo nityAnAM cetanash cetanAnAm eko bahUnAM yo vidadhAti kAmAn [ÁvetU 6.13] iti shruti-siddhaM svasmAj jIvAnAM ca pAramarthikaM bhedam Aha na tv evAham iti | he arjuna ! ahaM sarveshvaro bhagavAn itaH 
pUrvasminn Adau kAle jAtu kadAcin nAsam iti na, api tv Asam eva | tathA tvam arjuno nAsIr iti na, kintv AsIr eva | ime janAdhipA rAjAno nAsann iti na, kintv Asann eva | tathetaH parasminn ante kAle sarve vayam ahaM ca tvaM ca ime ca na bhaviShyAma iti na, kintu bhaviShyAma eveti | sarveshvaravaj jIvAnAM ca traikAlika-sattA-yogitvAt tad-viShayako na shoko yukta ity arthaH | na cAvidyA-kR^itatvAd vyavahAriko 'yaM bhedaH | sarvaj~ne bhagavaty avidyA-yogAt | idaM j~nAnam upAshritya ity AdinA mokShe 'pi tasyAbhidAsyamAnatvAc ca | na cAbhedaj~nasyApi harer bAdhitAnuvR^itti-nyAyeneyam arjunAdi-bheda-dR^iShTir iti vAcyam | tathA saty upadeshAsiddheH | maru-marIcikAdAv udaka-buddhir bAdhitApy anuvartamAnA mithyArtha-viShayatva-nishcayAn nodakAharaNAdau pravartayed evam abheda-bodha-bAdhitApy anuvartamAnArjunAdi-bheda-dR^iShTis tattva-nishcayAn nopadeshAdau pravartayiShyatIti yat ki¤cid etat | 

nanu phalavaty aj~nAte 'rthe shAstra-tAtparya-vIkShaNAt tAdR^isho 'bhedas tAtparya-viShayo vaiphalyAj j~nAtatvAc ca | bhedas tad-viShayo na syAt, kintu adbhyo vA eSha prAtar udety apaH sAyaM pravishati ity Adi-shruty-arthavad anuvAdya eva sa iti cen mandam etat | pR^ithag AtmAnaM preritAraM ca matvA juShTas tatas tenAmR^itatvam eti [ÁvetU 1.6] ity AdinA bheda evAmR^itatva-phala-shravaNAt | viruddha-dharmAvacchinna-pratiyogikatayA loke tasyAj~nAtatvAc ca | te ca dharmA vibhutvANutva-svAmitva-bhR^ityatvAdayaH shAstraika-gamyA mitho viruddhA bodhyAH | abhedas tv aphalas tatra phalAnaN^gIkArAt | aj~nAtash ca shasha-shR^iN^gavad asattvAt | tasmAt paramArthikas tad-bhedaH siddhaH ||12||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.13

dehino 'smin yathA dehe kaumAraM yauvanaM jarA |
tathA dehAntara-prAptir dhIras tatra na muhyati ||13||

shrIdharaH : nanv Ishvarasya tava janmAdi-shUnyatvaM satyam eva, jIvAnAM tu janma-maraNe prasiddhe | tatrAha dehina ity Adi | dehino dehAbhimAnino jIvasya yathAsmin sthUla-dehe kaumArAdy-avasthAs tad-deha-nibandhanA eva, na tu svataH, pUrvAvAsthA-nAshe |vasthAntarotpattAv api sa evAham iti pratyabhij~nAnAt | tathaiva etad-deha-nAshe dehAntara-prAptir api liN^ga-deha-nibandhanaiva | na tAvad Atmano nAshaH, jAta-mAtrasya pUrva-saMskAreNa stanya-pAnAdau pravR^itti-darshanAt | ato dhIro dhImAn tatra tayor deha-nAshotpattyor na muhyati | Atmaiva mR^ito jAtash ceti na manyate ||13||

madhusUdanaH :

vishvanAthaH : nanu cAtma-sambandhena deho 'pi prIty-AspadaM syAt, deha-sambandhena putra-bhrAtrAdayo 'pi, tat-sambandhena tat-putrAdayo 'pi | atas teShAM nAshe shokaH syAd eveti ced ata Aha dehina iti | dehino jIvasyAsmin dehe kaumAra kaumAraM kaumAra-prAptir bhavati, tataH kaumAra-nAshAnantaraM jarA-prAptir yathA tathaiva dehAntara-prAptir iti | tatas cAtma-sambandhinAM kaumArAdInAM prIty-AspadAnAM nAshe yathA shoko na kriyate tathA dehasyApi Atma-sambandhinaH prItyAspadasya nAshe shoko na kartavyaH | yauvanasya nAshe jarA-prAptau shoko jAyate iti cet kaumArasya nAshe yauvana-prAptau harSho 'pi jAyate ity ato bhIShma-droNAdInAM jIrNa-deha-nAshe khalu navya-dehAntara-prAptau tarhi harShaH kriyatAm iti bhAvaH | yad vA, ekasminn api dehe kaumArAdInAM yathA prAptis tathaivaikasyApi dehino jIvasya nAnA-dehAnAM prAptir iti ||13||

baladevaH : nanu bhIShmAdi-dehAvacchinnAnAm AtmanAM nityatve 'pi tad-dehAnAM tad-bhogAyatanAnAM nAshe yuktaH shoka iti cet tatrAha dehino 'sminn iti | traikAlikA bahavo dehA yasya santi, tasya dehino jIvasyAsmin vartamAne dehe kramAt kaumAra-yauvana-jarAs tisro 'vasthA bhavanti | tAsAm Atma-sambandhinAM tad-bhogopayuktAnAM pUrva-pUrva-vinAshena para-para-prAptau yathA na shokas tathaiva tad-deha-vinAshe sati dehAntara-prAptir yayAti-yauvana-prApti-nyAyena harSha-hetur eveti, na tad-deha-vinAsha-hetukaH shokas tavocita iti bhAvaH | dhIro dhImAn deha-svabhAva-jIva-karma-vipAka-svarUpa-j~naH | atra dehina ity eka-vacanaM jAty-abhiprAyeNa bodhyaM pUrvatrAtma-bahutvokteH | 

atrAhuH - eka eva vishuddhAtmA tasyAvidyayAparicchinnasya tasyAM pratibimbitasya vA nAnAtmatvam | shrutish caivam Aha AkAsham ekaM hi yathA ghaTAdiShu pR^ithag bhavet, tathAtmaiko hy anekastho jalAdhAreShv ivAMshumAn iti | tad-vij~nAnena tasya vinAshe tu tan-nAnAtva-nivR^ittyA tad-aikyaM sidhyatIty eka-vacanenaitat pArtha-sArathir Aheti | tan-mandaM jaDayA tayA caitanya-rAshesh chedAsambhavAt | tair api tad-viShayatvAnaN^gIkArAc ca | vAstave cchede vikAritvAdy-ApattiH TaN^ka-chinna-pAShANavat syAt - nIrUpasya vibhoH pratibimbAsambhavAc ca | anyathAkAshAdi-gAdInAM tad-ApattiH | na ca pratIty-anyathAnupapattir evAkAshasya pratibimbe mAnaM tad-varti-graha-nakShatra-prabhA-maNDalaM tasyiavAmbhasi bhAsamAnatvena pratIteH | AkAsham ekaM hi iti shrutis tu paramAtma-viShayA tasyAkAshavat sUryavac ca bahu-vR^ittikatvaM vadatIty aviruddham | na cAtmaikyasyopadeShTA sambhavati | sa hi tattvavin na vA ? Adye 'dvitIyam AtmAnaM vijAnatas tasyopadeshyApari-sphUrtiH | antye tv aj~natvAd eva nAtma-j~nAnopadeShTR^itvam | bAdhitAnuvR^ittyAshrayaNaM tu pUrva-nirastam ||13||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.14

mAtrA-sparshAs tu kaunteya shItoShNa-sukha-duHkhadAH |
AgamApAyino 'nityAs tAMs titikShasva bhArata ||14||

shrIdharaH : nanu tAn ahaM na shocAmi, kintu tad-viyogAdi-duHkha-bhAjaM mAm eveti cet tatrAha mAtrA-sparshA iti | mIyante jAyante viShayA Abhir iti mAtrA indriya-vR^ittayaH, tAsAM sparshA viShayeShu sambaddhAH, te shItoShNAdi-pradA bhavanti | te tu AgamApAyitvAd anityA asthirAH | atas tAn titikShasva sahasva | yathA jalAtapAdi-saMsargAs tat-tat-kAla-kR^itAH svabhAvataH shItoShNAdi prayacchanti evam iShTa-saMyoga-viyogA api sukha-duHkhAni prayacchanti, teShAM cAsthiratvAt sahanaM tava dhIrasyocitaM na tu tan-nimitta-harSha-viShAda-pAravashyam ity arthaH ||14||

madhusUdanaH :

vishvanAthaH : nanu satyam eva tattvam | tad apy avivekino mama mana evAnarthakAni vR^itahiva shoka-moha-vyAptaM duHkhayatIti | tatra na kevalam ekaM mana evApi tu manaso vR^ittayo 'pi sarvAs tv agAdIndriya-rUpAH sva-viShayAn anubhAvyAnarthakAriNya ity Aha mAtrA indriya-grAhya-viShayAs teShAM sparshA anubhavAH | shItoShNety AgamApAyina iti yad eva shItala-jalAdikam uShNa-kAle sukhadam | tad eva shIta-kAle duHkhadam ato 'niyatatvAd AgamApAyitvAc ca tAn viShayAnubhavAn titikShasva sahasva | teShAM sahanam eva shAstra-vihito dharmaH | nahi mAghe mAsi jalasya duHkhatva-buddhyaiva shAstre vihitaH snAna-rUpo dharmas tyajyate | dharma eva kAle sarvAnartha-nivartako bhavati | evam eva ye putra-bhrAtrAdyotpatti-kAle dhanAdy-upArjana-kAle ca sukhadAs ta eva mR^ityu-kAle duHkhadA AgamApAyino 'nityAs tAn api titikShasva | na tu tad-anurodhena yuddha-rUpaH shAstra-vihitaH sva-dharmas tyAjyo vihita-dharmAnAcaraNaM khalu kAle mahAnarthakR^id eveti bhAvaH ||14||

baladevaH : nanu bhIShmAdayo mR^itAH kathaM bhaviShyantIti tad-duHkha-nimittaH shoko mAbhUt | tad-viccheda-duHkha-nimittas tu me mana-prabhR^itIni pradahantIti cet tatrAha mAtreti | mAtrAs tv agAdIndriya-vR^ittayaH mIyante paricchidyante viShayA abhir iti vyutpatteH | sparshAs tAbhir viShayANAm anubhavAnte khalu shItoShNa-sukha-duHkhadA bhavanti | yad eva shItalam udakaM grIShme sukhadaM tad eva hemante duHkhadam ity ato 'niyatatvAd AgamApAyitvAc cAnityAn asthirAMs tAn titikShasva sahasva | etad uktaM bhavati mAgha-snAnaM duHkha-karam api dharmatayA vidhAnAd yathA kriyate tathA bhIShmAdibhiH saha yuddhaM duHkha-karam api tathA vidhAnAt kAryam eva | tatratyo duHkhAnubhavas tv Agantuko dharma-siddhatvAt soDhavyaH | dharmAj j~nAnodayena mokSha-lAbhe tUttaratra tasya nAnuvR^ittish ca j~nAna-niShThA paripAkaM vinaiva dharma-tyAgas tv anartha-hetur iti | kaunteya bhArateti padAbhyAm ubhaya-kula-shuddhasya te dharma-bhraMsho nocita iti sUcyate ||14||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.15

yaM hi na vyathayanty ete puruShaM puruSharShabha |
sama-duHkha-sukhaM dhIraM so 'mR^itatvAya kalpate ||15||

shrIdharaH : tat-pratikAra-prayatnAd api tat-sahanam evocitaM mahA-phalatvAd ity Aha yaM hIti | ete mAtrA-sparshA yaM puruShaM na vyathayanti nAbhibhavanti | same duHkha-sukhe sa tam | sa tair avikShipyamANo dharma-j~nAna-dvArA amR^itatvAya mokShAya kalpate yogyo bhavati ||15||

madhusUdanaH :

vishvanAthaH : evaM vicAreNa tat-tat-sahanAbhyAse sati te viShayAnubhavAH kAle kila nApi duHkhayanti | yadi ca na duHkhayanti, tadAtma-muktiH sva-pratyAsannaivety Aha yam iti | amR^itatvAya mokShAya ||15||

baladevaH : dharmArtha-duHkha-sahanAbhyAsasyottaratra sukha-hetutvaM darshayann Aha yaM hIti | ete mAtrA-sparshAH priyApriya-viShayAnubhAvA yaM dhIraM dhiyam Irayati dharmeShv iti vyutpatter dharma-niShThaM puruShaM na vyathayanti sukha-duHkha-mUrcchitaM na kurvanti so 'mR^itatvAya muktaye kalpyate | na tu tAdR^isho duHkha-sukha-mUrcchita ity arthaH | uktam arthaM sphuTayan puruShaM vishinaShTi sameti | dharmAnuShThAnasya kaShTa-sAdhyatvAd duHkham anuShaN^ga-labdhaM sukhaM ca yasya samaM bhavati tAbhyAM mukha-mlAnitollAsa-rahitam ity arthaH ||15||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.16

nAsato vidyate bhAvo nAbhAvo vidyate sataH |
ubhayor api dR^iShTo 'ntas tv anayos tattva-darshibhiH ||16||

shrIdharaH : nanu tathApi shItoShNAdikam atiduHsahaM kathaM soDhavyam | atyantaM tat-sahane ca kadAcid deha-nAshaH syAd ity AshaN^kya tattva-vicArataH sarvaM soDhuM shakyam ity AshayenAha nAsato vidyata iti | asato 'nAtma-dharmatvAd avidyamAnasya shItoShNAder Atmani bhAvaH sattA na vidyate | tathA sataH sat-svabhAvasyAtmano 'bhAvo nAsho na vidyate | evam ubhayoH sad-asator anto nirNayo dR^iShTaH | kaiH ? tattva-darshibhiH vastu-yAthArthya-vedibhiH | evambhUta-vivekena sahasvety arthaH ||16||

madhusUdanaH :

vishvanAthaH : etac ca viveka-dashAn adhirUDhAn prati uktam | vastutas tu asaN^go hy ayaM puruShaH iti shruter jIvAtmanash ca sthUla-sUkShma-dehAbhyAM tad-dharmaiH shoka-mohAdibhish ca sambandho nAsty eva | tat-sambandhasya avidyA kalpitatvAd ity Aha neti | asato 'nAtma-dharmatvAd Atmani jIve avartamAnasya shoka-mohAdes tad-Ashrayasya dehasya ca bhAvaH sattA nAsti | tathA sataH satya-rUpasya jIvAtmano 'bhAvo nAsho nAsti | tasmAd ubhayor etayor asat-sator anto nirNayo 'yaM dR^iShTaH | tena bhIShmAdiShu tvad-AdiShu ca jIvAtmasu satyatvAd anashvareShu deha-daihika-viveka-shoka-mohAdayo naiva santi kathaM bhIShmAdayo naN^kShanti | kathaM vA tAMs tvaM shocasIti bhAvaH ||16||

baladevaH : tad evaM bhagavatA pArthasyAsthAnAshocitvena tat-pANDityam AkShiptam | shoka-haraM ca svopAsanam eva tac copAsopAsaka-bheda-ghaTitam ity upAsyAj jIvAMshinaH svasmAd upAsakAnAM jIvAMshAnAM tAttvikaM dvaitam upadiShTam | atha yad Atma-tattvena tu brahma-tattvaM dIpopameneha yuktaH prapashyet [ÁvetU 2.15] ity AdAv aMsha-svarUpa-j~nAnasyAMshi-svarUpa-j~nAnopayogitva-shravaNAt tad Adau saniShThAdIn sarvAn pratyavisheSheNopadeshyaM tac ca dehAtmanor vaidharmya-dhiyam antarA na syAd iti tad-vaidharmya-bodhAyArabhyate nAsata ity AdibhiH | asataH pariNAmino dehAder bhAvo 'pariNAmitvaM na vidyate | sato ' pariNAmina Atmanas tv abhAvaH pariNAmitvaM na vidyate | dehAtmAnau pariNAmApariNAma-svabhAvau bhavataH | evam ubhayor asat-sac-chabditayor dehAtmanor anto nirNayas tattva-darshibhis tad-ubhaya-svabhAva-vedibhiH puruShair dR^iShTo 'nubhUtaH | atrAsac-chabdena vinashvaraM dehAdi jaDaM sac-chabdena tv avinashvaram Atma-caitanyam ucyate | evam eva shrI-viShNu-purANe 'pi nirNItaM dR^iShTaM jyotIMShi viShNur bhuvanAni viShNur [ViP 2.12.38] ity upakramya yad asti yan nAsti ca vipra-varya [?] ity asti | nAsti-shabda-vAcyayosh cetana-jaDayos tathAtvaM vastv asti kiM kutradcid ity Adibhir nirUpitaH | tatra nAsti shabda-vAcyaM jaDam | asti-shabdavAtyaM tu caitanyam iti svayam eva vivR^itam | yat tu sat-kArya-vAda-sthApanAyai tat-padyam ity Ahus tan-niravadhAnaM dehAtma-svabhAvAnabhij~nAna-mohitaM prati tan-moha-vinivR^ittaye tat-svabhAvAbhij~nApanasya prakR^itatvAt ||16||

BhG 2.17

avinAshi tu tad viddhi yena sarvam idaM tatam |
vinAsham avyayasyAsya na kashcit kartum arhati ||17||

shrIdharaH : atra sat-svabhAvam avinAshi vastu sAmAnyenoktaM tataM tat-sAkShitvena vyAptaM taM tu Atma-svarUpam avinAshi vinAsha-shUnyaM viddhi jAnIhi | tatra hetum Aha vinAsham iti ||17||

madhusUdanaH :

vishvanAthaH : nAbhAvo vidyate sataH ity asyArthaM spaShTayati avinAshIti | taM jIvAtma-svarUpaM yena sarvam idaM sharIraM tataM vyAptam | nanu sharIra-mAtra-vyApi-caitanyatve jIvAtmano madhyama-parimANatvena anityatva-prasaktiH ? maivam | sUkShmANAm apy ahaM jIvaH iti bhagavad-ukteH | eShoNur AtmA cetasA veditavyo yasmin prANaH pa¤cadhA saMvivesha iti, 

bAlAgra-shata-bhAgasya shatadhA kalpitasya ca |
bhAgo jIvaH sa vij~neyaH [ÁvetU 5.9] iti,

ArAgra-mAtro hy aparo 'pi dR^iShTaH iti shrutibhyash ca tasya paramANu-parimANatvam eva | tad api sampUrNa-deha-vyApi-shaktimattvaM jatu-jaTitasya mahA-maNer mahauShadhi-khaNDasya vA shirasy urasi vA dhR^itasya sampUrNa-deha-puShTi-karaNa-shaktimattvam iva nAsama¤jasam | svarga-naraka-nAnA-yoniShu gamanaM ca tasyopAdhi-pAravashyAd eva | tad uktaM prANam adhikR^itya dattAtrayeNa yena saMsarate pumAn iti | ataevAsya sarva-gatatvam apy agrima-shloke vakShyamANaM nAsama¤jasam | ataevAvyayasya nityasya nityo nityAnAM cetanash cetanAnAm eko bahUnAM yo vidadhAti kAmAn [ÁvetU 6.13] iti shruteH | 

yad vA, nanu deho jIvAtmA paramAtmety etad vastu-trikaM manuShya-tiryag-AdiShu sarvatra dR^ishyate, tatrAdyayor deha-jIvayos tattvaM nAsato vidyate bhAvaH ity anenoktam | tR^itIyasya paramAtma-vastunaH kiM tattvam ity ata Aha avinAshi tv iti | tu bhinnopakrame | paramAtmano mAyA-jIvAbhyAM svarUpataH pArthakyAd idaM jagat ||17||

baladevaH : uktaM jIvAtma-dehayoH svabhAvaM vishadayaty avinAshIti dvAbhyAm | taj jIvAtma-tattvam avinAshi nityaM viddhi | yena sarvam idaM sharIraM tataM dharma-bhUtena j~nAnena vyAptam asti | asyAvyayasya parmANutvena ca vinAshAnarhasya vinAshaM na kashcit sthUlo 'rthaH kartum arhati prANasyeva dehaH | iha jIvAtmano deha-parimitatvaM na pratyetavyam | eSho 'Nur AtmA cetasA veditavyo yasmin prANaH pa¤cadhA saMvivesha [MuNDU 3.1.9] ity AdiShu tasya paramANutva-shravaNAt | tAdR^ishasya nikhila-deha-vyAptis tu dharma-bhUta-j~nAnenaiva syAt | evam Aha bhagavAn sUtrakAraH - guNAd vAlokavad [Vs. 2.3.26] iti | ihApi svayaM vakShyati yathA prakAshayaty ekaH [GItA 13.33] ity AdinA ||17||
