BhG 2.18

antavanta ime dehA nityasyoktAH sharIriNaH |
anAshino 'prameyasya tasmAd yudhyasva bhArata ||18||

shrIdharaH : AgamApAya-dharmakaM sandarshyati antavanta iti | anto vinAsho vidyate yeShAM te antavantaH | nityasya sarvadaika-rUpasya sharIriNaH sharIravataH | ataevAnAshino vinAsha-rahitasya aprameyasyaparicchinnasyAtmana ime sukha-duHkhAdi-dharmaka-dehA uktAs tattva-darshibhiH | yasmAd evam Atmano na vinAshaH, na ca sukha-duHkhAdi-sambandhaH, tasmAn mohajaM shoktaM tyaktvA yudhyasva | svadharmaM mA tyakShIr ity arthaH ||18||

madhusUdanaH : nanu sphuraNa-rUpasya sataH katham avinAshitvaM tasya deha-dharmatvAd dehasya cAnukShaNa-vinAshAd iti bhUta-caitanya-vAdinas tAn nirAkurvann Asato vidyate bhAva ity etad vivR^iNoti antavanta iti | antavanto vinAshina ime 'parokShA dehA upacitApacita-rUpatvAc charIrANi | bahu-vacanAt sthUla-sUkShma-kAraNa-rUpA virAT-sUtrAvyAkR^itAkhyAH samaShTi-vyaShTy-AtmanaH sarve nityasyAvinAshina eva sharIriNa AdhyAsika-sambandhena sharIravataekasyAtmanaH sva-prakAsha-sphuraNa-rUpasya sambandhino dR^ishyatvena bhogyatvena coktAH shrutibhir brahma-vAdibhish ca | tathA ca taittirIyake 'nnamayAdyAnandamayAnantAn pa¤ca koshAn kalpayitvA tad-adhiShThAnam akalpitaM brahma pucchaM pratiShThA [TaittU 2.5] iti darshitam | tatra pa¤cIkR^ita-pa¤ca-mahAbhUta-tat-kAryAtmako virAN-mUrta-rAshir anna-maya-koshaH sthUla-samaShTiH | tat-kAraNI-bhUto 'pa¤cIkR^ita-pa¤ca-mahA-bhUta-tat-kAryAtmako hiraNyagarbhaH sUtram amUrta-rAshiH sUkShma-samaShTiH trayaM vA idaM nAma rUpaM karma [BAU 1.6.1] iti bR^ihad-AraNyakokta-try-annAtmakaH sarva-karmAtmakatvena kriyA-shakti-mAtram AdAya prANa-maya-kosha uktaH | nAmAtmakatvena j~nAna-shakti-mAtram AdAyamanomaya-kosha uktaH | rUpAtmakatvena tad-ubhayAshrayatayA kartR^itvam AdAya vij~nAna-maya-kosha uktaH  | tataH prANa-maya-mano-maya-vij~nAna-mayAtmaika eva hiraNyagarbhAkhyo liN^ga-sharIra-koshaH | tat-kAraNIbhUtas tu mAyopahita-caitanyAtmA sarva-saMskAra-sheSho 'vyAkR^itAkhya Ananda-maya-koshaH | te ca sarva ekasyaivAtmanaH sharIrANIty uktam | tasyaiSha eva shArIra AtmA yaH pUrvasya [TaittU 2.3.4] iti | tasya prANa-mayasyaiSha eva sharIre bhavaH shArIra AtmA yaH satya-j~nAnAdi-lakShaNo guhA-nihitatvenoktaH pUrvasyAnna-mayasya | evaM prANa-maya-mano-maya-vij~nAna-mayAnanda-mayeShu yojyam |

athaveme sarve dehAs trailokya-varti-sarva-prANi-sambandhina ekasyaivAtmana uktA iti yojanA | tathA ca shrutiH -

eko devaH sarva-bhUteShu gUDhaH
sarva-vyApI sarva-bhUtAntarAtmA |
karmAdhyakShaH sarva-bhUtAdhivAsaH
sAkShI ceto kevalo nirguNash ca || [ÁvetU 6.11]

iti sarva-sharIra-sambandhinam ekam AtmAnaM nityaM vibhuM darshayati |

nanu nityatvaM yAvat-kAla-sthAyitvaM tathA cAvidyAdivat kAlena saha nAshe 'pi tad-upapannam ity ata Aha anAshina iti | deshataH kAlato vastutash caparicchinasyAvidyAdeH kalpitatvenAnityatve 'pi yAvat-kAla-sthAyi-svarUpam aupacArikaM nityatvaM vyavahriyate yAvad-vikAraM tu vibhAgo lokavat [Vs 2.3.7] iti nyAyAt | Atmanas tu pariccheda-traya-shUnyasyAkalpitasya vinAsha-hetv-abhAvAn mukhyam eva kUTastha-nityatvaM na tu pariNAmi-nityatvaM yAvat-kAla-sthAyitvaM cety abhiprAyaH |

nanv etAdR^ishe dehini kiMcit pramANam avashyaM vAcyam anyathA niShpramANasya tasyAlIkatvApatteH shAstrArambha-vaiyarthyApattesh ca | tathA ca vastu-paricchedo duShpariharaH shAstra-yonitvAt [Vs 1.1.3] iti nyAyAc ca | ata Aha aprameyasyeti | ekadhaivAnudraShTavyam etad apramayaM dhruvam [BAU 4.7.2] apramayam aprameyam |

na tatra sUryo bhAti na candra-tArakaM
nemA vidyuto bhAnti kuto 'yam agniH  | [KaThU 5.15]

tam eva bhAntam anubhAti sarvaM
tasya bhAsA sarvam idaM vibhAti [MuNDU 2.2.10]

iti ca shruteH sva-prakAsha-caitanya-rUpa evAtmAtas tasya sarva-bhAsakasya svabhAnArthaM na svabhAsyApekShA, kintu kalpitAj~nAna-tat-kArya-nivR^itty-arthaM kalpita-vR^itti-visheShApekShA | kalpitasyaiva kalpita-virodhitvAt | yakShAnurUpo baliH iti nyAyAt | tathA ca sarva-kalpita-nivartaka-vR^itti-visheShotpatty-arthaM shAstrArambhaH, tasya tattvam asy Adi-vAkya-mAtrAdhInatvAt | svataH sarvadAbhAsamAnatvAt sarva-kalpanAdhiShThAnatvAd dR^ishyamAtra-bhAsakatvAc ca na tasya tucchatvApattiH | tathA caikam evAdvitIyaM satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahmety Adi-shAstram eva sva-prameyAnurodhena svasyApi kalpitatvam ApAdayati anyathA sva-prAmANyAnupapatteH |

kalpitasya cAkalpita-paricchedakatvaM nAstIti prAk-pratipAditam | AtmanaH svaprakAshatvaM ca yuktito 'pi bhagavat-pUjyapAdair upapAditam | tathA hi - yatra jij~nAsoH saMshaya-viparyaya-vyatireka-pramANAnAm anyatamam api nAsti tatra tad-virodhi j~nAnam iti sarvatra dR^iShTam | anyathA tritayAnyatamApatteH | Atmani cAhaM vA nAhaM veti na kasyacit saMshayaH | nApi nAham iti viparyayo vyatirekaH pramA veti tat-svarUpa-pramA sarvadAstIti vAcyaM tasya sarva-saMshaya-viparyaya-dharmitvAt | dharmyashe sarvam abhrAntaM prakAre tu viparyayaH iti nyAyAt | ata evoktam -

pramANam apramANaM ca pramAbhAsas tathaiva ca |
kurvanty eva pramAM yatra tad-asambhAvanA kutaH || [BR^ihad-vAmanaP 1.4.874]

pramAbhAsaH saMshayaH | sva-prakAshe sad-rUpe dharmiNi pramANApramANayor visheSho nAstIty arthaH | Atmano 'bhAsamAnatve ca ghaTa-j~nAnaM mayi jAtaM na vety Adi-saMshayaH syAt |  na cAntara-padArthe viShayasyaiva saMshayAdi-pratibandhakatva-svabhAvaH | bAhya-padArthe k ptena virodhi-j~nAnenaiva saMshayAdi-pratibandha-saMbhava Antara-padArthe svabhAva-bheda-kalpanAyA anaucityAt | anyathA sarva-viplavApatteH | Atma-mano-yoga-mAtraM cAtma-sAkShAtkAre hetuH | yasya ca j~nAna-mAtre hetutvAd ghaTAdi-bhAne 'py Atma-bhAnaM samUhAlambana-nyAyena tArkikANAM pravareNApi durnivAraM | na ca cAkShuShatva-mAna-sattvAdi-saN^karaH | laukikatvAlaukikatvavad aMsha-bhedenopapatteH | saN^karasyAdoShatvAc cAkShuShatvAder jAtitvAnabhyupagamAd vA | vyavasAyamAtra evAtmabhAna-sAmagryA vidyamAnatvAd anuvyavasAyo 'py apAstaH | na ca vyavasAya-bhAnArthaM sa tasya dIpavat sva-vyavahAre sajAtIyAnapekShatvAt | na hi ghaTa-taj-j~nAnayor iva vyavasAyAnuvyavasAyayor api viShayatva-viShayitva-vyavasthApakaM vaijAtyam asti vyakti-bhedAtirikta-vaidharmyAnabhyupagamAt | viShayatvAvacchedaka-rUpeNaiva viShayitvAbhyupagame ghaTa-taj-j~nAnayor api tad-bhAvApattir avisheShAt |

nanu yathA ghaTa-vyavahArArthaM ghaTa-j~nAnam abhyupeyate tathA ghaTa-j~nAna-vyavahArArthaM ghaTa-j~nAna-viShayaM j~nAnam abhyupeyaM vyavahArAsya vyavahartavya-j~nAna-sAdhyatvAd iti cet | kAnupapattir udbhAvitA devAnAM-priyeNa sva-prakAsha-vAdinaH | nahi vyavahartavya-bhinnatvam api j~nAna-visheShaNaM vyavahAra-hetutAvacchedakaM gauravAt | tathA ceshvara-j~nAnavadyogi-j~nAnavat prameyam iti j~nAnavac ca svenaiva sva-vyavahAropapattau na j~nAnAntara-kalpanAvakAshaH | anuvyavasAyasyApi ghaTa-j~nAna-vyavahAra-hetutvaM kiM ghaTa-j~nAna-j~nAnatvena kiM vA ghaTa-j~nAnatvenaiveti vivecanIyam | ubhayasyApi tatra sattvAt | tatra ghaTa-vyavahAre ghaTa-j~nAnatvenaiva hetutAyAH k ptatvAt tenaiva rUpeNa ghata-j~nAna-vyavahAre,pi hetutopapattau na ghaTa-j~nAna-j~nAnatvaM hetutAvacchedakaM gauravAn mAnAbhAvAc ca | tathA ca nAnuvyavasAya-siddhir ekasyaiva vyavasAyasya vayvasAtari vyavaseye vyavasAye ca vyavahAra-janakatvopapatter iti tripuTI-pratyakSha-vAdinaH prAbhAkarAH |

aupaniShadAstu manyante sva-prakAsha-j~nAna-rUpa evAtmA na svaprakAsha-j~nAnAshrayaH kartR^i-karma-virodhena tad-bhAnAnupapatteH | j~nAna-bhinnatve ghaTAdivaj-jaDatvena kalpitatvApattesh ca | svaprakAsha-j~nAna-mAtra-svarUpo 'py AtmAvidyopahitaH san sAkShIty ucyate | vR^itti-mad-antaHkaraNopahitaH pramAtety ucyate | tasya cakShur-AdIni karaNAni | sa cakShur-Adi-dvArAntaH-karaNa-pariNAmena ghaTAdIn vyApya tad-AkAro bhavati | tato ghaTAvacchinna-caitanyaM pramAtra-bhedAt svAj~nAnaM nAshayad aparokShaM bhavati | ghaTaM ca svAvacchedakaM sva-tAdAtmyAdhyAsAd bhAsayati | antaH-karaNa-pariNAmash ca vR^ittyAkhyo 'tisvacchaH svAvacchinnenaiva caitanyena bhAsyata ity antaH-karaNa-tad-vR^itti-ghaTAnAm aparokShatA | tad etad AkAra-trayam ahaM jAnAmi ghaTam iti | bhAsaka-caitanyasyaika-rUpatve 'pi ghaTaM prati vR^itty-apekShatvAt pramAtR^itA | antaHkaraNa-tad-vR^ittIH prati tu vR^itty-anapekShatvAt sAkShiteti vivekaH | advaita-siddhau siddhAnta-bindau ca vistaraH | 

yasmAd evaM prAg-ukta-nyAyena ntiyo vibhur asaMsArI sarvadaika-rUpash cAtmA tasmAt tan-nAsha-shaN^kayA svadharme yuddhe prAk-pravR^ittasya tava tasmAd uparatir na yukteti yuddhAbhyanuj~nayA bhagavAn Aha - tasmAd yudhyasva bhArateti | arjunasya svadharme yuddhe pravR^ittasya tata uparati-kAraNaM shoka-mohau | tau ca vicAra-janitena vij~nAnena vAdhitAv ity apavAdApavAda utsargasya sthitir iti nyAyena yudhyasvety anuvAdo na vidhiH | yathA kartR^i-karmaNoH kR^iti [PAN 2.3.65] ity utsargaH | ubhaya-prAptau karmaNi [PAN 2.3.66] ity apavAdaH | akAkArayoH strI-pratyayayoH prayoge neti vaktavyam iti tad-apavAdaH | tathA ca mumukShor brahmaNor jij~nAsety atrApavAdApavAde punar utsarga-sthiteH kartR^i-karmaNoH kR^itIty anenaiva ShaShThI | tathA ca karmaNi ceti niShedhA-prasArAd brahma-jij~nAseti karma-ShaShThI-samAsaH siddho bhavati | kashcit tv etasmAd eva vidher mokShe j~nAna-karmaNoH samuccaya iti pralapati | tac ca yudhyasvety ato mokShasya j~nAna-karma-samuccaya-sAdhyatvApratIteH | vistareNa caitad agre bhagavad-gItA-vacana-virodhenaiva nirAkariShyAmaH ||18||

vishvanAthaH : nAsato vidyate bhAvaH ity asyArthaM spaShTayati antavanta iti | sharIriNo jIvasyAprameyasyAti-sUkShmatvAd durj~neyasya | tasmAd yudhyasva iti shAstra-vihitasya svadharmasya tyAgo 'nucita iti bhAvaH ||18||

baladevaH : antavanto vinAshi-svabhAvAH, sharIriNo jIvAtmanaH | aprameyasyAtisUkShmatvAd vij~nAna-vij~nAtR^i-svarUpatvAc ca pramAtum ashakyasyety arthaH | tathA cedR^isha-svabhAvatvAj jIva-tad-dehau na shoka-sthAnam iti jIvAtmano deho dharmAnuShTAnuShThAna-dvArA tasya bhogAya mokShAya ca pareshena sR^ijyate | sa ca sa ca dharmeNa bhavet tasmAd yudhyasva bhArata ||18||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.19

ya enaM vetti hantAraM yash cainaM manyate hatam |
ubhau tau na vijAnIto nAyaM hanti na hanyate ||19||

shrIdharaH : tad evaM bhIShmAdi-mR^ityu-nimittaH shoko nivAritaH, yac cAtmano hantR^itva-nimittaM duHkham uktam etAn na hantum icchAmi ity AdinA, tad api tavad eva nirnimittam ity Aha ya enam iti | enam AtmAnam | Atmano hanana-kriyAyAH karmatvaM kartR^itvam api nAstIty arthaH | tatra hetur nAyam iti ||19||

madhusUdanaH : nanv evam ashocyAn anvashocacas tvam ity AdinA bhIShmAdi-bandhu-viccheda-nibandhane shoke 'panIte 'pi tad-vadha-kartR^itva-nibandhanasya pApasya nAsti pratIkAraH | nahi yatra shoko nAsti tatra pApaM nAstIti niyamaH | dveShya-brAhmaNa-vadhe pApAbhAva-prasaN^gAt | ato 'haM kartA tvaM preraka iti dvayor api hiMsA-nimitta-pAtakApatter ayuktam idaM vacanaM tasmAd yudhyasva bhAratety AshaN^kya kAThaka-paThitaya rcA pariharati bhagavAn ya enam iti | 

enaM prakR^itaM dehinam adR^ishyatvAdi-guNakaM yo hantAraM hanana-kriyAyAH kartAraM vetti aham asya hanteti vijAnAti | yash cAnya enaM manyate hataM hanana-kriyAyAH karma-bhUtaM deha-hananena hato 'ham iti vijAnAti | tAv ubhau dehAbhimAnitvAd enam avikAriNam akAraka-svabhAvam AtmAnaM na vijAnIto na vivekena jAnItaH shAstrAt | kasmAt yasmAn nAyaM hanti na hanyate kartA karma ca na bahvatIty arthaH | 

atra ya enaM vetti hantAraM hataM cety etAvati vaktavye padAnAm AvR^ittir vAkyAlaN^kArArthA | athavA ya enaM vetti hantAraM tArkikAdir AtmanaH kartR^itvAbhyupagamAt | tathA yash cainaM manyate hataM cArvAkAdir Atmano vinAshitvAbhyupagamAt | tAv ubhau na vijAnIta iti yojyam | vAdi-bheda-khyApanAya pR^ithag upanyAsaH | atishUrAtikAtara-viShayatayA vA pR^ithag-upadeshaH | hantA cen manyate hantuM hatash cen manyate hatam [KaThU 1.2.19] iti pUrvArdhe shrautaH pAThaH ||19||

vishvanAthaH : bho vayasya arjuna ! tvam AtmA | na hanteH kartA, nApi hanteH karma ity Aha ya iti | enaM jIvAtmAnaM hantAraM vetti bhIShmAdIn arjuno hantIti yo vettIty arthaH, hatam iti bhIShmAdibhir arjuno hanyate iti yo vetti, tAv ubhAv apy aj~nAninau | ato 'rjuno 'yaM guru-janaM hantIty aj~nAni-loka-gItAd duryashaH kA te bhItir iti bhAvaH ||19||

baladevaH : uktam avinAshitvaM draDhayati | enam ukta-svabhAvam AtmAnaM jIvaM yo hantAraM khaDgAdinA hiMsakaM vetti yash cainaM tena hataM hiMsitaM manyate tAv ubhau tat-svarUpaM na vijAnItaH | atisUkShmasya caitanyasya tasya chedAdy-asambhavAn nAyam AtmA hanti na hanyate | hanteH kartA karma ca bhavatIty arthaH | hanter deha-viyogArthatvAn na tenAtmanAM nAsho mantavyaH | shrutish caivam Aha - hantA cen manyate hantuM hatash cen manyate hatam [KaThU 1.2.19] ity AdinA | etena mA hiMsyAt sarva-bhUtAni ity Adi-vAkyaM deha-viyoga-paraM vyAkhyAtam | na cAtrAtmanaH kartR^itvaM prasiddham iti vAcyam | deha-viyojane tat tasya sattvAt ||19||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.20

na jAyate mriyate vA kadAcin
nAyaM bhUtvA bhavitA vA na bhUyaH |
ajo nityaH shAshvato 'yaM purANo
na hanyate hanyamAne sharIre ||20||

shrIdharaH : na hanyata ity etad eva ShaD-bhAva-vikAra-shUnyatvena draDhayati neti | na jAyata ity Adi | na jAyata iti janma-pratiShedhaH | na mriyata iti vinAsha-pratiShedhaH | vA-shabdau cArthe | na cAyaM bhUtvA utpadya bhavitA bhavati astitvaM bhajate, kintu prAg eva svataH sad-rUpa iti janmAntarAstitva-lakShaNa-dvitIya-vikAra-pratiShedhaH | tatra hetuH yasmAd ajaH | yo hi na jAyate sa hi janmAntaram astitvaM bhajate, na tu yaH svayam evAsti sa bhUyo 'pi anyad astitvaM bhajate ity arthaH | nityaH sarvdaika-rUpa iti vR^iddhi-pratiShedhaH | shAshvataH shashvad-bhava iti apakShaya-pratiShedhaH | purANa iti vipariNAma-pratiShedhaH | purApi nava eva na tu pariNAmataH rUpAntaraM prApya navo bhavatIty arthaH | 

yad vA na bhavitety asyAnuShaN^gaM kR^itvA bhUyo 'dhikaM yathA bhaviteti tathA na bhavatIti vR^iddhi-pratiShedhaH | ajo nitya iti cobhaya-vR^iddhy-Ady-abhAve hetur iti na paunaruktyam | tad evaM jAyate asti vardhate vipariNamate apakShIyate nashyaty evaM yAskAdibhir veda-vAdibhir uktAH ShaD-bhAva-vikArA nirastAH | yad artham ete vikArA nirastAs taM prastutaM vinAshAbhAvam upasaMharati na hanyate hanyamAne sharIra iti ||20||

madhusUdanaH : kasmAd ayam AtmA hanana-kriyAyAH kartA karma ca na bhavati ? avikriyatvAd ity Aha dvitIyena mantreNa | jAyate 'sti vardhate vipariNamate 'pakShIyate vinashyatIti ShaD-bhAva-vikArA iti vArShyAyaNiH iti nairuktAH | tatrAdy-antayor niShedhaH kriyate na jAyate mriyate veti | vA-shabdaH samuccayArthaH | na jAyate na mriyate cety arthaH | kasmAd ayam AtmA notpadyate ? yasmAd ayam AtmA kadAcit kasminn api kAle na bhUtvAbhUtvA prAg bhUyaH punar api bhavitA na | yo hy abhUtvA bhavati sa utpatti-lakShaNAM vikriyAm anubhavati | ayaM tu prAg api sattvAdyato notpadyate 'to 'jaH | tathAyam AtmA bhUtvA prAk kadAcid bhUyaH punar na bhavitA | na vA-shabdAd vAkya-vipari-vR^ittiH | yo hi prAg-bhUtvottara-kAle na bhavati sa mR^it-lakShaNAM vikriyAm anubhavati | ayaM tUttara-kAle 'pi sattvAdyato na miryate 'to nityo vinAshAyogya ity arthaH | atra na bhUtvety atra samAsAbhAve 'pi nAnupapattir nAnuyojeShv ativat | bhagavatA pANininA mahA-vibhAShAdhikAre na¤-samAsa-pAThAt | yat tu kAtyAyanenoktaM samAsa-nityatAbhiprAyeNa vA-vacanAnarthakyaM tu svabhAva-siddhatvAt iti tad-bhagavat-pANiini-vacana-virodhAd anAdeyam | tad uktam AcArya-shavara-svAminA - asad-vAdI hi kAtyAyanaH iti | 

atra na jAyate mriyate veti pratij~nA | kadAcin nAyaM bhUtvA bhavitA vA na bhUya iti tad-upapAdanam | ajo nitya iti tad-upasaMhAra iti vibhAgaH | Adyantayor vikArayor niShedhena madhyavarti-vikArANAM tad-vyApyAnAM niShedhe jAte 'pi gamanAdi-vikArANAm anuktAnAm apy upalakShaNAyApakShayash ca vR^iddhish ca sva-shabdenaiva nirAkriyete | tatra kUTastha-nityatvAd Atmano nirguNatvAc ca na svarUpato guNato vApakShayaH sambhavatIty uktaM shAshvata iti | shashvat sarvadA bhavati nApakShIyate nApacIyata ity arthaH | yadi nApakShIyate tarhi vardhatAm iti nety Aha purANa iti | purApi nava eka-rUpo na tv adhunA nUtanAM kA¤cid avasthAm anubhavati | yo hi nUtanAM kA¤cid upacayAvasthAm anubhavati sa vardhata ity ucyate loke | ayaM tu sarvadaika-rUpatvAn nApacIyate nopacIyate cety arthaH | astitva-vipariNAmau tu janma-vinAshAntarbhUtatvAt pR^ithaÇ na niShiddhau | yasmAd evaM sarva-vikAra-shUnya AtmA tasmAc charIre hanyamAne tat-sambaddho 'pi kenApy upAyena na hanyate na hantuM shakyata ity upasaMhAraH ||20||

vishvanAthaH : jIvAtmano nityatvaM spaShTatayA sAdhayati na jAyate miryate iti janma-maraNayor vartamAnatva-niShedhaH | nAyaM bhUtvA bhavitA iti tayor bhUtatva-bhaviShyatva-niShedhaH | ataeva aja iti kAla-traye 'pi ajasya janmAbhAvAn nAsya prAg-abhAvaH | shAshvataH shashvat sarva-kAla eva vartata iti nAsya kAla-traye 'pi dhvaMsaH | ataevAyaM nityaH | tarhi bahu-kAla-sthAyitvAj jarA-grasto 'yam iti cen na | purANaH purApi navaH prAcIno 'py ayaM navIna iveti ShaD-bhAva-vikArAbhAvAd iti bhAvaH | nanu sharIrasya maraNAd aupacArikaM tu maraNam asyAstu ? tatrAha neti | sharIreNa saha sambaddhAbhAvAt na upacAraH ||20|| 

baladevaH : atha jAyate asti vardhate viparaNamate apakShIyate vinashyati iti yAskAdy-ukta-ShaD-bhAva-vikAra-rAhityena prAg-ukta-nityatvaM draDhayati na jAyate iti | cArthe vA-shabdau | ayam AtmA jIvaH kadAcid api kAle na jAyate na mriyate ceti janma-vinAshayoH pratiShedhaH | na cAyam AtmA bhUtvotpadya bhavitA bhaviShyatIti janmAntarasyAstitvasya pratiShedhaH | na bhUya iti ayam AtmA bhUyo 'dhikaM yathA syAt tathA na bhavatIti buddheH pratiShedhaH | kuto bhUyo na bhavatIty atra hetur ajo nitya iti | utpatti-vinAsha-yogI khalu vR^ikShAdir utpadya vR^iddhiM gacchan naShTaH | Atmanas tu tad-ubhayAbhAvAt na vR^iddhir ity arthaH | shAshvata ity apakShayasya pratiShedhaH | shashvat sarvadA bhavati nApakShIyate nApakShayaM bhajatIty arthaH | purANa iti vipariNAmasya pratiShedhaH | purANaM purApi navo na tu kiMcin nUtanaM rUpAntaram adhunA na labdha ity arthaH | tad evaM ShaD-bhAva-vikAra-shUnyatvAd AtmA nityaH | yasmAd IdR^ishas tasmAc charIre hanyamAne 'pi sa na hanyate | tathA cArjuno 'yaM guru-hantety avij~noktyA duShkIrter abibhyatA tvayA shAstrIyaM dharma-yuddhaM vidheyam ||20||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.21

vedAvinAshinaM nityaM ya enam ajam avyayam |
kathaM sa puruShaH pArtha kaM ghAtayati hanti kam ||21||

shrIdharaH : ataeva hantR^itvAbhAvo 'pi pUrvoktaH prasiddha ity Aha vedAvinAshinam ity Adi | nityaM vR^iddhi-shUnyam | avyayam apakShaya-shUnyam | ajam avinAshinaM ca | yo veda sa puruShaH kaM hanti | kathaM vA hanti ? evaM-bhUtasya vadhe sAdhanAbhAvAt | tathA svayaM prayojako bhUtvAnyena kaM ghAtayati ? kathaM vA ghAtayati ? na ki¤cid api | na katha¤cid api ity arthaH | anena mayy api prayojakatvAd doSha-dR^iShTiM mA kArShIr ity uktaM bhavati ||21||

madhusUdanaH : nAyaM hanti na hanyata iti pratij~nAya na hanyata ity upapAditam idAnIM na hantIty upapAdayann upasaMharati | na vinaShTuM shIlaM yasya tam avinAshinam antya-vikAra-rahitam | tatra hetuH - avyayaM na vidyate vyayo 'vayavApacayo guNApacayo vA yasya tam avyayam | avayavApacayena guNApacayena vA vinAsha-darshanAt tad-ubhaya-rahitasya na vinAshaH sambhavatIty arthaH |

nanu janyatvena vinAshitvam anumAsyAmahe nety Aha - ajam iti | na jAyate ity ajam Adya-vikAra-rahitam | tatra hetuH - nityaM sarvadA vidyAmAnaM, prAg-avidyamAnasya hi janma dR^iShTaM na tu sarvatA sata ity abhiprAyaH | 

athavAvinAshinam abAdhyaM satyam iti yAvat | nityaM sarva-vyApakam | tatra hetuH - ajam avyayaM | janma-vinAsha-shUnyaM jAyamAnasya vinashyatash ca sarva-vyApakatva-satyatvayor ayogAt | 

evaM sarva-vikriyA-shUnyaM prakR^itam enaM dehinaM svam AtmAnaM yo veda vijAnAti shAstrAcAryopadeshAbhyAM sAkShAtkaroti ahaM sarva-vikriyA-shUnyaH sarva-bhAsakaH sarva-dvaita-rahitaH paramAnanda-bodha-rUpa iti sa evaM vidvAn puruShaH pUrNa-rUpaH kaM hanti ? kathaM hanti ? kiM-shabda AkShepe | na kam api hanti na katham api hantIty arthaH | tathA kaM ghAtayati kathaM ghAtayati kam api na ghAtayati katham api na ghAtayatIty arthaH | nahi sarva-vikAra-shUnyasyAkartur hanana-kriyAyAM kartR^itvaM sambhavati | tathA ca shrutiH -

AtmAnaM ced vijAnIyAd ayam asmIti pUruShaH |
kim icchan kasya kAmAya sharIram anusaJNjvaret || [BAU 4.4.12] 

iti shuddham AtmAnaM viduShas tad-aj~nAna-nibandhanAdhyAsa-nivR^ittau tan-mUla-rAga-dveShAdy-abhAvAt-kartR^itva-bhoktR^itvAdy-abhAvaM darshayati |

ayam atrAbhiprAyo bhagavataH | vastu-gatyA ko 'pi nakaroti na kArayati ca kiMcit sarva-vikriyA-shUnya-svabhAvatvAt paraM tu svapna ivAvidyayA kartR^itvAdikam Atmany abhimanyate mUDhaH | tad uktam ubhau tau na vijAnItaH [GItA 2.19] iti | shrutish ca - dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva [BAU 4.3.7] ity AdiH | ataeva sarvANi shAstrANy avidvad-adhikArikANi | vidvAMs tu samUlAdhyAsa-bAdhAn nAtmani kartR^itvAdikam abhimanyate sthANu-svarUpaM vidvAn iva coratvam | ato vikriyA-rahitatvAd advitIyatvAc ca vidvAn na karoti kArayati cety ucyate | tathA ca shrutiH -- vidvAn na bibheti kutashcana [TaittU 2.9.1] iti | arjuno hi svasmin kartR^itvaM bhagavati ca kArayitR^itvam adhyasya hiMsA-nimittaM doSham ubhayatrApy AshashaN^ke | bhagavAn api viditAbhiprAyo hanti ghAtayatIti tad-ubhayam AcikShepa | Atmani kartR^itvaM mayi ca kArayitR^itvam Aropya pratyavAya-shaN^kAM mA kArShIr ity abhiprAyaH |

avikriyatva-pradarshanenAtmanaH kartR^itva-pratiShedhAt sarva-karmAkShepe bhagavad-abhiprete hantir upalakShaNArthaH puraH-sphUrtikatvAt | pratiShedha-hetos tulyatvAt karmAntarAbhyanuj~nAnupapatteH | tathA ca vakShyati tasya kAryaM na vidyata [GItA 3.17] iti | ato 'tra hanana-mAtrAkShepeNa karmAntaraM bhagavatAbhyanuj~nAyata iti mUDha-jana-jalpitam apAstam | tasmAd yudhyasvety atra hananasya bhagavatAbhyanuj~nAnAd vAstava-kartR^itvAdy-abhAvasya karma-mAtre samatvAd iti dik ||21||

vishvanAthaH : ata evambhUta-j~nAne sati tvaM yudhyamAno 'pi ahaM yuddhe prerayann api doSha-bhAjau naiva bhavAva ity Aha vedeti | nityam iti kriyA-visheShaNam | avinAshinam iti, ajam iti, avyayam ity etair vinAsha-janyA apekShayA niShiddhAH | sa puruSho mal-lakShaNaH kaM ghAtayati, kathaM vA ghAtayati, sa puruShas tval-lakShaNaH kaM hanti ? kathaM vA hanti ? ||21||

baladevaH : evaM tattva-j~nAnavAn yo dharma-buddhyA yuddhe pravartate yash ca pravartayati, tasya tasya ca ko 'pi na doSha-gandha ity Aha vedeti | enaM prakR^itam AtmAnam avinAshinam ajam avyayam apakShaya-shUnyaM ca yo veda shAstra-yuktibhyAM jAnAti, sa puruSho yuddhe pravR^itto 'pi kaM hanti kathaM vA hanti ? tatra pravartayann api kaM ghAtayati kathaM vA ghAtayati ? kim AkShepe - na kam api na katham apIty arthaH | ntiyam iti vedana-kriyA-visheShaNam ||21|| 

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.22

vAsAMsi jIrNAni yathA vihAya
navAni gR^ihNAti naro 'parANi |
tathA sharIrANi vihAya jIrNAni
anyAni saMyAti navAni dehI ||22||

shrIdharaH : nanv Atmano 'vinAshe 'pi tadIya-sharIra-nAshaM paryAlocya shocAmIiti cet ? tatrAha vAsAMsIti | karmaNi bandhanAnAM nUtanAnAM dehAnAm avashyambhAvitvAt na taj-jIrNa-deha-nAshe shokAvakAsha ity arthaH ||22||

madhusUdanaH : nanv evam Atmano vinAshitvAbhAve 'pi dehAnAM vinAshitvAd yuddhasya ca tan-nAshakatvAt kathaM bhIShmAdi-dehAnAm aneka-sukR^ita-sAdhanAnAM mayA yuddhena vinAshaH kArya ity AshaN^kAyA uttaram vAsAMsIti | 

jIrNAni vihAya vastrANi navAni gR^ihNAti vikriyA-shUnya eva naro yathety etAvataiva virvAhe 'parANIit visheShaNam utkarShAtishaya-khyApanArtham | tena yathA nikR^iShTAni vastrANi vihAyotkR^iShTAni jano gR^ihNAtIty aucityAyAtam | tathA jIrNAni vayasA tapasA ca kR^ishAni bhIShmAdi-sharIrANi vihAyAnyAni devAdi-sharIrANi sarvotkR^iShTAni ciropArjita-dharma-phala-bhogAya saMyAti samyag-garbha-vAsAdi-klesha-vyatirekeNa prApnoti dehI prakR^iShTa-dharmAnuShThAtR^i-dehavAn bhIShmAdir ity arthaH | anyan navataraM kalyANataraM rUpaM kurute pitryaM vA gandharvaM vA daivaM vA prAjApatyaM vA brAhmaM vA ity Adi shruteH | 

etad uktaM bhavati bhIShmAdayo hi yAvaj jIvaM dharmAnuShThAna-kleshenaiva jarjara-sharIrA vartamAna-sharIra-pAtam antareNa tat-phala-bhogAyAsam arthA yadi dharma-yuddhena svarga-pratibandhakAni jarjarANi sharIrANi pAtayitvA divya-deha-sampAdanena svarga-bhoga-yogyAH kriyante tvayA tad-atyantam upakR^itvA eva te | duryodhanAdInAm api svarga-bhoga-yogya-deha-sampAdanAn mahAn upakAra eva | tathA cAtyantam upakArake yuddhe 'pakArakatva-bhramaM mA kArShIr iti | aparANi anyAni saMyAtIti pada-traya-vashAd bhagavad-abhiprAya evam abhyUhitaH | anena dR^iShTAntenAvikR^ita-pratipAdanam AtmanaH kriyata iti tu prAcAM vyAkhyAnam atispaShTam ||22||

vishvanAthaH : nanu madIya-yuddhAd bhIShma-saJNj~nakaM sharIraM tu jIvAtmA tyakShyaty eva ity atas tvaM cAhaM ca tatra hetu bhavAva eva ity ata Aha vAsAMsIti | navInaM vastraM paridhApayituM jIrNa-vastrasya tyajane kashcit kiM doSho bhavatIti bhAvaH | tathA sharIrANIti bhIShmo jIrNa-sharIraM parityajya divyaM navyaM anyac charIraM prApsyatIti kas tava vA mama vA doSho bhavatIti bhAvaH ||22||

baladevaH : nanu mA bhUd AtmanAM vinAsho bhIShmAdi-saJNj~nAnAM tac-charIrANAM tat-sukha-sAdhanAnAM yuddhena vinAshe tat-sukha-viccheda-hetuko doShaH syAd eva | anyathA prAyashcitta-shAstrANi nirviShayANi syur iti cet tatrAha vAsAMsIti | sthUla-jIrNa-vAsas-tyAgena navIna-vAso-dhAraNam iva vR^iddha-nR^i-deha-tyAgena yuva-deva-deha-dhAraNaM teShAm AtmanAm atisukhakaram eva | tad ubhayaM ca yuddhenaiva kShipraM bhaved ity upakArakAt tasmAn mA viraMsIr iti bhAvaH | saMyAtIti samyag-garbha-vAsAdi-yAtanAM vinaiva shIghram eva prApnotIty arthaH | prAyashcitta-vAkyAni tu yaj~na-yuddha-vadhAd anyasmin vadhe neyAni ||22||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.23

nainaM chindanti shastrANi nainaM dahati pAvakaH |
na cainaM kledayanty Apo na shoShayati mArutaH ||23||

shrIdharaH : kathaM hantIti anena uktaM vadha-sAdhanAbhAvaM darshayann avinAshitvam AtmanaH sphuTIkaroti nainam ity Adi | Apo kledayanti mR^idu-karaNena shithilaM na kurvanti | mAruto 'py enaM na shoShayati ||23||

madhusUdanaH :

vishvanAthaH : na ca yuddhe tvayA prayuktebhyaH shastrAstrebhyaH kApy Atmano vyathA sambhaved ity Aha nainam iti | shastrANi khaDgAdIni | pAvaka AgneyAstram api yuShmad-Adi-prayuktam | ApaH pArjanyAstram api | mAruto vAyavyAstram ||23||

baladevaH : nanu shastra-pAtaiH sharIra-vinAshe tad-antaH-sthasyAtmano vinAshaH syAt gR^iha-dAhe tan-madhya-sthasyaiva jantor iti cet tatrAha nainam iti | shastrANi khaDgAdIni | pAvaka AgneyAstram | ApaH pArjanyAstram api | mAruto vAyavyAstram | tathA ca tat-prayuktaiH shastrAstrair nAtmanaH kAcid vyatheti ||23||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.24

acchedyo 'yam adAhyo 'yam akledyo 'shoShya eva ca |
nityaH sarva-gataH sthANur acalo 'yaM sanAtanaH ||24||

shrIdharaH : tatra hetum Aha acchedya ity AdinA sArdhena | niravayavatvAd acchedyo 'kledyash ca | amUrtatvAd adAhyaH | dravatvAbhAvAd ashoShya iti bhAvaH | itash ca chedAdi-yogyo na bhavati | yato nityo 'vinAshI | sarva-gataH sthANuH sthira-svabhAvo rUpAntarApatti-shUnyaH | acalaH pUrva-rUpAparityAgI | sanAtano 'nAdiH ||24||

madhusUdanaH : shastrAdInAM tan-nAshakatvAsAmarthye tasya taj-janita-nAshAnarhatve hetum Aha acchedya iti | yato 'cchedyo 'yam ato nainaM chindanti shastrANi | adAhyo 'yaM yato 'to nainaM dahati pAvakaH | yato 'kledyo 'yam ato nainaM kledayanty ApaH | yato 'shoShyo 'yam ato nainaM shoShayati mAruta iti krameNa yojanIyam | eva-kAraH pratyekaM sambadhyamAno 'cchedyatvAdy-avadhAraNArthaH | caH samuccaye hetau vA | chedAdy-anarhatve hetum AhottarArdhena |

nityo 'yaM pUrvApara-koTi-rahito 'to 'nutpAdyaH | asarvagatatve hy anityatvaM syAt | yAvad-vikAraM tu vibhAgaH iti nyAyAt parAbhyupagata-paramANv-AdInAm anabhyupagamAt | ayaM tu sarva-gato vibhur ato nitya eva | etena prApyatvaM parAkR^itam | yadi cAyaM vikArI syAt tadA sarva-gato na syAt | ayaM tu sthANur avikArI | ataH sarva-gata eva | etena vikAryatvam apAkR^itam | yadi cAyaM calaH kriyAvAn syAt tadA vikArI syAd ghaTAdivat | ayaM tv acalo 'to na vikArI | etena saMskAryatvaM nirAkR^itam | pUrvAvasthA-parityAgenAvasthAntarApattir vikriyA | avasthaikye 'pi calana-mAtraM kriyeti visheShaH | yasmAd evaM tasmAt sanAtano 'yaM sarvadaika-rUpo na kasyA api kriyAyAH karmety arthaH | utpatty-Apti-vikR^iti-saMskR^ity-anyatara-kriyA-phala-yoge hi karmatvaM syAt | ayaM tu nityatvAn notpAdyaH | anityasyaiva ghaTAder utpAdyatvAt | sarvagatatvAn na prApyaH paricchinnasyaiva paya-AdeH prApyatvAt | sthANutvAd avikAryaH | vikriyAvato ghR^itAder eva vikAryatvAt | acalatvAd asaMskAryaH sakriyasyaiva darpaNAdeH saMskAryatvAt | tathA ca shrutayaH - AkAshavat sarva-gatash ca nityaH [ChAU 3.14.3], vR^ikSha iva stabdho divi tiShThaty ekaH [ÁvetU 3.9], niShkalaM niShkriyaM shAntaM [ÁvetU 6.19], ity AdayaH | yaH pR^ithivyAM tiShThan pR^ithivyA antaro yo 'psu tiShThann adbhyo 'ntaro yas tejasi tiShThaMs tejaso 'ntaro yo vAyau tiShTan vAyor antaraH [BAU 3.7.3 ff] ity AdyA ca shrutiH sarvagatasya sarvAntaryAmitayA tad-aviShayatvaM darshayati | yo hi shastrAdau na tiShThati taM shastrAdayash chindanti | ayaM tu shastrAdInAM sattA-sphUrti-pradatvena tat-prerakas tad-antaryAmI | ataH katham enaM shastrAdIni sva-vyApAra-viShayI kuryur ity abhiprAyaH | atra yena sUryas tapati tejaseddhaH [Taitt. Br. 3.12.97] ity Adi shrutayo 'nusandheyAH | saptamAdhyAye ca prakaTIkariShyati shrI-bhagavAn iti dik ||24||

vishvanAthaH : tasmAd AtmAyam evam ucyata ity Aha acchedya iti | atra prakaraNe jIvAtmano nityatvasya shabdato 'rthatash ca paunaruktyaM nirdhAraNa-prayojakaM sandigdhadhIShu j~neyam | yathA kalAv asmin dharmo 'sti dharmo 'stIti tri-caturdhA-prayogAd dharmo 'sty eveti niHsaMshayA pratItiH syAd iti j~neyam | sarva-gataH svakarma-vashAd deva-manuShya-tiryag-Adi-sarva-deha-gataH | sthANur acala iti paunaruktyaM sthairya-nirdhAraNArtham | atisUkShmatvAd avyaktas tad api deha-vyApi-caitanyatvAd acintyo 'tarkyaH | janmAdi-ShaD-vikArAnarhatvAd avikAryaH ||24-25||

baladevaH : chedAdy-abhAvAd eva tat-tan-nAmabhir ayam AkhyAyata ity Aha acchedyo 'yam iti | eva-kAraH sarvaiH sambadhyate | sarva-gataH sva-karma-hetukeShu deva-mAnavAdiShu pashu-pakShy-AdiShu ca sarveShu sharIreShu paryAyeNa gataH prApto 'pIty arthaH | sthANuH sthira-svarUpaH | acalaH sthira-guNakaH | avinAshI vA are 'yam AtmAnucchitti-dharmA [Bau 4.5.14] iti shruter ity arthaH | na cAnucchittir eva dharmo yasyeti vyAkhyeyaM tasyArthasyAvinAshIty anenaiva lAbhAt | tasmAd anucchittayo nityA dharmA yasya sa tathety evArthaH | sanAtanaH shAshvataH paunarukta-doShas tv agre parihariShyate ||24||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.25

avyakto 'yam acintyo 'yam avikAryo 'yam ucyate |
tasmAd evaM viditvainaM nAnushocitum arhasi ||25||

shrIdharaH : kiM ca avyakta iti | avyaktash cakShur-Ady-aviShayaH | acintyo manaso 'py aviShayaH | avikAryaH karmendriyANAm apy agocara ity arthaH | ucyata iti nityatvAdibhiyuktoktiM pramANayati | upasaMharati tasmAd evam ity Adi | tad evam Atmano janma-vinAshAbhAvAn na shokaH kArya ity uktam ||25||

madhusUdanaH : chedyatvAdi-grAhaka-pramANa-bhAvAd api tad-abhAva ity Aha - avyakto 'yam ity-Ady-ardhena | yo hIndriya-gocaro bhavati sa pratyakShatvAd vyakta ity ucyate | ayaM tu rUpAdi-hInatvAn na tathA | ato na pratyakShaM tatra cchedyatvAdi-grAhakam ity arthaH | 

pratyakShAbhAve 'py anumAnaM syAd ity ata Aha acintyo 'yaM cintyo 'numeyas tad-vilakShaNo 'yam | kvacit pratyakSho hi vahny-Adir gR^ihIta-vyAptikasya dhUmAder darshanAt kvacid anumeyo bhavati | apratyakShe tu vyApti-grahaNAsambhavAn nAnumeyatvam iti bhAvaH | apratyakShasyApIndriyAdeH sAmAnyato dR^iShTAnumAna-viShayatvaM dR^iShTam ata Aha avikAryo 'yaM yad vikriyAvac cakShur-AdikaM tat-svakAryAnyathAnupapattyA kalpyamAnam arthApatteH sAmAnyatodR^iShTAnumAnasya ca viShayo bhavati | ayaM tu na vikAryo na vikriyAvAn ato nArthApatteH sAmAnyato-dR^iShTasya vA viShaya ity arthaH | laukika-shabdasyApi pratyakShAdi-pUrvakatvAt tan-niShedhenaiva niShedhaH |

nanu vedenaiva tatra ccehdyatvAdi grahIShyata ity ata Aha - ucyate vedena sopakaraNenAcchedyAvyaktAdi-rUpa evAyam ucyate tAtparyeNa pratipAdyate | ato na vedasya tat-pratipAdikasyApi cchedyatvAdi-pratipAdakatvam ity arthaH |

atra nainaM chindanti [GItA 2.23] ity atra shastrAdInAM tan-nAshaka-sAmarthyAbhAva uktaH | acchedyo 'yam ity Adau tasya cchedAdi-karmatvAyogyatvam uktam | avyakto 'yam ity atra tac-chedAdi-grAhaka-mAnAbhAva ukta ity apaunaruktyaM draShTavyam | vedAvinAshinam ity AdInAM tu shlokAnAm arthataH shabdatash ca paunaruktyaM bhAShya-kR^idbhiH parihR^itam | durbodhatvAd Atma-vastunaH punaH punaH prasaN^gam ApAdya shabdAntareNa tad eva vastu nirUpayati bhagavAn vAsudevaH kathaM nu nAma saMsAriNAm buddhi-gocaratAm ApannaM tattvaM saMsAra-nivR^ittaye syAt iti [ÁaN^kara-bhAShya 2.24] iti vadadbhiH |

evaM pUrvokta-yuktibhir Atmano nityatve nirvikAratve ca siddhe tava shoko nopapanna ity upasaMharati tasmAd ity ardhena | etAdR^ishAtma-svarUpa-vedanasya shoka-kAraNa-nivartakatvAt tasmin sati shoko nocitaH kAraNa-bhAve kAryAbhAvasyAvashyakatvAt | tenAtmAnam aviditvA yad anvashocas tad yuktam eva | AtmAnaM viditvA tu nAnushocitum arhasIty abhiprAyaH ||25||

vishvanAthaH : None.

baladevaH : avyaktaH pratyaÇ cakShur-Ady-agrAhyaH | acintyas tarkAgocaraH shruti-mAtra-gamyaH | j~nAna-svarUpo j~nAtety AdikaM shrutyaiva pratIyate | avikAryaH ShaD-bhAva-vikArAnarhaH | atra avinAshi tu tad viddhi ity Adibhir Atma-tattvam upadishan hariH shabdato 'rthatash ca yat punaH punar avocat tasya durbodhasya saubodhyArtham evety adoShaH | nirdhAraNArthaM vA | ayaM dharmaM vettIty uktau tad vedanaM nishcitaM yathA syAt tadvat | evam evAgre vakShyati Ashcaryavat pashyati kashcit ity AdinA ||25|| 

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.26

atha cainaM nityajAtaM nityaM vA manyase mR^itam |
tathApi tvaM mahAbAho naivaM shocitum arhasi ||26||

shrIdharaH : idAnIM dehena saha Atmano janma tad-vinAshena ca vinAsham aN^gIkR^ityApi shoko na kArya ity Aha atha cainam ity Adi | atha ca yadyapy enam AtmAnam nityajAtaM nityaM vA manyase mR^itam tathApi tvaM mahAbAho naivaM shocitum arhasi ||26||

madhusUdanaH : evam Atmano nirvikAratvenAshocyatvam uktam idAnIM vikAravattvam abhyupetyApi shloka-dvayenAshocyatvaM pratipAdayati bhagavAn | tatrAtmA j~nAna-svarUpaH pratikShaNa-vinAshIti saugatAH | deha evAtmA sa ca sthiro 'py anukShaNa-pariNAmI  jAyate nashyati ceti pratyakSha-siddham evaitad iti lokAyatikAH | dehAtirikto 'pi dehena sahaiva jAyate nashyati cety anye | sargAdya-kAla evAkAshavaj jAyate deha-bhede 'py anuvartamAna evAkalpa-sthAyI nashyati pralaya ity apare | nitya evAtmA jAyate mriyate ceti tArkikAH | tathA hi - pretya-bhAvo janma | sa cApUrva-dehendriyAdi-sambandhaH | evaM maraNam api pUrva-dehendriyAdi-vicchedaH | idaM cobhayaM dharmAdharma-nimittatvAt tad-AdhArasya nityasyaiva mukhyam | anityasya tu kR^ita-hAnya-kR^itAbhyAgama-prasaN^gena dharmAdharmAdhAratvAnupapatter na janma-maraNe mukhye iti vadanti | ntiyasyAm evety anye | tatrAnityatva-pakShe 'pi shocyatvam Atmano niShedhati atha cainam iti |

atheti pakShAntare | co 'py arthe | yadi durbodhatvAd Atma-vastuno 'sakR^ic-chravaNe 'py avadhAraNA-sAmarthyAn mad-ukta-pakShAnaN^gIkAreNa pakShAntaram abhyupaiShi | tatrApy anityatva-pakSham evAshritya yady enam AtmAnaM nityaM jAtaM nityaM mR^itaM vA manyase | vA-shabdash cArthe | kShaNikatva-pakShe nityaM pratikShaNaM pakShAntare AvashyakatvAn nityaM niyataM jAto 'yaM mR^ito 'yam iti laukika-pratyaya-vashena yadi kalpayasi tathApi he mahAbAho ! puruSha-dhaureyeti sopahAsaM kumatAbhyupagamAt | tvayy etAdR^ishI kudR^iShTir na sambhavatIti sAnukampaM vA | evaM aha bata mahat pApaM kartuM vyavasitA vayam [GItA 1.45] ity Adi yathA shocasi evaM prakAram anushokaM kartuM svayam api tvaM tAdR^isha eva san nArhasi yogyo na bhavasi | kShaNikatva-pakShe dehAtma-vAda-pakShe dehena saha janma-vinAsha-pakShe ca janmAntarAbhAvena pApa-bhayAsambhavAt pApa-bhayenaiva khalu tvam anushocasi | tac caitAdR^ishe darshane na sambhavati bandhu-vinAsha-darshitvAbhAvAd ity adhikaM | pakShAntare dR^iShTa-duHkha-nimittaM shokam abhyanuj~nAtum evaM-kAraH | dR^iShTa-duHkha-nimitta-shoka-sambhave 'py adR^iShTa-duHkha-nimittaH shokaH sarvathA nocita ity arthaH prathama-shlokasya ||26||

vishvanAthaH : tad evaM shAstrIya-tattva-dR^iShTyA tvAm ahaM prabodhayan | vyAvahArahika-tattva-dR^iShTyApi prabodhayAmi avadhehIty Aha atheti | nitya-jAtaM dehe jAte saty enaM nityaM niyataM jAtaM manyase | tathA deha eva mR^ite mR^itaM nityaM niyataM manyase | mahA-bAho iti parAkramavataH kShatriyasya tava tad api yuddham avashyakaM svadharmaH | yad uktaM -

kShatriyANAm ayaM dharmaH prajApati-vinirmitaH |
bhrAtApi bhrAtaraM hanyAd yena ghorataras tataH || iti bhAvaH ||26||

baladevaH : evaM svoktasya jIvAtmano 'shocyatvam uktvA paroktasyApi tasya tad ucyate para-mata-j~nAnAya | tad-abhij~naH khalu shiShyas tad-avakarais tan nirasya vijayI san sva-mate sthairyam AsIt | tathA hi manuShyatvAdi-vishiShTe bhUmy-Adi-bhUta-catuShTaye tAmbUla-rAgavat mada-shaktivac ca caitanyam utpadyate | tAdR^ishas tac-catuShTaya-bhUto deha evAtmA | sa ca sthiro 'pi pratikShaNa-pariNAmAd utpatti-vinAsha-yogIti loka-pratyakSha-siddham iti lokAyatikA manyante | dehAd bhinno vij~nAna-svarUpo 'py AtmA pratikShaNa-vinAshIti vaibhAShikAdayo bauddhA vadanti | tad etad ubhaya-mate 'py AtmanaH shocyatvaM pratiShedhati | atheti pakShAntare | co 'py-arthe | tvaM cen mad-ukta-jIvAtma-yAthAtmyAvagAhanAsamartho lokAyatikAdi-pakSham Alambase, tatra dehAtma-pakShe enaM deha-lakShaNam AtmAnaM nityaM vA mR^itaM manyase | vA-shabdash cArthe | tathApi tvam enaM aho bata mahat pApaM ity Adi-vacanaiH shocituM nArhasi | pariNAma-svabhAvasya tasya tasya cAtmano janma-vinAshayor anivAryatvAj janmAntarAbhAvena pApa-bhayAsambhavAc ca | he mahAbAho iti sopahAsaM sambodhanaM kShatriya-varyasya vaidikasya ca te nedR^ishaM kumataM dhAryam iti bhAvaH ||26|

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.27

jAtasya hi dhruvo mR^ityur dhruvaM janma mR^itasya ca |
tasmAd aparihArye 'rthe na tvaM shocitum arhasi ||27||

shrIdharaH : kuta iti ? ata Aha jAtasyety-Adi | hi yasmAj jAtasya svArambhaka-karma-kShaye mR^ityur dhruvo nishcitaH | mR^itasya ca tad-deha-kR^itena karmaNA janmApi dhruvam eva | tasmAd evam aparihArye 'rthe avashyambhAvini janma-maraNa-lakShaNe 'rthe tvaM vidvAn shocitum nArhasi yogyo na bhavasi ||27||

madhusUdanaH : nanv Atmana AbhUta-saMplava-sthAyitva-pakShe ca dR^iShTAdR^iShTa-duHkha-sambhavAt tad-bhayena shocAmIty ata Aha dvitIya-shlokena jAtasya hIti | hi yasmAj jAtasya sva-kR^ita-dharmAdharmAdi-vashAl labdha-sharIrendriyAdi-sambandhasya sthirasyAtmano dhruva Avashyako mR^ityus tac-charIrAdi-vicchedas tad-Arambhaka-karma-kShaya-nimittaH saMyogasya viyogAvasAnatvAt | tathA dhruvaM janma mR^itasya ca prAg-deha-kR^ita-karma-phalopabhogArthaM sAnushayasyaiva prastutatvAn na jIvan-mukte vyabhicAraH | tasmAd evam aparihArye parihartum ashakye 'smin janma-maraNa-lakShaNe 'rthe viShaye tvam evaM vidvAn na shocitum arhasi | tathA ca vakShyati R^ite 'pi tvAM na bhaviShyanti sarve [GItA 11.32] iti | yadi hi tvayA yuddhe 'nAhanyamAnA ete jIveyur eva tadA yuddhAya shokas tavocitaH syAt | ete tu karma-kShayAt svayam eva mriyanta iti tat-parihArAsamarthasya tava dR^iShT-duHkha-nimittaH shoko nocita iti bhAvaH |

evam adR^iShTa-duHkha-nimitte 'pi shoke tasmAd aparihArye 'rthe ity evottaram | yuddhAkhyaM hi karma kShatriyasya niyatam agnihotrAdivat | tac ca yudha samprahAre ity asmAd dhAtor niShpannaM shatru-prANa-viyogAnukUla-shastra-prahAra-rUpaM vihitatvAgnIShomIyAdi-siMhAvan na pratyavAya-janakam | tathA ca gautamaH smarati na doSho hiMsAyAm Ahave 'nyatra vyashvAsArathyanuyudha-kR^itA¤jali-prakIrNa-kesha-parAÇmukhopaviShTa-sthala-vR^ikShArUDha-dUta-go-brAhmaNa-vAdibhyaH iti | brAhmaNa-grahaNaMcAtrAyoddhR^i-brAhmaNa-viShayaM gavAdi-prAya-pAThAd iti sthitam | etac ca sarvaM svadharmam api cAvekShyety atra spaShTIkariShyati | tathA ca yuddha-lakShaNe 'rthe 'gnihotrAdivad vihitatvAd aparihArye parihartum ashakye tad-akaraNe pratyavAya-prasaN^gAt tvam adR^iShTa-duHkha-bhayena shocituM nArahasIti pUrvavat |

yadi tu yuddhAkhyaM karma kAmyam eva -

ya AhaveShu yudhyante bhUmy-artham aparAÇmukhAH |
akUTair Ayudhair yAnti te svargaM yogino yathA || [Yaj~n. 13.324]

iti yAj~navalkya-vacanAt | hato vA prApsyasi svargaM jitvA vA bhokShyase mahIm [GItA 2.37] iti bhagavad-vacanAc ca | tadApi prArabdhasya kAmyasyApi avashya-parisamApanIyatvena nitya-tulyatvAt tvayA ca yuddhasya prArabdhatvAd aparihAryatvaM tyulyam eva |

athavAtma-nityatva-pakSha eva shloka-dvayam arjunasya paramAstikasya veda-bAhya-matAbhyupagamAsambhavAt | akShara-yojanA tu nityash cAsau dehendriyAdi-sambandha-vashAj jAtash ceti nitya-jAtas tam enam AtmAnaM nityam api santaM jAtaM cen manyase tathA nityam api santaM mR^itaM cen manyase tathApi tvaM nAnushocitum arhasIti hetum Aha jAtasya hIty AdinA | nityasya jAtatvaM mR^itatvaM ca prAg-vyAkhyAtam | spaShTam anyat | bhAShyam apy asmin pakShe yojanIyam ||27||

vishvanAthaH : hi yasmAt tasya svArambhaka-karma-kShaye mR^ityur dhruvo nishcitaH | mR^itasya ca tad-deha-kR^itena karmaNA janmApi dhruvam eva | aparihArye 'rthe iti mR^ityur janma ca parihartum a]cakyam eva ity arthaH ||27||

baladevaH : atha sharIrAtirikto nitya AtmA | tasyApUrva-sharIrendriya-yogo janma | pUrva-sharIrendriya-viyogas tu maraNaM tad-ubhayaM ca dharmAdharma-hetukatvAt tad-Ashrayasya nityasyAtmano mukhyaM, tad-atiriktasya sharIrasya tu gauNam | tasyAnityasya kR^ita-hAnya-kR^itAbhyAgama-prasaN^gena tad-AshrayatvAnupapatter iti tArkikA manyante | tat-pakShe 'py AtmanaH shocyatvaM pariharati jAtasyeti | hir hetau | jAtasya sva-karma-vashAt prApta-sharIrAdi-yogasya nityasyApy Atmanas tad-Arambhaka-karma-kShaya-hetuko mR^ityur dhruvo nishcitaH | mR^itasya tac-charIra-kR^ita-karma-hetukaM janma ca dhruvaM syAt | tasmAd evam aparihArye parihartum ashakye janma-maraNAtmake 'rthe tvaM vidvAn shocituM nArhasi | tvayi yuddhAn nivR^itte 'py ete svArambhake karmaNi kShINe sati mariShyanty eva | tava tu svadharmAd vicyutir bhAvinIti bhAvaH ||27||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.28

avyaktAdIni bhUtAni vyakta-madhyAni bhArata |
avyakta-nidhanAny eva tatra kA paridevanA ||28||

shrIdharaH : kiM ca dehAnAM svabhAvaM paryAlocya tad-upAdhike Atmano janma-maraNe shoko na kArya iti | ata Aha avyaktAdInIty Adi | avyaktaM pradhAnam | tad eva Adir utpatteH pUrva-rUpaM yeShAM tAni avyaktAdIni | bhUtAni sharIrANi | kAraNAtmanApi sthitAnAm eva utpatteH | tathA vyaktam abhivyaktaM madhyaM janma-maraNAntarAlaM sthiti-lakShaNaM yeShAM tAni vyakta-madhyAni | avyakte nidhanaM layo yeShAM tAnImAny evaM-bhUtAny eva | tatra teShu kA paridevanA ? kaH shoka-nimitto vilApaH ? pratibuddhasya svapna-dR^iShTa-vastuShv iva shoko na yujyata ity arthaH ||28||

madhusUdanaH : tad evaM sarva-prakAreNAtmano 'shocyatvam upapAditam athedAnIm Atmano 'shocyatve 'pi bhUta-saN^ghAtAtmakAni sharIrANy uddishya shocAmIty arjunAshaN^kAm apanudati bhagavAn avyaktAdInIti | Adau janmanaH prAg-avyaktAni anupalabdhAni bhUtAni pR^ithivyAdi-bhUta-mayAni sharIrANi madhye janmAnantaraM maraNAt prAg-vyaktAni upalabdhAni santi | nidhane punar avyaktAny eva bhavanti | yathA svapnendrajAlAdau pratibhAsa-mAtra-jIvanAni shukti-rUpyAdivan na tu j~nAnAt prAg UrdhvaM vA sthitAni dR^iShTi-sR^iShTy-abhyupagamAt | tathA ca - AdAv ante ca yan nAsti vartamAne 'pi tat tathA [MA. KA. 2.6] iti nyAyena madhye 'pi na santy evaitAni | nAsato vidyate bhAvaH [GItA 2.16] iti prAg-uktesh ca |

evaM sati tatra teShu mithyA-bhUteShv atyanta-tuccheShu bhUteShu kA paridevanA ko vA duHkha-pralApo na ko 'py ucita ity arthaH | na hi svapne vividhAn bandhUn upalabhya pratibuddhas tad-vicchedena shocati pR^ithag-jano 'pi etad evoktaM purANe adarshanAd ApatitaH punash cAdarshanaM gataH bhUta-saN^gha iti sheShaH | tathA ca sharIrANy apy uddishya shoko nocita iti bhAvaH |
AkAshAdi-mahA-bhUtAbhiprAyeNa vA shloko yojyaH | avyaktam avyAkR^itam avidyopahita-caitanyam AdiH prAg avasthA yeShAM tAni tathA vyaktaM nAma-rUpAbhyAm evAvidyakAbhyAM prakaTIbhUtaM na tu svena paramArtha-sadAtmanA madhyaM sthity-avasthA yeShAM tAdR^ishAni bhUtAni AkAshAdIni avyakta-nidhanAny evAvyakte sva-kAraNe mR^id iva ghaTAdInAM nidhanaM pralayo yeShAM teShu bhUteShu kA paridevaneti pUrvavat | tathA ca shrutiH - tad dhedaM tarhy avyAkR^itam AsIt tan-nAma-rUpAbhyAm eva vyAkriyata [BAU 1.4.7] ity Adir avyaktopAdAnatAM sarvasya prapa¤casya darshayati | laya-sthAnatvaM tu tasyArtha-siddhaM kAraNa eva kArya-layasya darshanAt | granthAntare tu vistaraH | tathA cAj~nAna-kalpitatvena tucchAny AkAshAdi-bhUtAny apy uddishya shoko nocitash cet tat-kAryANy uddishya nocita iti kim u vaktavyam iti bhAvaH |

athavA sarvadA teShAm avyakta-rUpeNa vidyamAnatvAd vicchedAbhAvena tan-nimittaH pralApo nocita ity arthaH | bhAratety anena sambodhayan shuddha-vaMshodbhavatvena shAstrIyam arthaM pratipattum arho 'si kim iti na pratipadyasa iti sUcayati ||28||

vishvanAthaH : tad evaM na jAyate na mriyate ity-AdinA, deha-pakShe ca jAtasya hi dhruvo mR^ityuH ity anena shoka-viShayaM nirAkR^itya idAnIm ubhaya-pakShe 'pi nirAkaroti avyakteti | bhUtAni deva-manuShya-tiryag-AdIni | avyaktAni na vyaktaM vyaktir Adau janma-pUrva-kAle yeShAM, kintu tadAnIm api liN^ga-dehaH sthUla-dehash ca svArambhaka-pR^ithivy-Adi-sattvAt kAraNAtmanA vartamAno 'spaShTam AsId evety arthaH | vyaktaM vyaktir madhye yeShAM tAni | na vyakti nidhanAd anantaraM yeShAM tAni | mahA-pralaye 'pi karma-mAtrAdInAM sattvAt sUkShma-rUpeNa bhUtAni santy eva | tasmAt sarva-bhUtAni Ady-antarayor avyaktAni madhye vyaktAnIty arthaH | yad uktaM shrutibhiH - sthira-cara-jAtayaH syur ajayottha-nimitta-yujaH iti | kA paridevanA kaH shoka-nimittaH vilApaH ? tathA coktaM nAradena - 

yan manyase dhruvaM lokam adhruvaM vA na cobhayam | 
sarvathA na hi shocyAs te snehAd anyatra mohajAt || [BhP 1.13.44] iti ||28||

baladevaH : atha dehAtma-pakShe AtmAtirikta-deha-pakShe ca deha-vinAsha-hetuka-shoko na yuktas tad-ArambhakANAM bhUta-mAtrANAm avinAshAd ity Aha avyaktAdInIti | avyaktaM nAma-rUpa-virahAt sUkShmaM pradhAnam Adi Adi-rUpaM yeShAM tAni avyakta-nidhanAni | avyakte tAdR^ishi pradhAne nidhanaM nAma-rUpa-vimardana-lakShaNo nAsho yeShAM tAni | mR^id-Adike sad-rUpe dravye kambu-grIvAdy-avasthA-yoge ghaTasyotpattis tad-virodhi-kapAlAdy-avasthA-yogas tu tasya vinAshaH kathyate | tad-dravyaM sarvadA sthAyIti | evam evAha bhagavAn parAsharaH - mahI ghaTatvaM ghaTataH kapAlikA cUrNa-rajas tato 'NuH [ViP 2.12.42] iti | evaM sharIrANy Ady-antayor nAma-rUpAyogAd avyaktimanti | madhye tu tad-yogAd vyaktimanti | tad-ArambhakAni bhUtAni tu sarvadA santIti teShu vastutaH satsu kA paridevanA kaH shoka-nimitta-vilApa ity arthaH | dehAnya-nityAtma-pakShe tu vAsAMsi ity AdikaM na vismartavyam | yat tv Ady-antayor asattvAn madhye 'pi bhUtAny asanty evAtaH svApnika-rathAshvAdi-prakhyAni mR^iShA-bhUtAny eva tena tad-viyoga-hetukaH shokaH pratibuddhasya na dR^iShTa iti dR^iShTi-sR^iShTim abhyupaityAhus tan mandaM tad-abhyupagame vaidikAsatkAryavAdApatteH | tad evaM mata-dvaye 'pi deha-vinAsha-hetukaH shoko nAstIti siddham ||28||

BhG 2.29

Ashcaryavat pashyati kashcid enam
Ashcaryavad vadati tathaiva cAnyaH |
Ashcaryavac cainam anyaH shR^iNoti
shrutvApy enaM veda na caiva kashcit ||29||

shrIdharaH : kutas tarhi vidvAMso 'pi loke shocanti ? AtmA-j~nAnAd eva ity AshayenAtmano durvij~neyatvam Aha Ashcaryavad ityAdi | kashcid enam AtmAnaM shAstrAcAryopadeshAbhyAM pashyann Ashcaryavat pashyati | sarva-gatasya nitya-j~nAnAnada-svabhAvasyAtmanaH alaukikatvAd aindrajAlikavad ghaTamAnaM pashyann iva vismayena pashyati asambhAvanAbhibhUtatvAt | tathA Ashcaryavad anyo vadati ca | shR^iNoti cAnyaH | kashcit punaH viparIta-bhAvanAbhibhUtaH shrutvApi naiva veda | ca-shabdAd uktvApi na dR^iShTvApi na samyag vedeti draShTavyam ||29||

madhusUdanaH : nanu vidvAMso 'pi bahavaH shocanti tat kiM mAm eva punaH punar evam upAlabhase | anyac ca vaktur eva hi taj jADyaM shrotA yatra na budhyate  iti nyAyAt tvad-vacanArthApartipattish ca tavApy anyeShAm iva svAshaya-doShAd iti nokta-doSha-dvayam ity abhipretyAtmano durvij~neyatAm Aha Ashcaryavad iti |

enaM prakR^itaM dehinam AshcaryeNAdbhutena tulyatayA vartamAnam Avidyaka-nAnA-vidha-viruddha-dharmavattayA satanm apy asantam iva sva-prakAsha-caitanya-rUpam api jaDam ivAnanda-ghanam api duHkhitam iva nirvikAram api savikAram iva nityam anityam iva prakAshamAnam apy aprakAshamAnam iva brahmAbhinnam api tad-bhinnam iva muktam api baddham ivAdvitIyam api sa-dvitIyam iva sambhAvita-vicitrAnekAkAra-pratIti-viShayaM pashyati shAstrAcAryopadeshAbhyAm Avidyaka-sarva-dvaita-niShedhena  paramAtma-svarUpa-mAtrAkArAyAM vedAnta-mahA-vAkya-janyAyAM sarva-sukR^ita-phala-bhUtAyAm antaHkaraNa-vR^ittau pratiphalitaM samAdhi-paripAkena sAkShAtkaroti  kashcic chama-damAdi-sAdhana-sampanna-carama-sharIraH kashcid eva na tu sarvaH | tathA kashcid enaM yat pashyati tad Ashcaryavad iti kriyA-visheShaNam | Atma-darshanam apy Ashcaryavad eva yat svarUpato mithyA-bhUtam api satyasya vya¤jakam Avidyakam apy avidyAyA vighAtakam avidyAm upaghnat tat-kAryatayA svAtmAnam apy upahantIti | tathA yaH kashcid enaM pashyati sa Ashcaryavad iti kartR^i-visheShaNam | yato 'sau nivR^ittAvidyAtat-kAryo 'pi prArabdha-karma-prAbalyAt tadvAn iva vyaharati sarvadA samAdhi-niShTho 'pi vyuttiShThati vyutthito 'pi punaH samAdhim anubhavatIti prArabdha-karma-vaicitryAd vicitra-caritraH prApta-duShprApa-j~nAnatvAt sakala-loka-spR^ihaNIyo 'ta Ashcaryavad eva bhavati | tad etat trayam apy Ashcaryam AtmA taj j~nAnaM taj-j~nAtA ceti parama-durvij~neyam AtmAnaM tvaM katham anAyAsena jAnIyA ity abhiprAyaH |

Ivam upadeShTur abhAvAd apy AtmA durvij~neyaH | yo hy AtmAnaM jAnAti sa eva tam anyasmai dhruvaM brUyAt | aj~nasyopadeShTR^itvAsambhavAt, jAnaMs tu samAhita-cittaH prAyeNa kathaM bravItu | vyutthita-citto 'pi pareNa j~nAtum ashakyaH | yathA kathaMcij j~nAto 'pi lAbha-pUjA-khyAty-Adi-prayojanAnapekShatvAc ca bravIty eva | kathaMcit kAruNya-mAtreNa bruvaMs tu parameshvaravad atyanta-durlabha evety Aha Ashcaryavad vadati tathaiva cAnya iti | yathAjAnAti tathaiva vadati | enam ity anukarShaNArthash ca-kAraH | sa cAnyaH sarvAj~na-jana-vilakShaNaH | na tu yaH pashyati tato 'nya iti vyAghAtAt | atrApi karmaNi kriyAyAM kartari cAshcaryavad iti yojyam | tatra karmaNaH kartush ca prAg AshcaryavattvaM vyAkhyAtaM kriyAyAs tu vyAkhyAyate | sarva-shabdAvAcyasya shuddhasyAtmano yad vacanaM tad Ashcaryavat | tathA ca shrutiH - yato vAco nivartante aprApya manasA saha iti | kenApi shabdenAvAcyasya shuddhasyAtmano vishiShTa-shaktena padena jahad-ajahat-svArtha-lakShaNAyA kalpita-sambandhena lakShyatAvacchedakam antareNaiva pratipAdanaM tad api nirvikalpa-sAkShAtkAra-rUpam atyAshcaryam ity arthaH |

athavA vinA shaktiM vinA lakShaNAM vinA sambandhAntaraM suShuptotthApaka-vAkya-vat tattvam asyAdi-vAkyena yadAtmatattva-pratipAdanaM tad Ashcaryavat | shabda-shakter acintyatvAt | na ca vinA sambandhaM bodhanen 'tiprasaN^gaH lakShaNA-pakShe 'pi tulyatvAt | shakya-sambandhasyAneka-sAdhAraNatvAt | tAtparya-visheShAn niyama iti cet, na | tasyApi sarvAn praty avisheShAt | kashcid eva tAtparya-visheSham avadhArayati na sarva iti cet | hanta tarhi puruSha-gata eva kashcid visheSho nirdoShatva-rUpo niyAmakaH | na cAsmin pakShe 'pi na daNDa-vAritaH | tathA ca yAdR^ishasya shuddhAntaH-karaNasya tAtparyAnusandhAna-puraH-saraM lakShaNayA vAkyArtha-bodho bhavadbhir aN^gI kriyate tAdR^ishasyaiva kevalaH shabda-visheSho 'khaNDa-sAkShAtkAraM vinApi sambandhena janayatIti kim anupapannam | etasmin pakShe shabda-vR^itty-aviShayatvAd yato vAco nivartanta iti sutarAm upapannam | ayaM ca bhagavad-abhiprAyo vArtika-kAraiH prapa¤citaH -

durbalatvAd avidyAyA AtmatvAd bodha-rUpiNaH |
shabda-shakter acitnyatvAd vidmas taM moha-hAnataH ||
agR^ihItvaiva sambandham abhidhAnAbhidheyayoH | 
hitvA nidrAM prabudhyante suShupter bodhitAH paraiH ||
jAgradvan na yataH shabdaM suShupte vetti kashcana |
dhvaste 'to j~nAnato 'j~nAne brahmAsmIti bhavet phalam ||
avidyA-ghAtinaH shabdAdyAhaM brahmeti dhIr bhavet |
nashyaty avidyayA sArdhaM hatvA rogam ivauShadham || [BR^ihat.VA 1.4.860-863] 
ity AdinA granthena | 

tad evaM vacana-viShayasya vaktur vacana-kriyAyAsh cAtyAshcarya-rUpatvAd Atmano durvij~nAnatvam uktvA shrotur durmilatvAd api tad Aha Ashcaryavac cainam anyaH shR^iNoti shrtuvA 'py enaM vedeti | anyo draShTur vaktushc a muktAd vilakShaNo mumukShur vaktAraM brahma-vidaM vidhivad upasR^ityainaM shR^iNoti shravaNAkhya-vicAra-viShayI karoti vedAnta-vAkya-tAtparya-nishcayenAvadhArayatIti yAvat | shrutvA cainaM manana-nididhyAsana-paripAkAd vedApi sAkShAtkaroty api Ashcaryavat | tathA cAshcaryavat pashyati kashcid enam iti vyAkhyAtam | atrApi kartur Ashcarya-rUpatvam aneka-janmAnuShThita-sukR^ita-kShAlita-mano-malatayAtidurlabhatvAt | tathA ca vakShyati -

manuShyANAM sahasreShu kash cid yatati siddhaye |
yatatAm api siddhAnAM kash cin mAM vetti tattvataH || [GItA 7.3] iti |

shravaNAyApi bahubhir yo na labhyaH 
shR^iNvanto 'pi bahavo yaM na vidyuH |
Ashcaryo vaktA kushalo 'sya labdhA
Ashcaryo j~nAtA kushalAnushiShTaH || [KaThU 1.2.7] iti shrutesh ca |

evaM shravaNa-shrotavyayor AshcaryatvaM prAgvad vyAkhyeyam |

nanu yaH shravaNa-mananAdikaM karoti sa AtmAnaM vedeti kim Ashcaryam ata Aha - na caiva kashcid iti | ca-kAraH kriyA-karma-padayor anuShaN^gArthaH | kashcid enaM naiva veda shravaNAdikaM kurvann api | tad akurvaMs tu na vedeti kim u vaktavyam | aihikam aprastuta-pratibandhe tad-darshanAt [Vs. 3.4.51] iti nyAyAt | uktaM ca vArtika-kAraiH -

kutas taj-j~nAnam iti cet tad dhi bandha-parikShayAt |
asAv api ca bhUtau vA bhAvI vA vartate 'thavA || [BR^ih. VA. Sa. 294] iti | 

shravaNAdi kurvatAm api pratibandha-parikShayAd eva j~nAnaM jAyate | anyathA tu na | sa ca pratibandha-parikShayaH kasyacid bhUta eva | yathA hiraNyagarbhasya | kasyacid bhAvI | yathA vAsudevasya | kasyacid vartate | yathA shvetaketoH | tathA ca pratibandha-kShaya-syAtidurlabhatvAt | j~nAnam utpadyate puMsAM kShayAt pApasya karmaNaH iti smR^itesh ca durvij~neyo 'yam Atmeti nirgalito 'rthaH | 

yadi tu shrutvApy enaM veda na caiva kashcid ity eva vyAkhyAyeta tadA Ashcaryo j~nAtA kushalAnushiShTaH [KaThU 1.2.7] iti shrutyaika-vAkyatA na syAt | yatatAm api siddhAnAM kash cin mAM vetti tattvataH [GItA 7.3] iti bhagavad-vacana-virodhash ceti vidvadbhir avinayaH kShantavyaH | athavA na caiva kashcid ity asya sarvatra sambandhaH kashcid enaM na pashyati na vadati na shR^iNoti shrutvApi na vedeti pa¤ca prakArA uktAH kashcit pashyaty eva na vadati kashcit pashyati na vadati ca kashcit tad-vacanaM shR^iNoti ca tad-arthaM jAnAti ca kashcic chrutvApi na jAnAti na kashcit tu sarva-bahirbhUta iti | avidvat-pakShe tu asambhAvanA-viparIta-bhAvanAbhibhUtatvAd Ashcarya-tulyatvaM darshana-vadana-shravaNeShv iti nigada-vyAkhyAtaH shlokaH | caturtha-pAde tu dR^iShTvoktvA shrutvApIti yojanA ||29||

vishvanAthaH : nanu kim idam AshcaryaM brUShe | kiM caitad apy Ashcaryam | yad eva prabodhyamAnasyApy aviveko nApayAtIti tatra satyam evem eva ity Aha Ashcaryavad iti | enam AtmAnaM dehaM ca tad-ubhaya-rUpaM sarva-lokam ||29||

baladevaH : nanu sarvaj~nena tvayA bahUpadishyamAno 'py ahaM shoka-nivArakam Atma-yAthAtmyaM na budhye kim etad iti cet tatrAha Ashcaryavad iti | vij~nAnAndobhaya-svarUpatve 'pi tad-bhedApratiyoginaM vij~nAna-svarUpatve 'pi vij~nAtR^itayA santaM paramANutve 'pi vyApta-bR^ihat-kAyaM nAnA-kAya-sambandhe 'pi tat-tad-vikArair aspR^iShTam evam Adi bahu-viruddha-dharmatayAshcaryavad adbhuta-sAdR^ishyena sthitam enaM mad-upadiShTaM jIvaM kashcid eva svadharmAnuShThAnena satya-tapo-japAdinA ca vimR^iShTa-hR^id-guru-prasAda-labdha-tAdR^isha-j~nAnaH pashyati yAthAtmyenAnubhavati | Ashcaryavad iti kriyA-visheShaNaM vA kartR^i-visheShaNaM veti vyAkhyAtAraH kashcid enam yat pashyati tad Ashcaryavat | yaH kashcit pashyati so 'py Ashcaryavad ity arthaH | evam agre 'pi | shrutvApy enam iti kashcit samyag amR^iShTa-hR^id ity arthaH | tathA ca duradhigamaM jIvAtmayAthAtmyam | shrutir apy evam Aha -

shravaNAyApi bahubhir yo na labhyaH
shR^iNvanto 'pi bahavo yaM na vidyuH |
Ashcaryo vaktA kushalo 'sya labdhA 
Ashcaryo j~nAtA kushalAnushiShTa || [KaThU 1.2.7] iti ||29||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.30

dehI nityam avadhyo 'yaM dehe sarvasya bhArata |
tasmAt sarvANi bhUtAni na tvaM shocitum arhasi ||30||

shrIdharaH : tad evam avadhyatvam AtmanaH saN^kShepenopadishan ashocyatvam upasaMharati dehIty Adi | spaShTo 'rthaH ||30||

madhusUdanaH : idAnIM sarva-prANi-sAdhAraNa-bhrama-nivR^itti-sAdhanam uktam upasaMharati dehIti | sarvasya prANi-jAtasya dehe vadhyamAne 'py ayaM dehI liN^ga-dehopAdhir AtmA vadhyo na bhavatIti nityaM niyataM yasmAt tasmAt sarvANi bhUtAni sthUlAni sUkShmANi ca bhIShmAdi-bhAvApannAny uddishya tvaM na shocitum arhasi | sthUla-dehasyAshocyatvam aparihAryatvAt | liN^ga-dehasyAshocyatvam Atmavad evAvadhyatvAd iti na sthUla-dehasya liN^ga-dehasyAtmano vA shocyatvaM yuktam iti bhAvaH ||30||

vishvanAthaH : tarhi nishcitya brUhi kim ahaM kuryAM kiM vA na kuryAm iti | tatra shokaM mA kuru yuddhaM tu kurv ity Aha dehIti dvAbhyAm ||30||

baladevaH : tad evaM duradhigamaM jIva-yAthAtmyaM samAsenopadishann ashocyatvam upasaMharati dehIti | sarvasya jIva-gaNasya dehe hanyamAne 'py ayaM dehI jIvo nityam avadhyo yasmAt tasmAt tvaM sarvANi bhUtAni bhIShmAdi-bhAvApannAni shocituM nArhasi | AtmanAM nityatvAd ashocyatvaM tad-dehAnAM tv avashya-vinAshatvAt tattvam ity arthaH ||30||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.31

sva-dharmam api cAvekShya na vikampitum arhasi |
dharmyAd dhi yuddhAc chreyo 'nyat kShatriyasya na vidyate ||31||

shrIdharaH : yac coktam arjunena vepathush ca sharIre me ity Adi tad apy ayuktam ity Aha svadharmam apIti | Atmano nAshAbhAvAd eva etesAM hanane 'pi vikampituM nArhasi | kiM ca svadharmam apy avekShya vikampitum nArhasi iti sambandhaH | yac coktaM - na ca shreyo 'nupashyAmi hatvA svajanam Ahava iti tatrAha dharmyAd iti | dharmAd anapetAn nyAyAd yuddhAd anyat ||31||

madhusUdanaH : tad evaM sthUla-sUkShma-sharIra-dvaya-tat-kAraNAvidyAkhyopAdhi-trayAvivekena mithyAbhUtasyApi saMsArasya satyatvAtma-dharmatvAdi-pratibhAsa-rUpaM sarva-prANi-sAdhAraNam arjunasya bhramaM nirAkartum upAdhi-traya-vivekenAtma-svarUpam abhihitavAn | samprati yuddhAkhye sva-dharme hiMsAdi-bAhulyenAdharmatva-pratibhAsa-rUpam arjunasyaiva karuNAdi-doSha-nibandhanam asAdhAraNaM bhramaM nirAkartuM hiMsAdimattve 'pi yuddhasya sva-dharmatvenAdharmatvAbhAvaM bodhayati bhagavAn svadharmam apIti |

na kevalaM paramArtha-tattvam evAvekShya kiM tu svadharmam api kShatriya-dharmam api yuddhAparAÇmukhatva-rUpam avekShya shAstrataH paryAlocya vikampituM vicalituM dharmAd adharmatva-bhrAntyA nivartituM nArhasi | tatraivaM sati yadyapy ete na pashyanti ity AdinA narake niyataM vAso bhavati ity antena yuddhasya pApa-hetutvaM tvayA yad uktaM kathaM bhIShmam ahaM saN^khye ity AdinA ca guru-vadha-brahma-vadhAdy-akaraNaM yad abhihitaM tat sarvaM dharma-shAstra-paryAlocanAd evoktam | kasmAt ? hi yasmAd dharmyAd aparAÇmukhatva-dharmAd anapetAd yuddhAd anyat kShatriyasya shreyaH shreyaH-sAdhanaM na vidyate | yuddham eva hi pR^ithivI-jaya-dvAreNa prajA-rakShaNa-brAhmaNa-shushrUShAdi-kShAtra-dharma-nirvAhakam iti tad eva kShatriyasya prashastataram ity abhiprAyaH | tathA coktaM parAshareNa -

kShatriyo hi prajA rakShan shastra-pANiH pradaNDayan |
nirjitya para-sainyAdi kShitiM dharmeNa pAlayet || [ParAshara-smR^iti 1.58] iti ||31||

manunApi -

samottamAdhamai rAjA tv AhUtaH pAlayan prajAH |
na nivarteta saMgrAmAt kShAtraM dharmam anusmaran ||
saMgrAmeShv anivartitvaM prajAnAM caiva pAlanam |
shushrUShA brAhmaNAnAM ca rAj~nAM shreyaskaraM param || [Manu 7.88-9] ity AdinA |

rAja-shabdash ca kShatriya-jAti-mAtra-vAcIti sthitam eveShThy-adhikaraNe | tena bhUmi-pAlasyaivAyaM dharma iti na bhramitavyam | udAhR^ita-vacane 'pi kShatriyo hIti kShAttraM dharmam iti ca spaShTaM liN^gam | tasmAt kShatriyasya yuddhaM prashasto dharma iti sAdhu bhagavato 'bhihitam | apashavo 'nye go-ashvebhyaH pashavo go-ashvAH itivat prashaMsA-lakShaNayA yuddhAd anyac-chreyaH-sAdhanaM na vidyata ity uktam iti na doShaH | etena yuddhAt prashastataraM kiMcid anuShThAtuM tato nivR^ittir uciteti nirastam | na ca shreyo 'nupashyAmi hatvA svajanam Ahave ity etad api ||31||

vishvanAthaH : Atmano nAshAbhAvAd eva vadhAd vikampituM bhetuM nArhasi | svadharmam api cAvekShya na vikampitum arhasIti sambandhaH ||31||

baladevaH : evaM paramAtma-j~nAnopayogitvAd Adau jIvAtma-j~nAnaM sarvAn prati taulyenopadishya sa-niShThAn prati niShkAmatayAnuShThitAni karmANi hR^id-vishuddhi-sahakR^itAm Atma-j~nAna-niShThAM niShpAdayantIti vadiShyan tasyAM pratItim utpAdayituM sakAmatayAnuShThitAnAM karmaNAM kAmya-phala-pradatvam Aha dvAbhyAm svadharmam apIti | 

yuddhaM khalu kShatriyasya nityatam agnihotrAdivad vihitam | tac ca shatru-prANa-vihaMsana-rUpam agniShTomAdi-pashu-hiMsanavan na pratyavAya-nimittam | ubhayatra hiMseyam upakR^iti-rUpaiva | hInayor deha-lokayos tyAgena divyayos tayor lobhAt | Aha caivaM smR^itiH -

AhaveShu mitho 'nyonyaM jighAMsanto mahIkShitaH | 
yudhyamAnAH paraM shaktyA svargaM yAnty aparAÇmukhAH || [Manu 7.90]
yaj~neShu pashavo brahman hanyante satataM dvijaiH |
saMskR^itAH kila mantraish ca te 'pi svargam avApnuvan || [?] ity AdyA | 

evaM nija-dharmam avekShya vikampituM dharmAt pracalituM nArhasi | yuktaM na ca shreyo 'nupashyAmIty AdinA narake nityataM vAso bhavatIyt antyena yuddhasya pApa-hetutvaM tvayoktam | tac cAj~nAnAd evety Aha dharmyAd iti | yuddham eva bhUmi-jaya-dvArA prajA-pAlana-guru-vipra-saMsevanAdi-kShAtra-dharma-nirvAhIti | evam Aha bhagavAn parAsharaH -

kShatriyo hi prajA rakShan shastra-pANiH pradaNDayan |
nirjitya para-sainyAdi kShitiM dharmeNa pAlayet || [ParAshara-smR^iti 1.58] iti ||31||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.32

yadR^icchayA copapannaM svarga-dvAram apAvR^itam |
sukhinaH kShatriyAH pArtha labhante yuddham IdR^isham ||32||

shrIdharaH : kiM ca mahati shreyasi svayam evopAgate sati kuto vikampasa iti | ata Aha yadR^icchayeti | yadR^icchayA aprArthitam eva upapannaM prAptam IdR^ishaM yuddham labhante | yato nirAvaraNaM svarga-dvAram evaitat | yad vA ya evaMvidhaM yuddhaM labhante ta eva sukhina ity arthaH | etena svajanaM hi kathaM hatvA sukhinaH syAma mAdhava iti yad uktaM tan nirastaM bhavati ||32||

madhusUdanaH : nanu yuddhasya kartavyatve 'pi na bhIShma-droNAdibhir gurubhiH saha tat kartum ucitam atigarhitatvAd ity AshaN^kyAha yadR^icchayeti | yadR^icchayA sva-prayatna-vyatirekeNa | co 'vadhAraNe | aprArthanayaivopasthitam IdR^ishaM bhIShma-droNAdi-vIra-puruSha-pratiyogikaM kIrti-rAjya-lAbha-dR^iShTa-phala-sAdhanaM yuddhaM ye kShatriyAH pratiyogitvena labhante te sukhinaH sukha-bhAja eva | jaye satyenAyAsenaiva yashaso rAjyasya ca lAbhAt | parAjaye cAtishIghram eva svargasya lAbhAd ity Aha svarga-dvAram apAvR^itam iti | apratibaddhaM svarga-sAdhanaM yuddham avyavadhAnenaiva svarga-janakaM jyotiShThomAdikaM tu ciratareNa deha-pAtasya pratibandhAbhAvasya cApekShaNAd ity arthaH | svarga-dvAram ity anena shyenAdivat pratyavAya-shaN^kA parihR^itA | shyenAdayo hi vihitA api phala-doSheNa duShTAH | tat-phalasya shatru-vadhasya na hiMsyAt sarvA bhUtAni, brAhmaNaM na hanyAt ity Adi-shAstra-niShiddhasya pratyavAya-janakatvAt phale vidhy-abhAvAc ca na vidhi-spR^iShTe niShedhAnavakAshaH iti nyAyAvatAraH | yuddhasya hi phalaM svargaH sa ca na niShiddhaH | tathA ca manuH --

     AhaveShu mitho 'nyonyaM jighAMsanto mahIkShitaH |
     yudhyamAnAH paraM shaktyA svargaM yAnty aparAÇmukhAH || [Manu 7.90] iti |

yuddhaM tu agnIShomIyAdy-Alambha-vadha-vihitatvAn na niShedhena spraShTuM shakyate ShoDashi-grahaNAdivat | grahaNAgrahayos tulya-balatayA vikalpavat sAmAnya-shAstrasya visheSha-shAstreNa saN^koca-sambhavAt | tathA ca vidhi-spR^iShTe niShedhAnavakAshaH iti nyAyAd yuddhaM na pratyavAya-janakaM nApi bhIShma-droNAdi-guru-brAhmaNAdi-vadha-nimitto doShaH | teShAm AtatAyitvAt | tad uktaM manunA -

guruM vA bAla-vR^iddhau vA brAhmaNaM vA bahu-shrutam |
AtatAyinam AyAntaM hanyAd evAvicArayan ||
AtatAyinam AyAntam api vedAnta-pAragam |
jighAMsantaM jighAMsIyAn na tena brahmahA bhavet ||
nAtatAyi-vadho doSho hantur bhavati kashcana || [Manu 8.350-351] ity Adi |

nanu -
smR^ityor virodhe nyAyas tu balavAn vyavahArataH |
artha-shAstrAt tu balavad dharma-shAstram iti sthitiH || [YAj~navalkya 2.21] 

iti yAj~navalkya-vacanAd AtatAyi-brAhmaNa-vadhe 'pi pratyavAyo 'sty eva | brAhmaNaM na hanyAt iti hi dR^iShTa-prayojanAnapekShatvAd dharma-shAstraM, jighAMsantaM jighAMsIyAn na tena brahmahA bhavet iti ca sva-jIvanArthatvAd artha-shAstram |

atrocyate brahmaNe brAhmaNam Alabheta itivad yuddha-vidhAyakam api dharma-shAstram eva sukha-duHkhe same kR^itvA ity atra dR^iShTa-prayojanAnapekShatvasya vakShyamANatvAt | yAj~navalkya-vacanaM tu dR^iShTa-prayojanoddeshyaka-kUTa-yuddhAdi-kR^ita-vadha-viShayam ity adoShaH | mitAkSharAkAras tu dharmArtha-sannipAte 'rtha-grAhiNa etad eveti dvAdasha-vArShika-prAyashcittasyaitac-chabda-parAmR^iShTasyApastambena vidhAnAn mitra-labdhyAdy-artha-shAstrAnusAreNa catuShpAd vyavahAre shatror api jaye dharma-shAstrAtikramo na kartavya ity etat paraM vacanam etad ity Aha | bhavatv evaM na no hAniH | tad evaM yuddha-karaNe sukhokteH svajanaM hi kathaM hatvA sukhinaH syAma mAdhava ity arjunoktam apAkR^itam ||32||

vishvanAthaH : kiM ca, jetR^ibhyaH sakAshAd api nyAya-yuddhe mR^itAnAm adhikaM sukham ato bhIShmAdIn hatvA tAn pratyuta svato 'pi adhika-sukhinaH kuru ity Aha yadR^icchayeti | svarga-sAdhanaM karma-yogam akR^itvApIty arthaH | apAvR^itam apagatAvaraNam ||32||

baladevaH : kiM cAyatnAd Agate 'smin mahati shreyasi na yuktas te kampa ity Aha yadR^icchayeti | co 'vadhAraNe | yatnaM vinaiva copapannam IdR^ishaM bhIShmAdibhir mahA-vIraiH saha yuddhaM sukhinaH sabhAgyAH kShatriyA labhante | vijaye satya-shrameNa kIrti-rAjyayor mR^ityau sati shIghram eva svargasya ca prApter ity arthaH | etad vya¤jayan vishinaShTi - svarga-dvAram upAvR^itam iti | apratiruddha-svarga-sAdhanam ity arthaH | jyotiShTomAdikaM ciratareNa svargopalambhakam iti tato 'syAtishayaH ||32||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.33

atha cet tvam imaM dharmyaM saMgrAmaM na kariShyasi |
tataH sva-dharmaM kIrtiM ca hitvA pApam avApsyasi ||33||

shrIdharaH : viparyaye doSham Aha atha ced iti ||33||

madhusUdanaH : nanu nAhaM yuddha-phala-kAmaH | na kAN^kShe vijayaM kR^iShNa, api trailokya-rAjyasya ity uktatvAt tat kathaM mayA kartavyam ity AshaN^kyAkaraNe doSham Aha atha ced iti | atheti pakShAntare | imaM bhIShma-droNAdi-vIra-puruSha-pratiyogikaM dharmyaM hiMsAdi-doShaNAduShTaM satAM dharmAd anapetAm iti vA | sa ca manunA darshitaH -

na kUTair Ayudhair hanyAd yudhyamAno raNe ripUn |
na karNibhir nApi digdhair nAgni-jvalita-tejanaiH ||
na ca hanyAt sthalArUDhaM na klIbaM na kR^itA¤jalim |
na mukta-keshaM nAsInaM na tavAsmIti vAdinam ||
na suptaM na visaMnAhaM na nagnaM na nirAyudham |
nAyudhyamAnaM pashyantaM na pareNa samAgatam ||
nAyudha-vyasana-prAptaM nArtaM nAtiparikShataM |
na bhItaM na parAvR^ittaM satAM dharmam anusmaran || [Manu 7.91-94] iti |

satAM dharmam ullaN^ghya yudhyamAno hi pApIyAn syAt | tvaM tu parair AhUto 'pi sad-dharmopetam api saN^grAmaM yuddhaM na kariShyasi dharmato lokato vA bhItaH parAvR^itto bhaviShyasi cet tato nirjitya para-sainyAni kShitiM dharmeNa pAlayet [ParAshara-smR^iti 1.58] ity Adi-shAstra-vihitasya yuddhasyAkaraNAt svadharmaM hitvAnanuShThAya kIrtiM ca mahAdevAdi-samAgama-nimittAM hitvA na nivarteta saN^grAmAt ity Adi-shAstra-niShiddha-saN^grAma-nivR^ittyA ca raNa-janyaM pApam eva kevalam avApsyasi na tu dharmaM kIrtiM cety abhiprAyaH | 

athavA 'neka-janmArjitaM dharmaM tyaktvA rAja-kR^itaM pApam evAvApsyasIty arthaH | yasmAt tvAM parAvR^ittam ete duShTA avashyaM haniShyanti ataH parAvR^itta-hataH saMsh ciropArjita-nija-sukR^ita-parityAgena paropArjita-duShkR^ita-mAtra-bhAÇ mA bhUr ity abhiprAyaH | tathA ca manuH -

yas tu bhItaH parAvR^ittaH saN^grAme hanyate paraiH |
bhartur yad duShkR^itaM kiMcit tat sarvaM pratipadyate ||
yac cAsya sukR^itaM kiMcid amutrArtham upArjitam |
bhartA tat sarvam Adatte parAvR^itta-hatasya tu || [Manu 7.95-96] iti |

yAj~navalkyo 'pi rAjA sukR^itam Adatte hatAnAM vipalAyinAm iti | tena yad uktam - pApam evAshrayed asmAn hatvaitAn AtatAyinaH [GItA 1.36], etAn na hantum icchAmi ghanto 'pi madhusUdana [GItA 1.35] iti tan nirAkR^itaM bhavati ||33||

vishvanAthaH : vipakShe doSham Aha atheti caturbhiH ||33||

baladevaH : vipakShe doShAn darshayati athety AdibhiH | svasya tava dharmyaM yuddha-lakShaNaM kIrtiM ca rudra-santoShaNa-nivAta-kavacAdi-vadha-labdhAM hitvA pApaM na nivarteta saN^grAmAd ity Adi smR^iti-pratiShiddhaM sva-dharma-tyAga-lakShaNaM prApsyasi ||33||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.34

akIrtiM cApi bhUtAni kathayiShyanti te 'vyayAm |
saMbhAvitasya cAkIrtir maraNAd atiricyate ||34||

shrIdharaH : kiM ca akIrtim ity Adi | avyayAm shAshvatIm | saMbhAvitasya bahu-matasya | atiricyate adhikatarA bhavati ||34||

madhusUdanaH : evaM kIrti-dharmayor iShTayor aprAptir aniShTasya ca pApasya prAptir yuddha-parityAge darshitA | tatra pApAkhyam aniShTaM vyavadhAnena duHkha-phaladam AmutrikatvAt | shiShTa-garhA-lakShaNaM tv aniShTam Asanna-phaladam atyasahyam ity Aha akIrtim iti | bhUtAni devarShi-manuShyAdIni te tavAvyayAM dIrgha-kAlam akIrtiM na dharmAtmAyaM na shUro 'yam ity evaM-rUpAM kathayiShyanty anyonyaM kathA-prasaN^ge | kIrti-dharma-nAsha-samuccayArthau nipAtau | na kevalaM kIrti-dharmau hitvA pApaM prApsyasi api tu akIrtiM ca prApsyasi | na kevalaM tvam eva tAM prApsyasi api tu bhUtAny api kathayiShyantIti vA nipAtayor arthaH | 

nanu yuddhe sva-maraNa-sandehAt tat-parihArArtham akIrtir api soDhavyA Atma-rakShaNasyAtyantApekShitatvAt | tathA coktaM shAnti-parvaNi[*ENDNOTE] --

sAmnA dAnena bhedena samastair atha vA pR^ithak |
vijetuM prayatetArIn na yuddhena kadA cana || 
anityo vijayo yasmAd dR^ishyate yudhyamAnayoH |
parAjayash ca saMgrAme tasmAd yuddhaM vivarjayet ||
trayANAm apy upAyAnAM pUrvoktAnAm asaMbhave |
tathA yudhyeta saMpanno vijayeta ripUn yathA || [ManuS 7.198-200]

evam eva manunApy uktam |

tathA ca maraNa-bhItasya kim akIrti-duHkham iti shaN^kAm apanudati sambhAvitasya dharmAtmA shUra ity evam Adibhir ananya-labhyair guNair bahumatasya janasyAkIrtir maraNAd apy atiricyate 'dhikA bhavati | co hetau | evaM yasmAd ato 'kIrter maraNam eva varaM nyUnatvAt | tvam apy atirsambhAvito 'si mahAdevAdi-samAgamena | ato nAkIrti-duHkhaM soDhuM shakShyasIty abhiprAyaH | udAhR^ita-vacanaM tv artha-shAstratvAt na nivarteta saN^grAmAt [Manu 7.88] ity Adi-dharma-shAstrAd durbalam iti bhAvaH ||34||

vishvanAthaH : avyayAm anashvarAm | saMbhAvitasyAtipratiShThitasya ||34||

baladevaH : na kevalaM svadharmasya kIrtesh ca kShati-mAtram | yuddhe samArabdhe 'rjunaH palAyata ity avyayAM shAshvatIm akIrtiM ca tava bhUtAni sarve lokAH kathayiShyanti | nanu maraNAd bhItena mayA akIrtiH soDhavyeti cet tatrAha sambhAvitasyAtipratiShThitasya | atiricyate adhikA bhavati | tathA ca tAdR^ishAkIR^iter maraNam eva varam iti ||34||

bhayAd raNAd uparataM maMsyante tvAM mahArathAH |
yeShAM ca tvaM bahumato bhUtvA yAsyasi lAghavam ||35||

shrIdharaH : kiM ca bhayAd iti | yeShAM bahu-guNatvena tvaM pUrvaM sammato 'bhUs ta eva bhayAt saMgrAmAn nivR^ittaM tvAM manyeran | tatash ca pUrvaM bahumato bhUtvA lAghavam laghutAM yAsyasi ||35||

madhusUdanaH :

vishvanAthaH : yeShAM tvaM bahu-mato 'smac-chatrur arjunas tu mahAshUra iti bahu-saMmAna-viShayo bhUtvA samprati yuddhAd uparame sati lAghavaM yAsyasi te duryodhanAdayo mahArathAs tvAM bhayAd eva raNAd uparataM maMsyanta ity anvayaH | kShatriyANAM hi bhayaM vinA yuddhoparati-hetur bandhu-snehAdiko nopapadyata iti matveti bhAvaH ||35||

baladevaH : nanu kula-kShaya-doShAt kAruNyAc ca vinivR^ittasya mama katham akIrtiH syAd iti cet tatrAha bhayAd iti | mahArathA duryodhanAdayas tvAM karNAdi-bhayAn na tu bandhu-kAruNyAd raNAd uparataM maMsyante | na hi shUrasya shatru-bhayaM vinA bandhu-snehena yuddhAd uparatir ity arthaH | itaH pUrvaM yeShAM tvaM bahumataH shUro vairIti bahu-guNavattayA saMmato 'bhUr idAnIM yuddhe samupasthite kAtaro 'yaM vinivR^itta ity evaM tat-kR^itaM lAghavaM duHsahaM yAsyasi ||35||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.36

avAcya-vAdAMsh ca bahUn vadiShyanti tavAhitAH |
nindantas tava sAmarthyaM tato duHkhataraM nu kim ||36||

shrIdharaH : kiM ca avAcya-vAdAn iti | avAcyAn vAdAn vacanAnarhAn shabdAn tava ahitAH tvac-chatravo vadiShyanti ||36||

madhusUdanaH : nanu bhIShmAdayo mahArathA na bahu manyantAM duryodhanAdayas tu shatravo bahu maMsyante mAM yuddha-nivR^ittyA tad-upakAritvAd ity ata Aha avAcyeti | tavAsAdhAraNaM yat sAmarthyaM loka-prasiddhaM tan nindantas tava shatravo duryodhanAdayo 'vAcyAn vAdAn vacanAn arhAn ShaNDha-tilAdi-rUpAn eva shabdAn bahUn aneka-prakArAn vadiShyanti na tu bahu maMsyanta ity abhiprAyaH | athavA tava sAmarthyaM stuti-yogyatvaM tava nindanto 'hitA avAcya-vAdAn vadiShyantIty anvayaH | 

nanu bhIShma-droNAdi-vadha-prayuktaM kaShTataraM duHkham asahamAno yuddhAn nivR^ittaH shatru-kR^ita-sAmarthya-nindanAdi-duHkhaM soDhuM shakShyAmIty ata Aha tatas tasmAn nindA-prApti-duHkhAt kiM tu duHkhataraM tato 'dhikaM kim api duHkhaM nAstIty arthaH ||36|| 

vishvanAthaH : avAcya-vAdAn | klIba ity Adi kaTUktIH ||36||

baladevaH : kiM cAvAcyeti | ahitAH shatravo dhArtarAShTrAs tava sAmarthyaM pUrva-siddhaM parAkramaM nindantaH bahUn avAcya-vAdAn shaNDhatilAdi-shabdAn vadiShyanti | tata evaMvidhAvAcya-vAda-shravaNAd atishAyitaM kiM duHkham asti | itthaM caite ShaDbhir yuddha-vairAgyasyAsvargatvam akIrti-karatvaM coktaM darshitam ||36||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.37

hato vA prApsyasi svargaM jitvA vA bhokShyase mahIm |
tasmAd uttiShTha kaunteya yuddhAya kR^ita-nishcayaH ||37||

shrIdharaH : yad uktaM na caitad vidmaH [GItA 2.6] iti tatrAha hato vety Adi | pakSha-dvaye 'pi tava lAbha evety arthaH ||37||

madhusUdanaH : nanu tarhi yuddhe gurv-Adi-vadha-vashAn madhyastha-kR^itA nindA tato nivR^ittau tu shatru-kR^itA nindety ubhayataH pAshA rajjur ity AshaN^kya jaye parAjaye ca lAbha-dhrauvyAd yuddhArtham evotthAnam Avashyakam ity Aha hato veti | spaShTaM pUrvArdham | yasmAd ubhayathApi te lAbhas tasmAj jeShyAmi shatrUn mariShyAmi veti kR^ita-nishcayaH san yuddhAyottiShTha | nayatara-phala-sandehe 'pi yuddha-kartavyatAyA nishcitatvAt | etena na caitad vidmaH kataran no garIyaH [GItA 2.6] ity Adi parihR^itam ||37||

vishvanAthaH : nanu yuddhe mama jaya eva bhAvIty api nAsti nishcayaH | tatash ca kathaM yuddhe pravartitavyam ity ata Aha hata iti ||37||

baladevaH : nanu yuddhe vijaya eva me syAd iti nishcayAbhAvAt tato 'haM nivR^itto 'smIti cet tatrAha hato veti | pakSha-dvaye 'pi te lAbha eveti bhAvaH ||37||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.38

sukha-duHkhe same kR^itvA lAbhAlAbhau jayAjayau |
tato yuddhAya yujyasva naivaM pApam avApsyasi ||38||

shrIdharaH : yad apy uktaM pApam evAshrayed asmAn [GItA 1.36] iti tatrAha sukha-duHkhe ity Adi | sukha-duHkhe same kR^itvA | tathA tayoH kAraNa-bhUtau lAbhAlAbhAv api | tayor api kAraNa-bhUtAu jayAjayAv api samau kR^itvA | eteShAM samatve kAraNaM harSha-viShAda-rAhityam | yujyasva sannadho bhava | sukhAdy-abhilAsaM hitvA svadharma-buddhyA yudhyamAnaH pApaM na prApsyasIty arthaH ||38||

madhusUdanaH : nanv evaM svargam uddishya yuddha-karaNe tasya nityatva-vyAghAtaH | rAjyam uddishya yuddha-karaNe tv artha-shAstratvAd dharma-shAstrApekShayA daurbalyaM syAt | tatash ca kAmyasyAkaraNe kutaH pApaM dR^iShTArthasya guru-brAhmaNAdi-vadhasya kuto dharmatvaM, tathA cAtha ced iti shlokArtho vyAhata iti cet tatrAha sukha-duHkhe iti | 

samatA-karaNaM rAga-dveSha-rAhityam | sukhe tat-kAraNe lAbhe tat-kAraNe lAbhe tat-kAraNe jaye ca rAgam akR^itvA, evaM duHkhe tad-dhetAv alAbhe tad-dhetAv ajaye ca dveSham akR^itvA tato yuddhAya yujyasva sannadhau bhava | evaM sukha-kAmanAM duHkha-nivR^itti-kAmanAM vA vihAya svadharma-buddhyA yudhyamAno guru-brAhmaNAdi-vadha-nimittaM nitya-karmAkaraNa-nimittaM ca pApaM na prApsyasi | yas tu phala-kAmanayA karoti sa guru-brAhmaNAdi-vadha-nimittaM pApaM prApnoti yo vA na karoti sa nitya-karmAkaraNa-nimittam | ataH phala-kAmanAm antareNa kurvann ubhaya-vidham api pApaM na prApnotIti prAg eva vyAkhyAto 'bhiprAyaH | hato vA prApsyasi svargaM jitvA vA bhokShyase mahIm [GItA 2.37] iti svAnuShaN^gika-phala-kathanam iti na doShaH | tathA ca ApastambaH smarati - tad yathAmre phalArthe nimitte chAyA-gandhAvanUtpadyete evaM dharmaM caryamANam arthA anUtpadyante no ced anUtpadyante na dharma-hAnir bhavati iti | ato yuddha-shAstrasyArtha-shAstratvAbhAvAt pApam evAshrayed asmAn [GItA 1.36] ity Adi nirAkR^itaM bhavati ||38||

vishvanAthaH : tasmAt tava sarvathA yuddham eva dharmas tad api yad imaM pApa-kAraNam AshaN^kase, tarhi mattaH pApAnutpatti-prakAraM shikShitvA yudhyasvety Aha sukha-duHkhe same kR^itvA | tad-dhetur lAbhAlAbhau rAjya-lAbha-rAja-cyUtI api | tad-dhetur jayAjayAv api samau kR^itvA vivekena tulyau vibhAvety arthaH | tatash caivaM-bhUta-sAmya-lakShaNe j~nAnavatas tava pApaM naiva bhavet | yad vakShyate lipyate na sa pApena padma-patram ivAmbhasA [GItA 5.10] iti ||38||

baladevaH : nanu atha cet tvam ity Adi-padyArtho vyAhR^itaH | rAjyAdy-uddeshena kR^itasya yuddhasya guru-viprAdi-vinAsha-hetutvena pApotpAdakatvAd iti cen mumukShu-vartmanA yuddhamAnasya tava tad-vinAsha-hetukaM pApaM na syAd ity Aha sukheti | sAmya-karaNam iha tatra tatra nirvikAratvaM bodhyam | sukhe tad-dhetau jaye ca rAgam akR^itvA duHkhe tad-dhetAv alAbhe tad-dhetau parAjaye ca dveSham akR^itvA tatra tatra nirvikAra-cittaH san tato yuddhAya yujyasva | kevala-svadharma-dhiyA yoddhum udyukto bhavety arthaH | evaM mumukShu-rItyA yoddhA tvaM pApaM tad-vinAsha-hetukaM nAvApsyasi | phalecchuH san yo yudhyate sa tat-pApaM vindati | vij~nAnArthI tu purAtanam ananta-pApam apanudatIty arthaH | 

nanu phala-rAgaM vinA duShkare yuddha-dAnAdau kathaM pravR^ittir iti ced anantAtmAnanda-rAgaM tatra pravartakaM gR^ihANa rAjyAdy-anurAgam iva bhR^igu-pAte ||38||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.39

eShA te 'bhihitA sAMkhye buddhir yoge tv imAM shR^iNu |
buddhyA yukto yayA pArtha karmabandhaM prahAsyasi ||39||

shrIdharaH : upadiShTaM j~nAna-yogam upasaMharaMs tat-sAdhanaM karma-yogaM prastauti eShety Adi | samyak khyAyate prakAshyate vastu-tattvam anayeti saN^khyA samyak j~nAnam | tasyAM prakAshamAnam Atma-tattvaM sAN^khyam | tasmin karaNIyA buddhir eShA tavAbhihitA | evam abhihitAyAm api tava ced Atma-tattvam aparokShaM na bhavati tarhy antaHkaraNa-shuddhi-dvArA Atma-tattvAparokShArthaM karma-yoga tv imAM buddhiM shR^iNu | yayA buddhyA yuktaH parameshvarArpita-karma-yogena shuddhAntaHkaraNaH san tat-prasAda-labdhAparokSha-j~nAnena karmAtmakaM bandhaM prakarSheNa hAsyasi tyakShyasi ||39||

madhusUdanaH :  nanu bhavatu svadharma-buddhyA yudhyamAnasya pApAbhAvaH, tathApi na mAM prati yuddha-kartavyatopadeshas tavocitaH | ya enaM vetti hantAraM [GItA 2.19] ity AdinA kathaM sa puruShaH pArtha kaM ghAtayati hanti kam [GItA 2.21] ity antena viduShaH sarva-karma-pratikShepAt | na hy akartr-bhoktR^i-shuddha-svarUpo 'ham asmi yuddhaM kR^itvA tat-phalaM bhokShya iti ca j~nAnaM sambhavati virodhAt | j~nAna-karmaNoH samuccayAsambhavAt prakAsha-tamasor iva | ayaM cArjunAbhiprAyo jyAyasI ced ity atra vyakto bhaviShyati | tasmAd ekam eva mAM prati j~nAnasya karmaNash copadesho nopapadyata iti cet, na | vidvad-avidvad-avasthA-bhedena j~nAna-karmopadeshopapatter ity Aha bhagavAn eSheti | 

eShA na tv evAham ity Ady-eka-viMshati-shlokais te tubhyam abhihitA sAN^khye samyak khyAyate sarvopAdhi-shUnyatayA pratipAdyate paramAtma-tattvam anayeti saN^khyopaniShat tayaiva tAparya-parisamAptyA pratipAdyate yaH sa sAN^khya aupaniShadaH puruSha ity arthaH | tasmin buddhis tan-mAtra-viShayaM j~nAnaM sarvAnartha-nivR^itti-kAraNaM tvAM prati mayoktaM naitAdR^isha-j~nAnavataH kvacid api karmocyate | tasya kAryaM na vidyata iti vakShyamANatvAt |
