yadi punar evaM mayokte 'pi tavaiShA buddhir nodeti citta-doShAt, tadA tad-apanayenAtma-tattva-sAkShAtkArAya karma-yoga eva tvayAnuShTheyaH | tasmin yoge karma-yoge tu karaNIyAm imAM sukha-duHkhe same kR^itvA ity atroktAM phalAbhisandhi-tyAga-lakShaNAM buddhiM vistareNa mayA vakShyamANAM shR^iNu | tu-shabdaH pUrva-buddher yoga-viShayatva-vyatireka-sUcanArthaH | tathA ca shuddhAntaH-karaNaM prati j~nAnopadesho 'shuddhAntaH-karaNaM prati karmopadesha iti kutaH samuccaya-shaN^kayA virodhAvakAsha ity abhiprAyaH |

yoga-viShayAM buddhiM phala-kathanena stauti - yathA vyavasAyAtmikayA buddhyA karmasu yuktas tvaM karma-nimittaM bandha-nAshAyAshuddhi-lakShaNaM j~nAna-pratibandhaM prakarSheNa punaH pratibandhAnutpatti-rUpeNa hAsyasi tyakShyasi | ayaM bhAvaH - karma-nimitto j~nAna-pratibandhaH karmaNaiva dharmAkhyenApanetuM shakyate dharmeNa pApam apanudati [MahAnA 13.6] iti shruteH | shravaNAdi-lakShaNo vicAras tu karmAtmaka-pratibandha-rahitasyAsambhAvanAdi-pratibandhaM dR^iShTa-dvAreNApanayatIti na karma-bandha-nirAkaraNAyopadeShTuM shakyate | ato 'tyanta-malinAntaH-karaNatvAd bahir aN^ga-sAdhanaM karmaiva tvayAnuShTheyaM, nAdhunA shravaNAdi-yogyatApi tava jAtA | dUre tu j~nAna-yogyateti | tathA ca vakShyati - karmaNy evAdhikAras te [GItA 2.47] iti | etena sAN^khya-buddher antaraN^ga-sAdhanaM shravaNAdi vihAya bahiraN^ga-sAdhanaM karmaiva bhagavatA kim ity arjunAyopadishyata iti nirastam | karma-bandhaM saMsAram Ishvara-prasAda-nimitta-j~nAna-prAptyA prahAsyasIti prAcAM vyAkhyAne tv adhyAhAra-doShaH karma-pada-vaiyarthyaM ca parihartavyam ||39||

vishvanAthaH : upadiShTaM j~nAna-yogam upasaMharati eSheti | samyak khyAyate prakAshyate vastu-tattvam aneneti sAN^khyaM samyak j~nAnam | tasmin karaNIyA buddhir eSha kathitA | adhunA yoge bhakti-yoge imAM vakShyamANAM buddhiM karaNIyAM shR^iNu, yayA bhakti-viShayiNyA buddhyA yuktaH sahitaH | karma-bandhaM saMsAram ||39|| 

baladevaH : uktaM j~nAna-yogam upasaMharan tad-upAyaM niShkAma-karma-yogaM vaktum Arabhate eSheti | saN^khyopaniShat samyak khyAyate nirUpyate tattvam anayA iti nirukteH | tayA pratipAdyam Atma-yAthAtmyaM sAN^khyam | shaiShikAn tasmin kartavyaiShA buddhis tavAbhihitA | ne tv evAhaM ity AdinA tasmAt sarvANi bhUtAni ity antena | sA cet tava citta-tad-doShAn nAbhyudeti tarhi yoge tam etaM vedAnuvacanena brAhmaNA vividiShanti yaj~nena dAnena tapasA nAshakena ity Adi shruty-uktAntargata-j~nAne niShkAma-karma-yoge kartavyAm imAM vakShyamANAM buddhiM shR^iNu | phaloktyA tAM stauti yayeti | karmANi kurvANas tvaM bhagavad-Aj~nayA mahA-prayAsAni karmANi kurvaMs tat-tad-uddesha-mahimnA tvad-antar-abhyuditayAtma-j~nAna-niShThayA saMsAraM tariShyasIti | pashu-putra-rAjyAdi-phalakaM karma sa-kAmaM j~nAna-phalakaM tu tan-niShkAmam iti shAstre 'smin paribhAShyate ||39||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.40

nehAbhikrama-nAsho 'sti pratyavAyo na vidyate |
svalpam apy asya dharmasya trAyate mahato bhayAt ||40||

shrIdharaH : nanu kR^iShyAdivat karmaNAM kadAcid vighna-bAhulyena phale vyabhicArAt mantrAdy-aN^ga-vaiguNyena ca pratyavAya-sambhavaAt kutaH karma-yogena karma-bandha-prahANam | tatrAha nehety Adi | iha niShkAma-karma-yoge abhikramasya prArambhasya nAsho niShphalatvaM nAsti | pratyavAyash ca na vidyate | Ishvaroddeshenaiva vighna-vaiguNyAdy-asambhavAt | kiM cAsya dharmasya IshvarArAdhanArtha-karma-yogasya svalpam apy upakrama-mAtram api kR^itaM mahato bhayAt saMsAra-lakShaNAt trAyate rakShati | na tu kAmya-karmavat ki¤cid aN^ga-vaikguNyAdinA naiShphalyam asyety arthaH ||40||

madhusUdanaH : nanu tam etaM vedAnuvacanena brAhmaNA vividiShanti yaj~nena dAnena tapasAnAshakena [BAU 4.4.22] iti shrutyA vividiShAM j~nAnaM coddishya saMyoga-pR^ithaktva-nyAyena sarva-karmaNAM viniyogAt tatra cAntaH-karaNa-shuddher dvAratvAn mAM prati karmAnuShThAnaM vidhIyate | tatra tad yatheha karma-jito lokaH kShIyata evam evAmutra puNya-jito lokaH kShIyate [ChA 8.1.6] iti shruti-bodhitasya phala-nAshasya sambhAvAj j~nAnaM vividiShAM coddishya kriyamANasya yaj~nAdeH kAmyatvAt sarvAN^gopasaMhAreNAnuShTheyasya yat kiMcid aN^gAsampattAv api vaiguNyApatter yaj~nenety Adi-vAkya-vihitAnAM ca sarveShAM karmaNAm ekena puruShAyuSha-paryavasAne 'pi kartum ashakyatvAt kutaH karma-bandhaM prahAsyasIti-phalaM pratyAshety ata Aha bhagavAn neheti | 

abhikramyate karmaNA prArabhyate yat phalaM so 'bhikramas tasya nAshas tad yathehety AdinA pratipAdita iha niShkAma-karma-yoge nAsti | etat-phalasya shuddheH pApa-kShaya-rUpatvena loka-shabda-vAcya-bhogyatvAbhAvena ca kShayAsambhavAt | vedana-paryantAyA eva vividiShAyAH karma-phalatvAd vedanasya cAvyavadhAnenAj~nAna-nivR^itti-phala-janakasya phalam ajanayitvA nAshAsambhavAd iha phala-nAsho nAstIti sAdhUktam | tad uktaM -

tad yatheheti yA nindA sA phale na tu karmaNi |
phalecchAM tu parityajya kR^itaM karma vishuddhi-kR^it || iti |

tathA pratyavAyo 'N^ga-vaiguNya-nibandhanaM vaiguNyam iha na vidyate tam iti vAkyena nityAnAm evopAtta-durita-kShaya-dvAreNa vividiShAyAM viniyogAt | tatra ca sarvAN^gopasaMhAra-niyamAbhAvAt | kAmyAnAm api saMyoga-pR^ithaktva-nyAyena  viniyoga iti pakShe 'pi phalAbhisandhi-rahitatvena teShAM nitya-tulyatvAt | nahi kAmya-nityAgnihotrayoH svataH kashcid visheSho 'sti | phalAbhisandhi-tad-abhAShAbhyAm eva tu kAmyatva-nityatva-vyapadeshaH | idaM ca pakSha-dvayam uktaM vArtike -

vedAnuvacanAdInAm aikAtmya-j~nAna-janmane |
tam etam iti vAkyena nityAnAM vakShyate vidhiH ||
yad vA vividiShArthatvaM kAmyAnAm api karmaNAm | 
tam etam iti vAkyena saMyogasya pR^ithaktvataH || iti | 

tathA ca phalAbhisandhinA kriyamANa eva karmaNi sarvAN^gopa-saMhAra-niyamAt tad-vilakShaNe shuddhy-arthe karmaNi pratinidhyAdinA samApti-sambhavAn nAN^ga-vaiguNya-nimittaH pratyavAyo 'stIty arthaH | tathAsya shuddhy-arthasya dharmasya tam etam ity Adi-vAkya-vihitasya madhye svalpam api saN^khyayetikartavyatayA vA yathA-shakti-bhagavad-ArAdhanArthaM kiMcid apy anuShThitaM san mahataH saMsAra-bhayAt trAyate bhagavat-prasAda-sampAdanenAnuShThAtAraM rakShati |

sarva-pApa-prasakto 'pi dhyAyan nimiSham acyutam |
bhUyas tapasvI bhavati paN^ki-pAvana-pAvanaH || ity Adi smR^iteH | 

tam etam iti vAkye samuccaya-vidhAyakAbhAvAc cAshuddhi-tAratamyAd evAnuShThAna-tAratamyopapatter yuktam uktaM karma-bandhaM prahAsyasi ||40||

vishvanAthaH : atra yogo dvividhaH shravaNa-kIrtanAdi-bhakti-rUpaH, shrI-bhagavad-arpita-niShkAma-karma-rUpash ca | tatra karmaNy evAdhikAraH ity ataH prAg bhakti-yoga eva nirUpyate | nistraiguNyo bhavArjuna ity ukter bhakter eve triguNAtItatvAt tayaiva puruSho nistraiguNyo bhavatIty ekAdasha-skandhe[*ENDNOTE] prasiddheH | j~nAna-karmaNos tu sAttvikatva-rAjasatvAbhyAM nistraiguNyatvAnupapatter bhagavad-arpita-lakShaNA bhaktis tu karmaNo vaiphalyAbhAva-mAtraM pratipAdayati, na tu svasya bhakti-vyapadeshaM prAdhAnyAbhAvAd eva | yadi ca bhagavad-arpitaM karmApi bhaktir eveti mataM, tadA karma kiM syAt ? yad-bhagavad-anarpita-karma, tad eva karmeti cen, na | 

naiShkarmyam apy acyuta-bhAva-varjitaM
na shobhate j~nAnam alaM nira¤janam |
kutaH punaH shashvad abhadram Ishvare
na cArpitaM karma yad apy akAraNam || [BhP 1.5.12]

iti nAradoktyA tasya vaiyarthya-pratipAdanAt | tasmAd atra bhagvac-caraNa-mAdhurya-prApti-sAdhanIbhUtA kevala-shravaNa-kIrtanAdi-lakShaNaiva bhaktir nirUpyate, yathA niShkAma-karma-yoga 'pi nirUpayitavyaH | ubhAv apy etau buddhi-yoga-shabda-vAcyau j~neyau - dadAmi buddhi-yogaM taM yena mAm upayAnti te [10.10], dUreNa hy avaraM karma buddhi-yogAd dhana¤jaya [2.49] iti cokteH | 

atha nirguNa-shravaNa-kIrtanAdi-bhakti-yogasya mAhAtmyam Aha neheti | iha bhakti-yoge 'bhikrame Arambha-mAtre kR^ite 'py asya bhaktiyogasya nAsho nAsti | tataH pratyavAyash ca na syAt | yathA karma-yoge ArambhaM kR^itvA karmAnuShThitavataH karma-nAsha-pratyavAyau syAtAm iti bhAvaH |

nanu tarhi tasya bhakty-anuShThAtu-kAmasya samucita-bhakty-akaraNAt bhakti-phalaM tu naiva syAt | tatrAha svalpam iti | asya dharmasya svalpam apy Arambha-samaye yA ki¤cin-mAtrI bhaktir abhUt | sApIty arthaH | mahato bhayAt saMsArAt trAyata eva | yan-nAma sakR^ic-chravaNAt pukkasho 'pi vimucyate saMsArAd ity [BhP 6.16.44] Adi-shravaNAt | ajAmilAdau tathA darshanAc ca | 

na hy aN^gopakrame dhvaMso 
mad-dharmasyoddhavANv api |
mayA vyavasitaH samyaÇ 
nirguNatvAd anAshiShaH || [BhP 11.29.20]

iti bhagavato vAkyena sahAsya-vAkyasyaikArtham eva dR^ishyate | kintu tatra nirguNatvAn na hi guNAtItaM vastu kadAcid dhvastaM bhavatIti hetur upanyastaH | sa cehApi draShTavyaH | na ca niShkAma-karmaNo 'pi bhagavad-arpaNa-mahimnA nirguNatvam eveti vAcyam - mad-arpaNaM niShphalaM vA sAttvikaM nija-karma tat [BhP 11.25.23] ||40||

baladevaH : vakShyamANayA buddhyA yuktaM karma-yogaM stauti neheti | iha tam etam ity Adi vAkyokteH niShkAma-karma-yoge 'bhikramasyArambhasya phalotpAdakatva-nAsho nAsti | ArambhasyAsamAptasya vaiphalyaM na bhavatIty arthaH | mantrAdy-aN^ga-vaikalye ca pratyavAyo na vidyate | Atmoddesha-mahimnA oM tat sat iti bhagavan-nAmnA ca tasya vinAshAt | iha bhagavad-arpitasya niShAma-karma-lakShaNa-dharmasya ki¤cid apy anuShThitaM san mahato bhayAt saMsArAt trAyate anuShThAtAraM rakShati | vakShyati caivaM pArtha naiveha nAmutra [GItA 6.40] ity AdinA | kAmya-karmANi sarvAN^gopasaMhAreNAnuShThitAny ukta-phalAya kalpante | mantrAdy-aN^ga-vaikalye tu pratyavAyaM janayantIti | niShkAma-karmANi tu yathA-shakty-anuShThitAni j~nAna-niShThA-lakShaNaM phalaM janayanty evokta-hetutaH pratyavAyaM noptAdayantIti ||40||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.41

vyavasAyAtmikA buddhir ekeha kuru-nandana |
bahu-shAkhA hy anantAsh ca buddhayo 'vyavasAyinAm ||41||

shrIdharaH : kuta ity apekShAyAm ubhayor vaiShamyam Aha vyavasAyAtmiketi | iha IshvarArAdhana-lakShaNe karma-yoge vyavasAyAtmikA parameshvara-bhaktyaiva dhruvaM tariShyAmIti nishcayAtmikA ekaiva ekaniShThaiva buddhir bhavati | avyavasAyinAM tu IshvarArAdhana-bahirmukhAnAM kAminAM kAmAnAm AnantyAt anantAH | tatrApi hi karma-phala-guNa-phalatvAdi-prakAra-bhedAd bahu-shAkhAsh ca buddhayo bhavanti | IshvarArAdhanArthaM hi nityaM naimittikaM ca karma ki¤cid aN^ga-vaiguNye 'pi na nashyati | yathA shaknuyAt tathA kuryAd iti hi tad vidhIyate | na ca vaiguNyam api | Ishvaroddeshenaiva vaiguNyopashamAt | na tu tathA kAmyaM karma | ato mahad vaiShamyam iti bhAvaH ||41||

madhusUdanaH : etad-upapAdanAya tam etam iti vAkya-vihitAnAm ekArthatvam Aha vyavasAyAtmiketi | he kurunandaneha shreyo-mArge tam etam iti vAkye vA vyavasAyAtmikAtma-tattva-nishcayAtmikA buddhir ekaiva caturNAm AshramANAM sAdhyA vivakShitA vedAnuvacanena ity Adau tR^itIyA-vibhaktyA pratyekaM nirapekSha-sAdhanatva-bodhanAt | bhinnArthatve hi samuccayaH syAt | ekArthatve 'pi darsha-pUrNamAsAbhyAm itivad dvandva-samAsena yad agnaye ca prajApataye cetivac ca-shabdena na tathAtra kiMcit pramANam astIty arthaH | sAN^khya-viShayA  yoga-viShayA ca buddhir eka-phalatvAd ekA vyavasAyAtmikA sarva-viparIta-buddhInAM bAdhikA nirdoSha-veda-vAkya-samutthatvAd itarAs tv avyavasAyinAM buddhayo bAdhyA ity artha iti bhAShya-kR^itaH | anye tu parameshvarArAdhanenaiva saMsAraM tariShyAmIti nishcayAtmikaika-niShThaiva buddhir iha karma-yoge bhavatIty artham AhuH | sarvathApi tu j~nAna-kANDAnusAreNa svalpam apy asya dharmasya trAyate mahato bhayAt ity upapannam | karma-kANDe punar bahu-shAkhA aneka-bhedAH kAmAnAm aneka-bhedatvAt | anantAsh ca karma-phala-guNa-phalAdi-prakAropashAkhA-bhedAt, buddhayo bhavanty avyavasAyinAM tat-tat-phala-kAmAnAm | buddhInAm Anantya-prasiddhi-dyotanArtho hi-shabdaH | ataH kAmya-karmApekShayA mahad-vailakShaNya-shuddhy-artha-karmaNAm ity abhiprAyaH ||41||

vishvanAthaH : kiM ca sarvAbhyo 'pi buddhibhyo bhakti-yoga-viShayiNy eva buddhir uktR^iShTety Aha vyavasAyeti | iha bhakti-yoge vyavasAyAtmikA buddhir ekaiva | mama shrImad-gurUpadiShTaM bhagavat-kIrtana-smaraNa-caraNa-paricarNAdikam etad eva mama sAdhanam etad eva mama sAdhyam etad eva mama jIvAtuH sAdhana-sAdhya-dashayos tyaktum ashakyam etad eva me kAmyam etad eva me kAryam etad anyan na me kAryaM nApy abhilaShaNIyaM svapne 'pIty atra sukham astu duHkhaM vAstu saMsAro nashyatu vA na nashyatu | tatra mama kApi na kShatir ity evaM nishcayAtmikA buddhir akaitava-bhaktAv eva sambhavet | tad uktaM - tato bhajeta mAM bhaktyA shraddhAlur dR^iDha-nishcayaH [BhP 11.20.28] iti | 

tato 'nyatra naiva buddhir ekety Aha bahv iti | bahavaH shAkhA yAsAM tAH | tathA hi karma-yoge kAmAnAm AnantyAd buddhayo 'nantAH | tathaiva j~nAna-yoge prathamam antaHkaraNa-shuddhy-arthaM niShkAma-karmaNi buddhis tatas tasmin shuddhe sati karma-saMnyAse buddhiH | tadA j~nAne buddhiH | j~nAna-vaiphalyAbhAvArthaM bhaktau buddhiH j~nAnaM ca mayi saMnyaset iti bhagavad-ukter j~nAna-saMnyAse ca bhaktau buddhir iti buddhayo 'nantAH | karma-j~nAna-bhaktInAm avashyAnuShTheyatvAt tat-tac-chAkhA apy anantAH ||41||

baladevaH : kAmya-karma-viShayaka-buddhito niShkAma-karma-viShayaka-buddher vaishiShTyam Aha vyavasAyeti | he kurunandana iha vaidikeShu sarveShu karmasu vyavasAyAtmikA bhagavad-arcana-rUpair niShkAma-karmabhir vishuddha-citto viShorNAdivat tad-antargatena j~nAnenAtma-yAthAtmyam aham anubhaviShyAmIti nishcaya-rUpA buddhir ekA ekav-viShayatvAt | ekasmai tad-anubhavAya teShAM vihitatvAd iti yAvat | avyavasAyinAm kAmya-karmAnuShThAtÌNAM tu buddhayo hy anantAH | pashv-anna-putra-svargAdy-ananta-kAma-viShayatvAt | tatrApi bahu-shAkhAH | eka-phalake 'pi darsha-paurNamAsAdAv AyuH suprajastAdy-avAntarAneka-phalAshaMsA-shravaNAt | atra hi dehAtiriktAtma-j~nAna-mAtram apekShate na tUktAtma-yAthAtmyaM tan nishcaye kAmya-karmasu pravR^itter asambhavAt ||41||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.42-44

yAm imAM puShpitAM vAcaM pravadanty avipashcitaH |
veda-vAda-ratAH pArtha nAnyad astIti vAdinaH ||42||
kAmAtmAnaH svarga-parA janma-karma-phala-pradAm |
kriyA-visheSha-bahulAM bhogaishvarya-gatiM prati ||43||
bhogaishvarya-prasaktAnAM tayApahR^ita-cetasAm |
vyavasAyAtmikA buddhiH samAdhau na vidhIyate ||44||

shrIdharaH : nanu kAmino 'pi kaShTAn kAmAn vihAya vyavasAyAtmikAm eva buddhiM kim iti na kurvanti | tatrAha yAm imAm ity Adi | yAm imAM puShpitAM viSha-latAvad ApAta-ramaNIyAM prakR^iShTAM paramArtha-phala-parAm eva vadanti vAcaM svargAdi-phala-shrutim | teShAM tayA vAcA 'pahR^ita-cetasAM vyavasAyAtmikA buddhiH samAdhau na vidhIyate iti tR^itIyenAnvayaH | kim iti tathA vadanti | yato 'vipashcito mUDhAH | tatra hetuH veda-vAda-ratA iti | vede ye vAdA artha-vAdAH | akShayyaM ha vai cAturmAsya-yAjinaH sukR^itaM bhavati | tathA, apAM somam amR^itA ambhUma ity AdyAH | teShv eva ratAH prItAH | ataevAtaHparam anyad Ishvara-tattvaM prApyaM nAstIti-vadana-shIlAH ||42||

ataeva kAmAtmAna iti | kAmAtmAnaH kAmAkulita-cittAH | ataH svarga eva paraH puruShArtho yeShAM te | janma ca tatra karmANi ca tat-phalAni ca pradadAtIti tathA | tAM bhogaishvaryayor gatiM prAptiM prati sAdhana-bhUtA ye kriyA-visheShAs te bahulA yasyAM tAM pravadantIty anuShaN^gaH ||43||

tatash ca bhogaishvarya-prasaktAnAm ity Adi | bhogaishvaryayoH prasaktAnAm abhiniviShTAnAM tayA puShpitayA vAcApahR^itam AkR^iShTaM ceto yeShAm teShAm | samAdhish cittaikAgryam | parameshvarAbhimukhatvam iti yAvat | tasmin nishcayAtmikA buddhis tu na vidhIyate | karma-kartari prayogaH | sA notpadyata iti bhAvaH ||44||

madhusUdanaH : avyavasayinAm api vyavasAyAtmikA buddhiH kuto na bhavati pramANasya tulyatvAd ity AshaN^kya pratibandhaka-sad-bhAvAn na bhavatIty Aha yAm imAm iti tribhiH | kuta evam ata Aha bhogaishvarya-gatiM prati kriyA-visheSha-bahulAm amR^ita-pAnorvashI-vihAra-pArijAta-parimalAdi-nibandhano yo bhogas tat-kAraNaM ca yad aishvaryaM devAdi-svAmitvaM tayor gatiM prAptiM prati sAdhana-bhUtA ye kriyA-visheShA agnihotra-darsha-pUrNamAsa-jyotiShTomAdayas tair bahulAM vistR^itAm atibAhulyena bhogaishvarya-sAdhana-kriyA-kalApa-pratipAdikAm iti yAvat | karma-kANDasya hi j~nAna-kANDApekShayA sarvatrAtivistR^itatvaM prasiddham | etAdR^ishIM karma-kANDa-lakShaNAM vAcaM pravadanti prakR^iShTAM paramArtha-svargAdi-phalAm abhyupagacchanti |

ke ye 'vipashcito vicAra-janya-tAtparya-parij~nAna-shUnyAH | ataeva veda-vAda-ratA vede ye santi vAdA artha-vAdAH akShayyaM ha vai cAturmAsya-yAjinaH sukR^itaM bhavati ity evam Adayas teShv eva ratA vedArtha-satyatvenaivam evaitad iti mithyA-vishvAsena santuShTAH | he pArtha ! ataeva nAnyad astIti-vAdinaH karma-kANDApekShayA nAsty anyaj j~nAna-kANDaM sarvasyApi vedasya kArya-paratvAt | karma-phalApekShayA ca nAsty anyan niratishayaM j~nAna-phalam iti vadana-shIlA mahatA prabandhena j~nAna-kANDa-viruddhArtha-bhAShiNa ity arthaH | kuto mokSha-dveShiNyas te ? yataH kAmAtmAnaH kAmyamAna-viShaya-shatAkula-cittatvena kAma-mayAH | evaM sati mokSham api kuto na kAmayante ? yataH svarga-parAH svarga evorvashy-Ady-apetatvena para utkR^iShTo yeShAM te tathA | svargAtiriktaH puruShArtho nAstIti bhrAmyanto viveka-vairAgyAbhAvAn mokSha-kathAm api  soDhum akShamA iti yAvat |

teShAM ca pUrvokta-bhogaishvaryayoH prasaktAnAM kShayitvAdi-doShAdarshanena niviShTAntaH-karaNAnAM tayA kriyA-visheSha-bhulayA vAcApahR^itam AcchAditaM ceto viveka-j~nAnaM yeShAM tathA-bhUtAnAm artha-vAdAH stuty-arthAs tAtparya-viShaye pramANAntarAbAdhite vedasya prAmANyam iti suprasiddham api j~nAtum ashaktAnAM samAdhAv antaH-karaNe vayavasAyAtmikA buddhir na vidhIyate na bhavatIty arthaH | samAdhi-viShayA vyavasAyAtmikA buddhis teShAM na bhavatIti vA adhikaraNe viShaye vA sapatamyAs tulyatvAt | vidhIyata iti karma-kartari la-kAraH | samAdhIyate 'smin sarvam iti vyutpattyA samAdhir antaH-karaNaM vA paramAtmA veti nAprasiddhArtha-kalpanam | ahaM brahmety avasthAnaM samAdhis tan-nimittaM vyavasAyAtmikA buddhir noptadyata iti vyAkhyAne tu rUDhir evAdR^itA |

ayaM bhAvaH -- yadyapi kAmyAny agnihotrAdIni shuddhy-arthebhyo na vishiShyante tathApi phalAbhisandhi-doShAn nAshaya-shuddhiM sampAdayanti | bhogAnuguNA tu shuddhir na j~nAnopayoginI | etad eva darshayituM bhogaishvarya-prasaktAnAm iti punar upAttam | phalAbhisandhim antareNa tu kR^itAni j~nAnopayoginIM shuddhim AdadhatIti siddhaM vipashcid-avipashcitoH phala-vailakShaNyam | vistareNa caitad agre pratipAdayiShyate ||42-44||

vishvanAthaH : tasmAd avyavasAyinaH sakAma-karmiNas tv atimandA ity Aha yAm imAm iti | puShpitAM vAcaM puShpitAM viphalatAm ivApAtato ramaNIyam | pravadanti prakarSheNa sarvataH prakR^iShTA iyam eva veda-vAg iti ye vadanti, teShAM tayA vAcA apahR^ita-cetasAM ca vyavasAyAtmikA buddhir na vidhIyate iti tR^itIyenAnvayaH | teShu tasyA asambhavAt sA teShu nopadishyata ity arthaH | kim iti te tathA vadanti, yato 'vipashcito mUrkhAH | tatra hetuH vedeShu ye 'rtha-vAdAH - akShayyaM vai cAturmAsya-yAjinaH sukR^itaM bhavati, apAM somam amR^itA ambhUma ity AdyAH | anyad Ishvara-tattvaM nAstIti prajalpinas te kIdR^ishIM vAcaM pravadanti | janma-karma-phala-pradAyinIM bhogaishvarya-gatiM prati ye kriyA-visheShAs tAn bahu yathA syAt tathA lAti dadAti pratipAdayatIti tAm ||42-43||

tatash ca bhogaishvaryayoH prasaktAnAm tayA puShpitayA vAcA apahR^itam AkR^iShTaM ceto yeShAm te | tathA teShAm samAdhish cittaikAgryam parameshvaraikonmukhatvaM tasmin nishcayAtmikA buddhir na vidhIyate | karma-kartari prayogaH | sA notpadyata iti bhAvaH iti svAmi-vacanaiH ||44||

baladevaH : nanv eShAM vyavasAyAtmikA buddhir bhavet shrutes taulyAd iti cec citta-doShAn na bhaved ity Aha yAm iti tribhiH | avipashcito 'lpa-j~nAH yAm imAM jyotiShTomena svarga-kAmo yajetety AdikAM vAcaM pravadanti iyam eva prakR^iShTA vedavAg iti kalpayanti | tayA vAcApahR^ita-cetasAM teShAM samAdhau manasi vyavasAyAtmikA buddhir na vidhIyate nAbhyudeti ity anuShaN^gaH | kIdR^ishIM vAcam ity Aha puShpitAm iti || kusumita-viSha-latAvad ApAta-manoj~nAM niShphalAm ity arthaH | evaM kutas te vadanti tatrAha vedeti | vedeShu ye vAdAH apAM somam amR^itA ambhUma, akShayyaM ha vai cAturmAsya-yAjinaH sukR^itaM bhavati ity Adayo 'rthavAdAs teShv eva ratAH vedasya satya-bhAShitvAd evam evaitad iti pratItimantaH | ataeva nAnyad iti karma-phalAt svargAd anyat jIvAMshi-paramArtha-j~nAnaM labhyaM mokSha-lakShaNaM niratishayaM nitya-sukhaM nAsti | tat-pratipAdikAnAM vedAnta-vAcAM karmAN^ga-kartR^i-devatAd ekatayA tac-cheShatvAd iti vadana-shIlA ity arthaH ||42|| 

citta-doSham Aha kAmAtmAnaH vaiShayika-sukha-vAsanA-grasta-cittAH | evaM cet tAdR^ishaM mokShaM kuto necchanti tatrAha svargeti | svarga eva sudhA devAN^ganAdy-upetatvena paraH shreShTho yeShAM te | tAdR^ig-vAsanA-grastatvAt teShAM nAnyad bhAShata ity arthaH | janma karmeti janma ca dehendriya-sambandha-laksaNaM, tatra karma ca tat-tad-varNAshrama-vihitaM, phalaM ca vinAshi-pashv-anna-svargAdi | tAni prakarSheNAvicchedena dadAti tAM bhogaishvaryayor gatiM prAptiM prati ye kriyA-visheShA jyotiShTpmAdayas te bahulAH pracurA yatra tAM vAcaM vadantIti pUrveNAnvayaH | bhogaH sudhA-pAna-devAN^ganAdiH, aishvaryaM ca devAdi-svAmitvaM tayor gatim ity arthaH ||43||

baladevaH : bhogeti teShAM pUrvoktayor bhogaishvaryayoH prasaktAnAM kShayitva-doShAsphUrtyA tayor abhiniviShTAnAM tayA puShpitayA vAcApahR^itam viluptaM ceto viveka-j~nAnaM yeShAm tAdR^ishAnAM samAdhAv iti yo 'yam | samyag AdhIyate 'sminn Atma-tattva-yAthAtmyam iti nirukteH samAdhir manas tasminn ity arthaH ||44||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.45

traiguNya-viShayA vedA nistraiguNyo bhavArjuna |
nirdvandvo nitya-sattva-stho niryoga-kShema AtmavAn ||45||

shrIdharaH : nanu svargAdikaM paramaM phalaM yadi na bhavati, tarhi kim iti vedas tat-sAdhanatayA karmANi vidhIyante | tatrAha traiguNya-viShayA iti | triguNAtmakAH sakAmA ye 'dhikAriNas tad-viShayAs teShAM karma-phala-sambandha-pratipAdakA vedAH | tvaM tu nistraiguNyo niShkAmo bhava | tatropAyam Aha - nirdvandvaH | sukha-duHkha-shItoShNAdi-yugalAni dvandvAni | tad-rahito bhava | tAni sahasvety arthaH | katham iti | ata Aha nitya-sattva-sthaH san | dhryam avalambyety arthaH | tathA niryoga-kShemaH | aprApta-svIkAro yogaH, prApta-pAlanaM kShemaH | tad-rahitaH | AtmavAn apramattaH | nahi dvandvAkulasya yoga-kShema-vyApR^itasya ca pramAdinas traiguNyAtikramaH sambhavatIti ||45||

madhusUdanaH : nanu sakAmAnAM mA bhUd Ashaya-doShAd vyavasAyAtmikA buddhiH | niShkAmAnAM tu vyavasAyAtmaka-buddhyA karma kurvatAM karma-svAbhAvyAt svargAdi-phala-prAptau j~nAna-pratibandhaH samAna ity AshaN^kyAha traiguNyeti | trayANAM guNAnAM karma traiguNyaM kAma-mUlaH saMsAraH | sa eva prakAshatvena viShayo yeShAM tAdR^ishA vedAH karma-kANDAtmakA yo yat-phala-kAmas tasyaiva tat-phalaM bodhayantIty arthaH | na hi saarvebhyaH kAmebhyo darsha-pUrNamAsAv iti viniyoge 'pi sakR^id-anuShThAnAt sarva-phala-prAptir bhavati tat-tat-kAmanAvirahAt | yat-phala-kAmanayAnutiShThati tad eva phalaM tasmin prayoga iti sthitaM yogasiddhy-adhikaraNe | yasmAd evaM kAmA-virahe phala-virahas tasmAt tvaM nistraiguNyo niShkAmo bhava | he arjuna ! etena karma-svAbhAvyAt saMsAro nirastaH | 

nanu shItoShNAdi-dvandva-pratIkArAya vastrAdy-apekShaNAt kuto niShkAmatvam ata Aha nirdvandvaH | sarvatra bhaveti sambadhyate | mAtrA-sparshAs tv ity ukta-nyAyena shItoShNAdi-dvandva-sahiShNur bhava | tasmiMs tiShThatIti tathA | rajas-tamobhyAm abhibhUta-sattvo hi shItoShNAdi-pIDayA mariShyAmIti manvAno dharmAd vimukho bhavati | tvaM tu rajas tamasI abhibhUya sattva-mAtrAlambano bhava |

nanu shItoShNAdi-sahane 'pi kShut-pipAsAdi-pratIkArArthaM kiMcid anupAttam upAdeyam upAttaM ca rakShaNIyam iti tad-arthaM yatne kriyamANe kutaH sattva-sthatvam ity ata Aha niryoga-kShemaH | alabdha-lAbho yogaH, labdha-parirakShaNaM kShemas, tad-rahito bhava | citta-vikShepa-kAri-parigraha-rahito bhavety arthaH | na caivaM cintA kartavyA katham evaM sati jIviShyAmIti | yataH sarvAntaryAmI parameshvara eva tava yoga-kShemAdi nirvAhayiShyatIty Aha AtmavAn | AtmA paramAtmA dhyeyatvena yoga-kShemAdi-nirvAhakatvena ca vartate yasya sa AtmavAn | sarva-kAmanA-parityAgena parameshvaram ArAdhayato mama sa eva deha-yAtrA-mAtram apekShitaM sampAdayiShyatIti nishcitya nishcinto bhavety arthaH | AtmavAn apramatto bhaveti vA ||45||

vishvanAthaH : tvaM tu catur-varga-sAdhanebhyo virajya kevalaM bhakti-yogam evAshrayasvety Aha traiguNyeti | traiguNyAs triguNAtmikAH karma-j~nAnAdyAH prakAshyatvena viShayA yeShAM te traiguNya-viShayA vedAH svArthe Shya¤, etac ca bhUmnA vyapadeshA bhavanti iti nyAyenoktam | kintu bhaktir evainaM nayati iti | yasya deve parA bhaktir yathA deve tathA gurau ity Adi shrutayaH | pa¤carAtrAdi-smR^itayash ca gItopaniShad-gopAla-tApanyAdy-upaniShadash ca nirguNAM bhaktim api viShayIkurvanty eva vedoktatvAbhAve bhakter aprAmANyam eva syAt | tatash ca vedoktA ye triguNamayA j~nAna-karma-vidhayas tebhya eva nirgato bhava tAn na kuru | ye tu vedoktA bhakti-vidhayas tAMs tu sarvathaivAnutiShTha | tad-anuShThAne -

shruti-smR^iti-purANAdi-pA¤carAtra-vidhiM vinA |
aikAntikI harer bhaktir utpAtAyaiva kalpyate ||

iti doSho durvAra eva | tena sa-guNAnAM guNAtItAnAm api, vedAnA-viShayAs traiguNyA nistraiguNyAsh ca | tatra tvaM tu nistraiguNyo bhava | nirguNayA mad-bhaktyaiva triguNAtmakebhyas tebhyo niShkrAnto bhava | tata eva nirdvandvo guNamaya-mAnApamAnAdi-rahitaH | ataeva nityaiH sattvaiH prANibhir mad-bhaktair eva saha tiShThatIti tathA saH | nityaM sattva-guNastho bhaveti vyAkhyAyAM nistraiguNyo bhaeti vyAkhyAyAM virodhaH syAt | alabdha-lAbho yogaH, labdhasya rakShaNaM kShemas tad-rahitaH | mad-bhakti-rasAsvAda-vashAd eva tayor ananusandhAnAt | yoga-kShemaM vahAmy aham it bhakta-vatsalena mayaiva tad-bhAra-vahanAt | AtmavAn mad-datta-buddhi-yuktaH | atra nistraiguNya-traiguNyayor vivecanam | yad uktam ekAdashe -

mad-arpaNaM niShphalaM vA sAttvikaM nija-karma yat |
rAjasaM phala-saN^kalpaM hiMsA-prAyAdi tAmasam || [BhP 11.25.23]

niShphalaM veti naimittikaM nija-karma-phalAkAN^kShyA-rahitam ity arthaH |

kaivalyaM sAttvikaM j~nAnaM rajo vaikalpikaM tu yat |
prAkR^itaM tAmasaM j~nAnaM man-niShThaM nirguNaM smR^itam || 
vanaM tu sAttviko vAso grAmo rAjasa ucyate |
tAmasaM dyuta-sadanaM man-niketaM tu nirguNam || 
sAttvikaH kArako 'saN^gI rAgAndho rAjasaH smR^itaH |
tAmasaH smR^iti-vibhraShTo nirguNo mad-apAshrayaH || 
sAttvikyAdhyAtmikI shraddhA karma-shraddhA tu rAjasI |
tAmasy adharme yA shraddhA mat-sevAyAM tu nirguNA || 
pathyaM pUtam anAyastam AhAryaM sAttvikaM smR^itam |
rAjasaM cendriya-preShThaM tAmasaM cArtidAshuci || 
sAttvikaM sukham AtmotthaM viShayotthaM tu rAjasam |
tAmasaM moha-dainyotthaM nirguNaM mad-apAshrayam || [BhP 11.25.24-29] iti |

ity antena granthena traiguNya-vastUny api bhaktyA svasmin katha¤cit sthitasya traiguNyasya nirjayo 'py uktas tad-anantaram eva | yathA -

dravyaM deshas tathA kAlo j~nAnaM karma ca kArakaH |
shraddhAvasthA-kR^itir niShThA traiguNyaH sarva eva hi || 
sarve guNamayA bhAvAH puruShAvyakta-dhiShThitAH |
dR^iShTaM shrutam anudhyAtaM buddhyA vA puruSharShabha || 
etAH saMsR^itayaH puMso guNa-karma-nibandhanAH |
yeneme nirjitAH saumya guNAjIvena cittajAH |
bhakti-yogena man-niShTho mad-bhAvAya prapadyate || [BhP 11.25.30-32]

tasmAd bhaktyaiva nirguNayA traiguNyajayo nAnyathA | atrApy agre kathaM caitAMs trIn guNAn ativartate iti prashne vakShyate --

mAM ca yo 'vyabhicAreNa bhakti-yogena sevate |
sa guNAn samatItyaitAn brahma-bhUyAya kalpate || [GItA 14.26]

shrI-svAmi-caraNAnAM vyAkhyA ca - ca-kAro 'trAvadhAraNArthaH | mAm eva parameshvaram avyabhicAreNa bhakti-yogena yaH sevate ity eShA |
nistraiguNyo bhavArjuna nirdvandvo nityasattvastho niryogakShema AtmavAn ||45||

baladevaH : nanu phalanairapekShyeNa karmANi kurvANAn api tAni sva-phalair yojayeyus tat svAbhAvyAt tataH kathaM tad-buddheH sambhava iti cet tatrAha traiguNyeti | trayANAM guNAnAM karma traiguNyam | guNa-vacana-brAhmaNAdibhyaH karmaNi ca iti sUtrAt [PAN 5.1.124] Shya¤-sakAmatvam ity arthaH | tad-viShayA vedAH karma-kANDAni tvaM tu tac-chiro-bhUta-vedAnta-niShTho nistraiguNyo niShkAmo bhava | 

ayam arthaH - pitR^i-koTi-vatsalo hi vedo 'nAdi-bhagavad-vimukhAn mAyA-guNair nibaddhAMs tad-guNa-sR^iShTa-sAttvikAdi-sukha-saktAn prati tat-kAmAn anurudhya phalAni prakAshayan svasmiMs tAn vishrambhayati | tad-vishrambheNa tat-parishIlinas te tan-mUrdha-bhUtopanisat-pratIta-yAthAtmya-nishcayena tAM buddhiM yAntIti na cAkAmitAny api tAny ApateyuH kAmitAnAm eva teShAM phalatva-shravaNAt | na ca sarveShAM vedAnAM traiguNya-viShayatvaM nistraiguNyatAyA aprAmANikatvApatteH | 

nanu shItoShNAdi-nivAraNAya mAtrAsparshAs tu kaunteyety Adi vimarshena dvandva-saho bhava | tatra hetur nityeti | nityaM yat sattvam apariNAmitvaM jIva-niShThaM tat-sthas tad-vibhAvyety arthaH | tata eva niryogakShemaH | alabdha-lAbho yogaH labdhasya parirakShaNaM kShemaM tad-rahito bhavety arthaH |

nanu kShut-pipAse tathApi vAdhike iti cet tatrAha AtmavAn iti | AtmA vishvambharaH paramAtmA sa yasya dhyeyatayAsti tAdR^isho bhavety arthaH | sa te deha-yAtrAM sampAdayed ity arthaH ||45||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.46

yAvAn artha udapAne sarvataH saMplutodake |
tAvAn sarveShu vedeShu brAhmaNasya vijAnataH ||46||

shrIdharaH : nanu vedokta-nAnA-phala-tyAgena niShAmatayeshvarArAdhana-viShayA vyavasAyAtmikA buddhiH kubuddhir evety AshaDkyAha yAvAn iti | udakaM pIyate yasmiMs tad udapAnaM vApI-kUpa-taDAg-Adi | tasmin svalpodaka ekatra kR^itsnArthasyAsambhavAt tatra tatra paribhramaNena vibhAgasho yAvAn snAna-pAnAdir arthaH prayojanaM bhavati tAvAn sarvo 'py arthaH sarvataH saMplutodake mahA-hrade ekatraiva yathA bhavati | evaM yAvAn sarveShu vedeShu tat-tat-karma-phala-rUpo 'rthas tAvAn sarvo 'pi vijAnato vyavasAyAtmikA-buddhi-yuktasya brAhmaNasya brahma-niShThasya bhavaty eva | brahmAnande kShudAnandAnAm antarbhAvAt | etasyaivAnandasyAnyAni bhUtAni mAtrAm upajIvanti iti shruteH | tasmAd iyam eva subuddhir ity arthaH ||46||

madhusUdanaH : na caivaM shaN^kanIyaM sarva-kAmanA-parityAgena karma kurvann ahaM tais taiH karma-janitair Anandair va¤citaH syAm iti | yasmAt yAvAn iti | udapAne kShudra-jalAshaye | jAtAv eka-vacanam | yAvAn artho yAvat-snAna-pAnAdi-prayojanaM bhavati sarvataH saMplutodake mahati jalAshaye tAvAn artho bhavaty eva | yathA hi parvata-nirjharAH sarvataH sravantaH kvacid upatyakAyAm ekatra milanti tatra pratyekaM jAyamAnam udaka-prayojanaM samudite sutarAM bhavati sarveShAM nirjharANAm ekatraiva kAsAre 'ntarbhAvAt | evaM sarveShu vedeShu vedokteShu kAmya-karmasu yAvAn artho hairaNyagarbhAnanda-paryantas tAvAn vijAnato brahma-tattvaM sAkShAt-kR^itavato brAhmaNasya brahma-bubhUShor bhavaty eva | kShudAnandAnAm brahmAnandAMshatvAt tatra kShudrAnandAnAm antarbhAvAt | etasyaivAnandasyAnyAni bhUtAni mAtrAm upajIvanti iti shruteH | ekasyApy AnandasyAvidyA-kalpita-tat-tad-upAdhi-paricchedam AdAyAMshAMshivad vyapadesha AkAshasyeva ghaTAdy-avaccheda-kalpanayA |

tathA ca niShkAma-karmabhiH shuddhAntaH-karaNasya tavAtma-j~nAnodaye para-brahmAnanda-prAptiH syAt tathaiva ca sarvAnanda-prAptau na kShudrAnanda-prApti-nibandhana-vaiyagryAvakAshaH | ataH paramAnanda-prApakAya tattva-j~nAnAya niShkAma-karmANi kurv ity abhiprAyaH | atra yathA tathA bhavatIti-pada-trayAdhyAhAro yAvAMs tAvAn iti pada-dvayAnuShaN^gash ca dArShTAntike draShTavyaH ||46||

vishvanAthaH : hanta kiM vaktavyaM niShkAmasya nirguNasya bhaktiyogasya mAhAtmyaM yasyaivArambhaNa-mAtre 'pi nAsha-pratyavAyau na staH | svalpa-mAtreNApi kR^itArthatety ekAdashe 'py uddhavAyApi vakShyate -

na hy aN^gopakrame dhvaMso
mad-dharmasyoddhavANv api |
mayA vyavasitaH samyaÇ
nirguNatvAd anAshiShaH || iti | [BhP 11.29.20]

kintu sa-kAmo bhakti-yogo 'pi vyavasAyAtmika-buddhi-shabdenocyate | iti dR^iShTAntena sAdhayati yAvAn iti | udapAna iti jAtyaika-vacanam udapAneShu kUpeShu | yAvAn artha iti kashcit kUpaH shauca-karmArthakaH, kashcid dAnta-dhAvanArthakaH, kashcid vastra-dhAvanAdy-arthakaH, kashcit keshAdi-mArjanArthakaH, kashcit snAnArthakaH, kashcit pAnArthaka ity evaM sarvataH sarveShudapAneShu yAvAn artho yAvanti prayojanAnIty arthaH tasmin ekasminn eva shaucAdi-karma-siddheH | kiM ca, tat-tat-kUpeShu pR^ithak pR^ithak paribhramaNa-shrameNa, sarovare tu taM vinaiva | tathA kUpeShu virasa-jalena sarovare tu surama-jalenaivety api visheSho draShTavyaH | evaM sarveShu vedeShu tat-tad-devatArAdhanena yAvanto 'rthAs tAvanta ekasya bhagavad-ArAdhanena vijAnato vij~nasya brAhmaNasyeti brahma vedaM bettIti brahmaNas tasya vijAnato vedaj~natve 'pi veda-tAtparyaM bhaktiM visheShato jAnataH | yathA dvitIya-skandhe -

brahma-varcasa-kAmas tu yajeta brahmaNaH patim |
indram indriya-kAmas tu prajA-kAmaH prajApatim || [BhP 2.3.2]

daivIM mAyAM tu shrI-kAmaH ity Ady-uktyA,

akAmaH sarva-kAmo vA mokSha-kAma udAra-dhIH |
tIvreNa bhakti-yogena yajeta puruShaM param || [BhP 2.3.10]

iti meghAdy-amishrasya saura-kiraNasya tIvratvam iva bhaktiyogasya j~nAna-karmAdy-amishratvaM tIvratvaM j~neyam | atra bahubhyo bahu-kAma-siddhir iti sarvathA bahu-buddhitvam eva | ekasmAd bhagavata eva sarva-kAma-siddhir ity aMshenaika-buddhitvAd eka-buddhitvam eva viShaya-sAdguNyAj j~neyam ||46||

baladevaH : mami sarvAn vedAn adhIyAnasya bahu-kAla-vyayAd bahu-vikShepa-sambhavAc ca kathaM tad-buddher abhudayas tatrAha yAvAn iti | sarvataH samplutodaketi | vistIrNe udapAne jalAshaye snAnAdy-arthino yAvAn snAna-pAnAdir arthaH prayojanaM tAvAn eva sa tena tasmAt sampadyate | evaM sarveShu sopaniShatsu vedeShu brAhmaNasya vedAdhyAyino vijAnata Atma-yAthAtmya-j~nAnaM labdhu-kAmasya yAvAn taj-j~nAna-siddhi-lakShaNo 'rthaH syAt tAvAn eva tena tebhyaH sampAdyate ity arthaH | tathA ca sva-shAkhayaiva sopaniShadAcireNaiva tat siddhau tad buddhir abhudiyAd eveti | iha dArShTAntike 'pi yAvAMs tAvAn iti pada-dvayam anuSha¤janIyam ||46||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.47

karmaNy evAdhikAras te mA phaleShu kadAcana |
mA karma-phala-hetur bhUr mA te saN^go 'stv akarmaNi ||47||

shrIdharaH : tarhi sarvANi karma-phalAni parameshvarArAdhanAd eva bhaviShyantIty abhisandhAya pravarteta | kiM karmaNA ity AshaN^kya tad vArayann Aha karmaNy eveti | te tava tattva-j~nAnArthinaH karmaNy evAdhikAraH | tat-phaleShu adhikAraH kAmo mAstu | nanu karmaNi kR^iti tat-phalaM syAd eva bhojane kR^ite tR^iptivat | ity AshaN^kyAha meti | mA karma-phala-hetur bhUH | karma-phalaM pravR^itti-hetur yasya sa tathAbhUto mA bhUH | kAmyamAnasyaiva svargAder niyojya-visheShaNatvena phalatvAd akAmitaM phalaM na syAd iti bhAvaH | ataeva phalaM bandhakaM bhaviShyatIti bhayAd akarmaNi karmAkaraNe 'pi tava saN^go niShThA mAstu ||47||

madhusUdanaH : nanu niShkAma-karmabhir Atma-j~nAnaM sampAdya parAnanda-prAptiH kriyate ced Atma-j~nAnam eva tarhi sampAdyaM kiM bahvAyAsaiH karmabhir bahiraN^ga-sAdhana-bhUtair ity AshaN^kyAha karmaNy eveti | te tavAshuddhAntaHkaraNasya tAttvika-j~nAnotpatty-ayogyasya karmaNy evAntaHkaraNa-shodhake 'dhikAro mayedaM kartavyam iti bodho 'stu na j~nAna-niShThA-rUpaM vedAnta-vAkya-vicArAdau | karma ca kurvatas tava tat-phaleShu svargAdiShu kadAcana kasyAMcid apy avasthAyAM karmAnuShThAnAt prAg UrdhvaM tat-kAle vAdhikAro mayedaM bhoktavyam iti bodho mAstu | 

nanu mayedaM bhoktavyam iti buddhy-abhAve 'pi karma sva-sAmArthyAd eva phalaM janayiShyatIti cen nety Aha mA karma-phala-hetur bhUH | phala-kAmanayA hi karma kurvan phalasya heteur utpAdako bhavati | tvaM tu niShkAmaH san karma-phala-hetur mA bhUH | na hi niShkAmena bhagavad-arpaNa-buddhyA kR^itaM karma phalAya kalpata ity uktam | phalAbhAve kiM karmaNety ata Aha - mA te saN^go 'stv akarmaNi | yadi phalaM neShyate kiM karmaNA duHkha-rUpeNety akaraNe tava prItir mA bhUt ||47||

vishvanAthaH : evam ekam evArjunaM sva-priya-sakhaM lakShIkR^itya j~nAna-bhakti-karma-yogAn AcikhyAsur bhagavAn j~nAna-bhakti-yogau procya tayor arjunasyAnadhikAraH vimR^ishya niShkAma-karma-yogam Aha karmaNIti | mA phaleShv iti - phalAkAN^kShiNo 'py atyanta-shuddha-cittA bhavanti | tvaM tu prAyaH shuddha-citta iti mayA j~nAtvaivocyasa iti bhAvaH | 

nanu karmaNi kR^ite phalam avashyaM bhaviShyaty eveti | tatrAha mA karma-phala-hetur bhUH phala-kAmanayA hi karma kurvan phalasya hetur utpAdako bhavati | tvaM tu tAdR^isho mA bhUr ity AshIr mayA dIyata ity arthaH | akarmaNi sva-dharmAkaraNe vikarmaNi pApe vA saN^gas tava mAstu, kintu dveSha evAstv iti punar apy AshIr dIyata iti | atrAgrimAdhyAye vyAmishreNaiva vAkyena buddhiM mohayasIva me ity arjunokti-darshanAd atrAdhyAye pUrvottara-vAkyAnAm avatArikAbhir nAtIva saN^gatir vidhitsiteti j~neyam | kintu tva-Aj~nAyAM sArathy-Adau yathAhaM tiShThAmi, tathA tvam api mad-Aj~nAyAM tiShTheti kR^iShNArjunayor mano 'nulApo 'yam atra draShTavyaH ||47||

baladevaH : nanu karmabhir j~nAna-siddhir iShyate cet tarhi tasya shamAdIny evAntaraN^gatvAd anuShTheyAni santu kiM bahu prayAsais tair iti cet tatrAha - karmaNy eveti | jAtAv eka-vacanam | te tava sva-dharme 'pi yuddhe 'dharma-buddher ashuddha-cittasya tAvat karmasv eva yuddhAdiShv adhikAro 'stu mayaitAni bhoktavyAnIti tat phaleShu bandhakeShu tavAdhikAro mAstu mayaitAni bhoktavyAnIti |

nanu phalecchA-virahe 'pi tAni sva-phaair yojayeyur iti cet tatrAha mA karmeti | karma-phalAnAM hetur utpAdakas tvaM mAbhUH kAmanayA kR^itAni tAni sva-phalair yojayanti kAmitAnAm eva phalAnAM niyojya-visheShaNatvena phalatvAmnAtAt | ataeva bandhakAni phalAni ApatiShyantIti bhayAd akarmaNi karmAkaraNe tava saN^gaH prItir mAstu kintu vidveSha evAstv ity arthaH | niShkAmatayAnuShThitAni karmANi yaShTidhAnyavad antar eva j~nAna-niShThAM niShpAdayiShyanti | shamAdIni tu tat-pR^iShTha-lagnAny eva syur iti bhAvaH ||47||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.48

yogasthaH kuru karmANi saN^gaM tyaktvA dhanaJNjaya |
siddhy-asiddhyoH samo bhUtvA samatvaM yoga ucyate ||48||

shrIdharaH : kiM tarhi ? yoga-stha iti | yogaH parameshvaraikaparatA | tatra sthitaH karmANi kuru | tathA saN^gaM kartR^itvAbhiniveshaM tyaktvA kevalam IshvarAshrayeNaiva kuru | tat-phalasya j~nAnasyApi siddhy-asiddhyoH samo bhUtvA kevalam IshvarAshrayeNaiva kuru | yata evaMbhUtaM samatvam eva yoga ucyate sadbhiH citta-samAdhAna-rUpatvAt ||48||

madhusUdanaH : pUrvoktam eva vivR^iNoti yoga-stha iti | he dhana¤jaya tvaM yogasthaH san saN^gaM phalAbhilAShaM kartR^itvAbhiniveshaM ca tyaktvA karmANi kuru | atra bahu-vacanAt karmaNy evAdhikAras ta ity atra jAtAv eka-vacanam | saN^ga-tyAgopAyam Aha siddhy-asiddhyoH samo bhUtvA phala-siddhau harShaM phalAsiddhau ca viShAdaM tyaktvA kevalam IshvarArAdhana-buddhyA karmANi kurv iti | 

nanu yoga-shabdena prAk-karmoktam | atra tu yoga-sthaH karmANi kurv ity ucyate | ataH katham etad boddhyM shakyam ity ata Aha samatvaM yoga ucyate | yad etat siddhy-asiddhyoH samatvam idam eva yoga-stha ity atra yoga-shabdenocyate na tu karmeti na ko 'pi virodha ity arthaH | atra pUrvArdhasyottarArdhena vyAkhyAnaM kriyata ity apaunaruktyam iti bhAShyakArIyaH panthAH | sukha-duHkhe same kR^itvA ity atra jayAjaya-sAmyena yuddha-mAtra-kartavyatA prakR^itatvAd uktA | iha tu dR^iShTAdR^iShTa-sarva-phala-parityAgena sarva-karma-kartavyateti visheShaH ||48||

vishvanAthaH : niShkAma-karmaNaH prakAraM shikShayati yoga-stha iti | tena jayAjayayos tulya-buddhiH san saN^grAmam eva sva-dharmaM kurv iti bhAvaH | ayaM niShkAma-karma-yoga eva j~nAna-yogatvena pariNamatIti | j~nAna-yogo 'py evaM pUrvottara-granthArtha-tAtparyato j~neyaH ||48||

baladevaH : pUrvoktaM vishadayati yoga-stha iti | tvaM saN^gaM phalAbhilAShaM kartR^itvAbhiniveshaM ca tyaktvA yogasthaH san karmANi kuru yuddhAdIni | Adyena mAyA-nimajjanam eva | dvitIyena tu svAtantrya-lakShaNa-paresha-dharma-cauryam | tena tan-mAyA-vyAkopaH | atas tayoH parityAga iti bhAvaH | yogastha-padaM vivR^iNoti -- siddhy-asiddhyor iti | tad-anuShaN^ga-phalAnAM jayAdInAM siddhAv asiddhau ca samo bhUtvA rAga-dveSha-rahitaH san kuru | idam eva samatvaM mayA yoga-stha ity atra yoga-shabdenoktaM citta-samAdhi-rUpatvAt ||48||


__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.49

dUreNa hy avaraM karma buddhi-yogAd dhanaJNjaya |
buddhau sharaNam anviccha kR^ipaNAH phala-hetavaH ||49||

shrIdharaH : kAmyaM tu karmAtinikR^iShTam ity Aha dUreNeti | buddhyA vyavasAyAtmikayA kR^itaH karma-yogo buddhi-yogo buddhi-sAdhana-bhUto vA, tasmAt sakAshAd anyat sAdhana-bhUtaM kAmyaM karma dUreNa avaraM atyantam apakR^iShTaM hi | yasmAd evaM tasmAd buddhau j~nAne sharaNam AshrayaM karma-yogam anviccha anutiShTha | yad vA buddhau sharaNaM trAtAram Ishvaram Ashrayety arthaH | phalahetur astu sakAmA narAH kR^ipaNA dInAH yo vA etad akSharam gArgy aviditvA asmAl lokAt praiti sa kR^ipaNa [BAU 3.8.10] iti shruteH ||49||

madhusUdanaH : nanu kiM karmAnuShThAnam eva puruShArtho yena niShphalam eva sadA kartavyam ity ucyate prayojanam anuddishya na mando 'pi pravartate iti nyAyAt | tad varaM phala-kAmanayaiva karmAnuShThAnam iti cen nety Aha dUreNeti | buddhi-yogAd Atma-buddhi-sAdhana-bhUtAn niShkAma-karma-yogAd dUreNAtiviprakarSheNAvaram adhamaM karma phalAbhisandhinA kriyamANaM janma-maraNa-hetu-bhUtam | athavA paramAtma-buddhi-yogAd dUreNAvaraM sarvam api karma yasmAd, he dhana¤jaya, tasmAd buddhau paramAtma-buddhau sarvAnartha-nivartikAyAM sharaNaM pratibandhaka-pApa-kShayeNa rakShakaM niShkAma-karma-yogam anviccha kartum iccha | ye tu phala-hetavaH phala-kAmA avaraM karma kurvanti te kR^ipaNAH sarvadA janma-maraNAdi-ghaTI-yantra-bhramaNena para-vashA atyanta-dInA ity arthaH | yo vA etad akSharam gArgy aviditvA asmAl lokAt praiti sa kR^ipaNa [BAU 3.8.10] iti shruteH | tathA ca tvam api kR^ipaNo mA bhUH kintu sarvAnartha-nivartakAtma-j~nAnotpAdakaM niShkAma-karma-yogam evAnutiShThety abhiprAyaH | yathA hi kR^ipaNA janA atiduHkhena dhanam arjayanto yat kiMcid dR^iShTa-sukha-mAtra-lobhena dAnAdi-janitaM mahat sukham anubhavituM na shaknuvantIty AtmAnam eva va¤cayanti tathA mahatA duHkhena karmANi kurvANAH kShudra-phala-mAtra-lobhena paramAnandA-nubhavena va¤citA ity aho daurbhAgyaM mauDhyaM ca teShAm iti kR^ipaNa-padena dhvanitam ||49||

vishvanAthaH : sakAma-karma nindati dUreNeti | avaram atinikR^iShTaM kAmyaM karma | buddhi-yogAt parameshvarArpita-niShAma-karma-yogAt | buddhau niShkAma-karmaNy eva buddhi-yogo niShkAma-karma-yogaH ||49||

baladevaH : atha kAmya-karmaNo nikR^iShTatvam Aha dUreNeti | buddhi-yogAd avaraM karma dUreNa, he dhana¤jaya, Atma-yAthAtmya-buddhi-sAdhana-bhUtAn niShkAma-karma-yogAt dUreNAtiviprakarSheNAvaram atyapakR^iShTaM janma-maraNAdy-anartha-nimittaM kAmyaM karmety arthaH | hi yasmAd evam atas tvaM buddhau tad-yAthAtmya-j~nAne sharaNam AshrayaM niShkAma-karma-yogam anviccha kuru | ye tu phala-hetavaH phala-kAmA avara-karma-kAriNas te kR^ipaNAs tat-phala-janma-karmAdi-pravAha-paravashA dInA ity arthaH | tathA ca tvaM kR^ipaNo mAbhUr iti iha kR^ipaNAH khalu kaShTopArjita-vittAdR^iShTa-sukha-lava-lubdhA vittAni dAtum asamarthA mahatA dAna-sukhena va¤citAs tathA kaShTAnuShThita-karmANas tuccha-tat-phala-lubdhA mahatAtma-sukhena va¤citA bhavantIti vyajyate ||49||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.50

buddhi-yukto jahAtIha ubhe sukR^ita-duShkR^ite |
tasmAd yogAya yujyasva yogaH karmasu kaushalam ||50||

shrIdharaH : buddhi-yoga-yuktas tu shreShTha ity Aha buddhi-yukta iti | sukR^itaM svargAdi-prApakaM duShkR^itaM nirayAdi-prApakam | te ubhe ihaiva janmani parameshvara-prasAdena tyajati | tasmAd yogAya tad-arthAya karma-yogAya yujyasva ghaTasva | yogo hi karmasu kaushalam | sva-dharmAkhyeShu karmasu vartamAnasya yA siddhy-asiddhyoH samatva-buddhir IshvarArpita-cetastayA tat kaushalaM kushala-bhAvaH | tad dhi kaushalaM yad bandha-svabhAvAny api karmANi samatva-buddhyA svabhAvAn nivartante | tasmAt samatva-buddhi-yukto bhava tvam ||50||

madhusUdanaH : evaM buddhi-yogAbhAve doSham uktvA tad-bhAve guNam Aha buddhIti | iha karmasu buddhi-yuktaH samatva-buddhyA yukto jahAti parityajati ubhe sukR^ita-duShkR^ite puNya-pApe sattva-shuddhi-j~nAna-prApti-dvAreNa | yasmAd evaM tasmAt samatva-buddhi-yogAya tvaM yujyasva ghaTasvodyukto bhava | yasmAd IdR^ishaH samatva-buddhi-yoga IshvarArpita-cetasaH karmasu pravartamAnasya kaushalaM kushala-bhAvo yad-bandha-hetUnAm api karmaNAM tad-abhAvo mokSha-paryavasAyitvaM ca tan mahat kaushalam |

samatva-buddhi-yuktaH karma-yogaH karmAtmApi san duShTa-karma-kShayaM karotIti mahA-kushalaH | tvaM tu na kushalo yatash cetano 'pi san sajAtIya-duShTa-kShayaM na karoShIti vyatireko 'tra dhvanitaH | athavA iha samatva-buddhi-yukte karmaNi kR^ite sati sattva-shuddhi-dvAreNa buddhi-yuktaH paramAtma-sAkShAtkAravAn sa¤jahAty ubhe sukR^ita-duShkR^ite | tasmAt samatva-buddhi-yuktAya karma-yogAya yujyasva | yasmAt karmasu madhye samatva-buddhi-yuktaH karma-yogaH kaushalaM kushalo duShTa-karma-nivAraNa-catura ity arthaH ||50||

vishvanAthaH : yogAyokta-lakShaNAya yujyasva ghaTasva | yataH karmasu sakAma-niShkAmeShu madhye yoga evodAsInatvena karma-karaNam eva | kaushalaM naipuNyam ity arthaH ||50||

baladevaH : uktasya buddhi-yogasya prabhAvam Aha buddhIti | iha karmasu yo buddhi-yuktaH pradhAna-phala-tyAga-viShayAnuShaN^ga-phala-siddhy-asiddhi-samatva-viShayayA ca buddhyA yuktas tAni karoti, sa ubhe anAdi-kAla-sa¤cite j~nAna-pratibandhake sukR^ita-duShkR^ite jahAti vinAshayatIty arthaH | tasmAd uktAya buddhi-yogAya yujyasva ghaTasva | yasmAt karma-yogas tAdR^isha-buddhi-sambandhaH | kaushalam cAturyaM bandhakAnAm eva buddhi-samparkAd vishodhita-viSha-pArada-nyAyena mocakatvena pariNAmAt ||50||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.51

karmajaM buddhi-yuktA hi phalaM tyaktvA manIShiNaH |
janma-bandha-vinirmuktAH padaM gacchanty anAmayam ||51||

shrIdharaH : karmaNAM mokSha-sAdhanatva-prakAram Aha karma-jam iti | karmajaM phalaM tyaktvA kevalam IshvarArAdhanArthaM karma kurvANo manIShiNo j~nAnino bhUtvA janma-rUpeNa bandhena vinirmuktAH santo 'nAmayaM sarvopadrava-rahitaM viShNoH padaM mokShAkhyaM gacchanti ||51||

madhusUdanaH : nanu duShkR^ita-hAnam apekShitaM na tu sukR^ita-hAnaM puruShArtha-bhraMshApatter ity AshaN^kya tuccha-phala-tyAgena parama-puruShArtha-prAptiM phalam Aha karma-jam iti | samatva-buddhi-yuktA hi yasmAt karmajaM phalaM tyaktvA kevalam IshvarArAdhanArthaM karmANi kurvANAH sattva-shuddhi-dvAreNa manIShiNas tat tvam asi ity Adi-vAkya-janyAtma-manIShAvanto bhavanti | tAdR^ishAsh ca santo janmAtmakena bandhena vinirmuktA visheSheNAtyantikatva-lakShaNena niravasheShaM muktAH padaM padanIyam Atma-tattvam Ananda-rUpaM brahmAnAmayam avidyA-tat-kAryAtmaka-roga-rahitAbhayaM mokShAkhyaM puruShArthaM gacchanty abhedena prApnuvantIty arthaH | 

yasmAd evaM phala-kAmanAM tyaktvA samatva-buddhyA karmANy anutiShThantas taiH kR^itAntaHkaraNa-shuddhayas tat tvam asy Adi-pramANotpannAtma-tattva-j~nAna-tat-kAryAH santaH sakalAnartha-nivR^itti-paramAnanda-prApti-rUpaM mokShAkhyaM viShNoH paramaM padaM gacchanti tasmAt tvam api yac chreyaH syAn nishcitaM brUhi tan me [GItA 2.7] ity ukteH shreyo jij~nAsur evaMvidhaM karma-yogam anutiShTheti bhagavato 'bhiprAyaH ||51||

vishvanAthaH : Nothing.

baladevaH : karmajam iti | buddhi-yuktAs tAdR^isha-buddhimantaH karmajaM phalaM tyaktvA karmANy anutiShThanto manIShiNaH karmAntargatAtma-yAthAtmya-praj~nAvanto bhUtvA janma-bandhena vinirmuktAH santo 'nAmayaM klesha-shUnyaM padaM vaikuNThaM gacchantIti | tasmAt tvam api shreyo jij~nAsur evaM vidhAni karmANi kurv iti bhAvaH | svAtma-j~nAnasya paramAtma-j~nAna-hetutvAt tasyApi tat-pada-gati-hetutvaM yuktam ||51||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.52

yadA te mohakalilaM buddhir vyatitariShyati |
tadA gantAsi nirvedaM shrotavyasya shrutasya ca ||52||

shrIdharaH : kadAhaM tat padaM prApsyAmi ity apekShAyAm Aha yadeti dvAbhyAm | moho dehAdiShu Atma-buddhiH | tad eva kalilaM gahanam | kalilaM gahanaM vidur ity abhidhAna-koSha-smR^iteH | tatash cAyam arthaH | evaM parameshvarArAdhane kriyamANe yadA tat-prasAdena tava buddhir dehAbhimAna-lakShaNaM moha-mayaM gahanaM durgaM visheSheNAtitariShyati tadA shrotavyasya shrutasya cArthasya nirvedaM vairAgyaM gantAsi prApsyasi | tayor anupAdeyatvena jij~nAsAm na kariShyasIty arthaH ||52||

madhusUdanaH : evaM karmANy anutiShThataH kadA me sattva-shuddhiH syAd ity ata Aha yadeti | na hy etAvatA kAlena sattva-shuddhir bhavatIti kAla-niyamo 'sti | kintu yadA yasmin kAle te tava buddhir antaHkaraNaM moha-kalilaM vyatitariShyati avivekAtmakaM kAluSham aham idaM mamedaM ity Ady-aj~nAna-vilasitam atigahanam vyatikramiShyati rajas-tamo-malam apahAya shuddha-bhAvam Apatsyata iti yAvat | tadA tasmin kAle shrotavyasya shrutasya ca karma-phalasya nirvedaM vaitR^iShNyaM gantAsi prAptAsi | parIkShya lokAn karma-citAn brAhmaNo nirvedam AyAt [MuNDU 1.2.12] iti shruteH | nirvedena phalenAntaHkaraNa-shuddhiM j~nAsyasIty abhiprAyaH ||52||

vishvanAthaH : evaM parameshvarArpita-niShkAma-karmAbhyAsAt tava yogo bhaviShyatIty Aha yadeti | tava buddhir antaHkaraNaM moha-kalilaM moha-rUpaM gahanaM visheShato 'tishayena tariShyati, tadA shrotavyasya shrotavyeShv artheShu shrutasya shruteShv apy artheShu nirvedaM prApsyasi asambhAvanA-viparIta-bhAvanayor naShTatvAt kiM me shAstropadesha-vAkya-shravaNena | sAmprataM me sAdhaneShv eva pratikShaNam abhyAsaH sarvathocita iti maMsyasa iti bhAvaH ||52||

baladevaH : nanu niShkAmANi karmANi kurvato me kadAtma-viShayA manIShAbhyudiyAd iti cet tatrAha yadeti | yadA te buddhir antaHkaraNaM moha-kalilaM tuccha-phalAbhilASha-hetum aj~nAna-gahanaM vyatitariShyati parityakShyatIty arthaH, tadA pUrvaM shrutasyAnantaraM shrotavyasya ca tasya tuccha-phalasya sambandhinaM nirvedaM gantAsi gamiShyasi | parIkShya lokAn karma-citAn brAhmaNo nirvedaM AyAt iti shravaNAt | nirvedena phalena tad-viShayAM tAM pariceShyati iti nAsty atra kAla-niyama ity arthaH ||52||


__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.53

shruti-vipratipannA te yadA sthAsyati nishcalA |
samAdhAv acalA buddhis tadA yogam avApsyasyi ||53||

shrIdharaH : tatash ca shrutIti | shrutibhir nAnA-laukika-vaidikArtha-shravaNair vipratipannA | itaH pUrvaM vikShiptA satI tava buddhir yadA samAdhau sthAsyati | samAdhIyate cittam asminn iti samAdhiH parameshvaraH | tasmin nishcalA viShayair antarair anAkR^iShTA | ataevAcalA | abhyAsa-pATavena tatraiva sthirA ca satI yogaM yoga-phalaM tattva-j~nAnam avApsyasi ||53||

madhusUdanaH : antaHkaraNa-shuddhyaivaM jAta-nirvedasya kadA j~nAna-prAptir ity apekShAyAm Aha shrutIti | te tava buddhiH shrutibhir nAnA-vidha-phala-shravaNair avicArita-tAtparyair vipratipannA 'neka-vidha-saMshaya-viparyAsavattvena vikShiptA prAk | yadA yasmin kAle shuddhija-viveka-janitena doSha-darshanena taM vikShepaM parityajya samAdhau parmAtmani nishcalA jAgrat-svapna-darshana-lakShaNa-vikShepa-rahitAcalA suShupti-mUrcchA-stabdhIbhAvAdi-rUpa-laya-lakShaNa-calana-rahitA satI sthAsyati laya-vikShepa-lakShaNau doShau parityajya samAhitA bhaviShyatIti yAvat | athavA nishcalAsambhAvanA-viparIta-bhAvanA-rahitAcalA dIrgha-kAlAdara-nairantarya-satkAra-sevanair vijAtIya-pratyayAdUShitA satI nirvAta-pradIpavad Atmani sthAsyatIti yojanA | tadA tasmin kAle yogaM jIva-paramAtmaikya-lakShaNaM tat-tvam-asIty Adi-vAkya-janyam akhaNDa-sAkShAtkAraM sarva-yoga-phalam avApsyasi | tadA punaH sAdhyAntarAbhAvAt kR^ita-kR^ityaH sthita-praj~no bhaviShyasIty abhiprAyaH ||53||

vishvanAthaH : tatash ca shrutiShu nAnA-laukika-vaidikArtha-shravaNeShu vipratipannA asammatA viraketit yAvat | tatra hetuH nishcalA teShu teShv artheShu calituM vimukhIbhUtety arthaH | kintu samAdhau ShaShThe 'dhyAye vakShyamANa-lakShaNe 'calA sthairyavatI | tadA yogam aparokShAnubhava-prAptyA, jIvan-mukta ity arthaH ||53||

baladevaH : nanu karma-phala-nirviNNatayA karmAnuShThAnena labdha-hR^id-vishuddher abhyuditAtma-j~nAnasya me kadAtma-sAkShAt-kR^itir iti cet tatrAha shrutIti | shrutyA karmaNAM j~nAna-garbhatAM prabodhayantyA tam etam ity AdikayA vipratipannA visheSheNa saMsiddhA te buddhir acalA asambhAvanA-viparIta-bhAvanAbhyAM virahitA yadA samAdhau manasi nirvAta-dIpa-shikheva nishcalA sthAsyati tadA yogam AtmAnubhava-lakShaNam avApsyasi | ayam arthaH phalAbhilASha-shUnyatayAnuShThitAni karmANi sthita-praj~natA-rUpAM j~nAna-niShThAM sAdhayanti | j~nAna-niShThA-rUpA sthita-praj~natA tv AtmAnubhavam iti ||53||
 
__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.54

arjuna uvAca
sthita-praj~nasya kA bhAShA samAdhi-sthasya keshava |
sthita-dhIH kiM prabhASheta kim AsIta vrajeta kim ||54||

shrIdharaH : pUrva-shlokoktasyAtma-tattva-j~nasya lakShaNaM jij~nAsur arjuna uvAca - sthita-praj~nasyeti | svAbhAvike samAdhau sthitasya, ataeva sthitA nishcalA praj~nA buddhir yasya tasya bhAShA kA ? bhAShyate 'nayA iti bhAShA lakShaNam iti yAvat | sa kena lakShaNena sthita-praj~na ucyate ity arthaH | tathA sthita-dhIH kiM kathaM bhAShaNam AsanaM vrajanaM ca kuryAd ity arthaH ||54||

madhusUdanaH : evam labdhAvasaraH sthita-praj~na-lakShaNaM j~nAtum arjuna uvAca | yAny eva hi jIvan-muktAnAM lakShaNAni tAny eva mumukShUNAM mokShopAya-bhUtAnIti manvAnaH | sthitA nishcalA ahaM-brahmAsmi iti praj~nA yasya sa sthita-praj~no 'vasthA-dvayavAn samAdhistho vyutthita-cittash ceti | ato vishinaShTi samAdhi-sthasya sthita-praj~nasya kA bhAShA ? karmaNi ShaShThI | bhAShyate 'nayeti bhAShA lakShaNam | samAdhi-sthaH sthita-praj~naH kena lakShaNenAnyair vyavahriyata ity arthaH | 

sa ca vyutthita-cittaH sthita-dhIH sthita-praj~naH svayaM kiM prabhASheta ? stuti-nindAdAv abhinandana-dveShAdi-lakShaNaM kiM kathaM prabhASheta ? sarvatra sambhAvanAyAM liÇ | tathA kim AsIteti vyutthita-citta-nigrahAya kathaM bahir indriyANAM nigrahaM karoti ? tan-nigrAhAbhAva-kAle kiM vrajeta kathaM viShayAn prApnoti ? tat-kartR^ika-bhAShaNAsana-vrajanAni mUDha-jana-vilakShaNAni kIdR^ishAnIity arthaH | 

tad evaM catvAraH prashnAH samAdhi-sthe sthita-praj~na ekaH | vyutthite sthita-praj~ne traya iti | keshaveti sambodhayan sarvAntaryAmitayA tvam evaitAdR^ishaM rahasyaM vaktuM samartho 'sIti sUcayati ||54||

vishvanAthaH : samAdhAv acalA buddhir iti shrutvA tattvato yogino lakShaNaM pR^icchati sthita-praj~nasyeti | sthitA sthirAcalA praj~na buddhir yasyeti | kA bhAShA ? bhAShyate 'nayeti bhAShA lakShaNaM kiM lakShaNam ity arthaH | kIdR^ishasya samAdhi-sthasyeti samAdhau sthAsyatIti | asyArthaH - evaM ca sthita-praj~na iti | samAdhi-stha iti jIvan-muktasya saJNj~nA-dvayam | kiM prabhASheteti sukha-duHkhayor mAnApamAnayoH stuti-nindayoH sneha-dveShayor vA samupasthitayoH kiM prabhASheta ? spaShTaM svagataM vA kiM vaded ity arthaH | kim AsIta ? tad indriyANAM bAhya-viShayeShu calanAbhAvaH kIdR^ishaH ? vrajeta kim ? teShu calanaM vA kIdR^isham iti ||54||

baladevaH : evam ukto 'rjunaH pUrva-padyoktasya sthita-praj~nasya lakShaNaM j~nAtuM pR^icchati sthiteti | sthita-praj~ne 'tra catvAraH prashnAH - samAdhisthe ekaH, vyutthite tu trayaH | tathA hi - sthitA sthirA praj~na dhIr yasya tasya samAdhi-sthasya kA bhAShA kiM lakShaNam ? bhAShyate 'nayeti vyutpatteH | kena lakShaNena sthita-praj~no 'bhidhIyata ity arthaH | tathA vyutthitaH sthita-praj~naH kathaM bhAShaNAdIni kuryAt ? tadIyAni tAni pR^ithag-jana-vilakShaNAni kIdR^ishAnIty arthaH | tatra kiM prabhASheta ? svayoH stuti-nindayoH sneha-dveShayosh ca prAptayor mukhataH svagataM vA kiM brUyAt ? kim AsIta bAhya-viShayeShu katham indriyANAM nigrahaM kuryAt ? vrajeta kim ? kiM tan-nigrAhAbhAve ca kathaM viShayAnavApnuyAd ity arthaH | triShu sambhAvanAyAm ||54||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.55

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca
prajahAti yadA kAmAn sarvAn pArtha mano-gatAn |
Atmany evAtmanA tuShTaH sthita-praj~nas tadocyate ||55||

shrIdharaH : atra ca yAni sAdhakasya j~nAna-sAdhanAni tAny eva svAbhAvikAni siddhasya lakShaNAni | ataH siddhasya lakShaNAni kathayann evAntaraN^gAni j~nAna-sAdhanAny Aha yAvad adhyAya-samApti | tatra prathama-prashnasyottaram Aha prajahAtIti dvAbhyAm | manasi sthitAn kAmAn yadA prakarSheNa jahAti | tyAge hetum Aha AtmanIti | Atmany eva svasminn eva paramAnanda-rUpe AtmanA svayam eva tuShTa ity AtmArAmaH san yadA kShudra-viShayAbhilAShAMs tyajati tadA tena lakShaNena muniH sthita-praj~na ucyate ||55||

madhusUdanaH : eteShAM catUrNAM prashnAnAM krameNottaraM bhagavAn uvAca prajahAtIti yAvad-adhyAya-samApti | kAmAn kAma-saN^kalpAdIn mano-vR^itti-visheShAn pramANa-viparyaya-vikalpa-nidrA-smR^iti-bhedena tantrAntare pa¤cadhA prapa¤citAn sarvAn niravasheShAn prakarSheNa kAraNa-bAdhena yadA jahAti parityajati sarva-vR^itti-shUnya eva yadA bhavati sthita-praj~nas tadocyate samAdhistha iti sheShaH | kAmAnAm anAtma-dharmatvena parityAga-yogyatAm Aha manogatAn iti | yadi hy Atma-dharmAH syus tadA na tyaktuM shakyeran vahny-auShNyavat svAbhAvikatvAt | manasas tu dharmA ete | atas tat-parityAgena parityaktuaM shakyA evety arthaH | 
nanu sthita-praj~nasya mukha-prasAda-liN^ga-gamyaH santoSha-visheShaH pratIyate sa kathaM sarva-kAma-parityAge syAd ity Aha - Atmany eva paramAnanda-rUpe na tv anAtmani tuccha AtmnaA svaprakAsha-cid-rUpeNa bhAsamAnena na tu vR^ittyA tuShTaH paritR^iptaH parama-puruShArtha-lAbhAt | tathA ca shrutiH -

     yadA sarve pramucyante kAmA ye 'sya hR^idi shritAH |
atha martyo 'mR^ito bhavaty atra brahma samashnute || [KaThU 2.3.14] iti | 

tathA ca samAdhi-sthaH sthita-praj~na evaMvidhair lakShaNa-vAcibhiH shabdair bhAShyata iti prathama-prashnasyottaram ||55||

vishvanAthaH : catUrNAM prashnAnAM krameNottaram Aha prajahAtIti yAvad adhyAya-samAptiH | sarvAn iti kasminn apy arthe yasya kiMcin mAtro 'pi nAbhilASha ity arthaH | mano-gatAn iti kAmAnAm Atma-dharmatvena parityAge yogyatA darshitA | yadi te hy Atma-dharmAH syus tadA tAMs tyaktum ashakyeran vahner auShNyavad iti bhAvaH | tatra hetuH - Atmani pratyAhR^ite manasi prApto ya AtmAnanda-rUpas tena tuShTaH | tathA ca shrutiH -

yadA sarve pramucyante kAmA ye 'sya hR^idi shritAH |
atha martyo 'mR^ito bhavaty atra brahma samashnute || [KaThU 2.3.14] iti ||55||

baladevaH : evaM pR^iShTo bhagavAn krameNa catUrNAM uttaram Aha yAvad adhyAya-pUrtiH | tatra prathamasyAha prajahAtIty ekena | he pArtha ! yadA mano-gatAn manasi sthitAn kAmAn sarvAn prajahAti saMtyajati tadA sthita-praj~na ucyate | kAmAnAm mano-dharmatvAt parityAgo yuktaH | Atma-dharmatve duHshakyaH sa syAd vahny-uShNatAdInAm iveti bhAvaH | 

nanu shuShka-kAShThavat kathaM tiShThatIti cet tatrAha Atmany eveti | Atmani pratyAhR^ite manasi bhAsamAnena sva-prakAshAnanda-rUpeNAtmanA svarUpeNa tuShTaH paritR^iptaH kShudra-viShayAbhilAShAn saMtyajyAtmAnandArAmaH samAdhisthaH sthita-praj~na ity arthaH | 

     AtmA puMsi svabhAve 'pi prayanta-manasor api |
     dhR^itAv api manIShAyAM sharIra-brahmaNor api || iti medinI-kAraH |

brahma cAtra jIveshvarAnyatarad-grAhyam ||55||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.56

duHkheShv anudvigna-manAH sukheShu vigata-spR^ihaH |
vIta-rAga-bhaya-krodhaH sthita-dhIr munir ucyate ||56||

shrIdharaH : kiM ca duHkheShv iti | duHkheShu prApteShv api anudvignam akShubhitaM mano yasya saH | sukheShu vigatA spR^ihA yasya saH | tatra hetuH - vItA apagatA rAga-bhaya-krodhA yasmAt | tatra rAgaH prItiH | sa muniH sthita-dhIr ucyate ||56||

madhusUdanaH : idAnIM vyutthitasya sthita-praj~nasya bhAShaNopaveshana-gamanAni mUDha-jana-vilakShaNAni vyAkhyeyAni | tatra kiM prabhAShetety asyottaram Aha duHkheShv iti dvyAbhyAm | duHkhAni trividhAni shoka-moha-jvara-shiro-rogAdi-nimittAny AdhyAtmikAni vyAghra-sarpAdi-prayuktAny AdhibhautikAni ativAtAtivR^iShTy-Adi-hetukAny AdhidaivikAni teShu duHkheShu rajaH-pariNAma-santApAtmaka-citta-vR^itti-visheSheShu prArabdha-pApa-karma-prApiteShu nodvignaM duHkha-parihArAkShamatayA vyAkulaM na bhavati mano yasya so 'nudvigna-manAH | avivekino hi duHkha-prAptau satyAm aho pApo 'haM dhiÇ mAM durAtmAnam etAdR^isha-duHkha-bhAginaM ko me duHkham IdR^ishaM nirAkuryAd ity anutApAtmako bhrAnti-rUpas tAmasash citta-vR^itti-visheSha udvegAkhyo jAyate | yady ayaM pApAnuShThAna-samaye syAt tadA tat-pravR^itti-pratibandhakatvena saphalaH syAt | bhoga-kAle tu bhavan kAraNe sati kAryasyocchettum ashakyatvAn niShprayojano duHkha-kAraNe saty api kim iti mama duHkhaM jAyate iti avivekaja-bhrama-rUpatvAn na vivekinaH sthita-praj~nasya sambhavati | duHkha-mAtraM hi prArabdha-karmaNA prApyate na tu tad-uttara-kAlIno bhramo 'pi |

nanu duHkhAntara-kAraNatvAt so 'pi prArabdha-karmAntareNa prApyatAm iti cet, na | sthita-praj~nasya bhramopAdAnAj~nAna-nAshena bhramAsambhavaAt taj-janya-duHkha-prApaka-prArabdhAbhAvAt | yathA-kathaMcid deha-yAtrA-mAtra-nirvAhaka-prArabdha-karma-phalasya bhramAbhAve 'pi bAdhitAnuvR^ittyopapatter iti vistareNAgre vakShyate |

tathA sukheShu sattva-pariNAma-rUpa-prItyAtmaka-citta-vR^itti-visheSheShu trividheShu prArabdha-puNya-karma-prApiteShu vigata-spR^iha AgAmi-taj-jAtIya-sukha-spR^ihA-rahitaH | spR^ihA hi nAma sukhAnubhava-kAle taj-jAtIya-sukhasya kAraNaM dharmam ananuShThAya vR^ithaiva tad-AkAN^kShA-rUpA tAmasI citta-vR^ittir bhrAntir eva | sA cAvivekina eva jAyate | na hi kAraNAbhAve kAryaM bhavitum arhati | ato yathA sati kAraNe kAryaM mA bhUd iti vR^ithAkAN^kShA-rUpa udvego vivekino na sambhavati tathaivAsati kAraNe kAryaM bhUyAd iti vR^ithAkAN^kShA-rUpA tR^iShNAtmikA spR^ihApi nopapadyate prArabdha-karmaNaH sukha-mAtra-prApakatvAt | 

harShAtmikA vA citta-vR^ittiH spR^ihA-shabdenoktA | sApi bhrAntir eva | aho dhanyo 'haM yasya mamedR^ishaM sukham upasthitaM ko vA mayA tulas tribhuvane kena vopAyena mamedR^ishaM sukhaM na vicchidyetety evam AtmikotphullatA-rUpA tAmasI citta-vR^ittiH | ataevoktaM bhAShye - nAgnir ivendhanAdy-AdhAne yaH sukhAny anuvivardhate sa vigata-spR^ihaH iti | vakShyati ca -- na prahR^iShyet priyaM prApya nodvijet prApya cApriyam [GItA 5.20] iti | sApi na vivekinaH sambhavati bhrAntitvAt | 

tathA vIta-rAga-bhaya-krodhaH | rAgaH shobhanAdhyAsa-nibandhano viShayeShu ra¤janAtmakash citta-vR^itti-visheSho 'tyantAbhinivesha-rUpaH | rAga-viShayasya nAshake samupasthite tan-nivAraNAsAmarthyam Atmano manyamAnasya dainyAtmakash citta-vR^itti-visheSho bhayam | evaM rAga-viShaya-vinAshake samupasthite tan-nivAraNa-sAmarthyam Atmano manyamAnasyAbhijvalanAtmakash citta-vR^itti-visheShaH krodhaH | te sarve viparyaya-rUpatvAd vigatA yasmAt sa tathA | etAdR^isho munir manana-shIlaH saMnyAsI sthita-praj~na ucyate | evaM-lakShaNaH sthita-dhIH svAnubhava-prakaTanena shiShya-shikShArtham anudvega-nispR^ihatvAdi-vAcaH prabhASheta ity anvaya uktaH | evaM cAnyo 'pi mumukShur duHkhe nodvijet sukhe na prahR^iShyet, rAga-bhaya-krodha-rahitash ca bhaved ity abhiprAyaH ||56||

vishvanAthaH : kiM prabhAShetety asya uttaram Aha duHkheShu kShut-pipAsa-jvara-shiro-rogAdiShv AdhyAtmikeShu sarpa-vyAghrAdy-utthiteShv anudvigna-manAH prArabdhaM duHkham idaM mayAvashyaM bhoktavyam iti svagataM kenacit pR^iShTaH san spaShTaM ca bruvan | na duHkheShUdvijata ity arthaH | tasya tAdR^isha-mukha-vikriyAbhAva evAnudvega-liN^gaM sudhiyA gamyam | kR^itrimAnudvega-liN^gavAMs tu kapaTI | sudhiyA paricito bhraShTa evocyata iti bhAvaH | evaM sukheShv apy upasthiteShu vigata-spR^iha iti prArabdham idam avashya-bhogyam iti svagataM spaShTaM ca bruvANasya tasya sukha-spR^ihA-rAhitya-liN^gaM sudhiyA gamyam eveti bhAvaH | tat-tal-liN^gam eva spaShTIkR^itya darshayati vIto vigato rAgo 'nurAgaH sukheShu bandhu-janeShu yasya saH | yathaivAdi-bharatasya devyAH pArshvaM prApitasya svaccheda-cikIrShor vR^iShala-rAjAn na bhayam | nApi tatra krodho 'bhUd iti ||56||

baladevaH : atha vyutthitaH sthita-praj~naH kiM bhAShetety asyottaram Aha duHkheShv iti dvyAbhyAm | trividheShv adhyAtmikAdiShu duHkheShu samutthiteShu satsv anudvigna-manAH prArabdha-phalAny amUni mayAvashyaM bhoktavyAnIti kenacit pR^iShTaH svagataM vA bruvan tebhyo nodvijata ity arthaH | sukheShu cottamAhAra-satkArAdinA samupasthiteShu vigata-spR^ihas tR^iShNA-shUnyaH prArabdhAkR^iShTAny amUni mayAvashya-bhoktavyAnIti kenacit pR^iShTaM svagataM vA bruvan tair upasthitaH prahR^iShTa-mukho na bhavatIty arthaH | vIteti - vIta-rAgaH kamanIyeShu prIti-shUnyaH | vIta-bhayaH viShayApahartR^iShu prApteShu durlabhasya mamaitAni dharmyair bhavadbhir hriyanta iti dainya-shUnyaH | vIta-krodhaH teShv eva prabalasya mamaitAni tucchair bhavadbhiH katham apahartavyAnIti krodha-shUnyash ca | evaMvidho munir Atma-manana-shIlaH sthita-praj~na ity arthaH | itthaM svAnubhavaM parAn prati svagataM vA vadan naudvego nispR^ihatAdi-vacaH prabhAShate ity uttaram ||56||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.57

yaH sarvatrAnabhisnehas tat tat prApya shubhAshubham |
nAbhinandati na dveShTi tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA ||57||

shrIdharaH : kathaM bhASheta ity asyottaram Aha ya iti | yaH sarvatra putra-mitrAdiShv apy anabhisnehaH sneha-varjitaH | ataeva bAdhitAnuvR^ittyA tat tat shubham anukUlaM prApya nAbhinandati ashubhaM pratikUlaM prApya na dveShTi na nindati | kintu kevalam udAsIna eva bhAShate | tasya praj~nA pratiShThitety arthaH ||57||

madhusUdanaH : kiM ca | sarva-deheShu jIvanAdiShv api yo munir anabhisnehaH, yasmin saty anyadIye hAni-vR^iddhI svasminn Aropyete sa tAdR^isho 'nya-viShayaH premApara-paryAyas tAmaso vR^itti-visheShaH snehaH sarva-prakAreNa tad-rahito 'nabhisnehaH | bhagavati paramAtmani tu sarvathAbhisnehavAn bhaved eva | anAtman-snehAbhAvasya tad-arthatvAd iti draShTavyam |

tat-tat-prArabdha-karma-pariprApitaM shubhaM sukha-hetuM viShayaM prApya nAbhinandati harSha-visheSha-puraHsaraM na prashaMsati | ashubhaM duHkha-hetuM viShayaM prApya na dveShTi antar-asUyA-pUrvakaM na nindati | aj~nasya hi sukha-hetur yaH sva-kalatrAdiH sa shubho viShayas tad-guNa-kathanAdi-pravartikA dhI-vR^ittir bhrAnti-rUpAbhinandaH | sa ca tAmasaH, tad-guNa-kathanAdeH para-prarocanArthatvAbhAvena vyarthatvAt | evam asUyotpAdanena duHkha-hetuH parakIya-vidyA-prakarShAdir enaM pratyashubho viShayas tan-nindAdi-pravartikA bhrAnti-rUpA dhI-vR^itti-visheShaH | so 'pi tAmasaH | tan-nindAyA nivAraNArthatvAbhAvena vyarthatvAt | tAv abhinanda-dveShau bhrAnti-rUpau tAmasau katham abhrAnte shuddha-sattve sthita-praj~ne sambhavatAm | tasmAd vicAlakAbhAvAt tasyAnabhisnehasya harSha-viShAda-rahitasya muneH praj~nA paramAtma-tattva-viShayA pratiShThitA phala-paryavasAyinI sa sthita-praj~na ity arthaH | evam anyo 'pi mumukShuH sarvatrAnabhisneho bhavet | shubhaM prApya na prashaMset, ashubhaM prApya na ninded ity abhiprAyaH | atra ca nindA-prashaMsAdi-rUpA vAco na prabhASheteti vyatireka uktaH ||57||

vishvanAthaH : anabhisnehaH sopAdhi-sneha-shUnyo dayAlutvAn nirupAdhir IShan-mAtra-snehas tu tiShThed eva | tat tat prasiddhaM sammAna-bhojanAdibhyaH sva-paricaraNaM shubhaM prApyAshubham anAdaraNaM muShTi-prahArAdikaM ca prApya krameNa nAbhinandati | na prashaMsati tvaM dhArmikaH paramahaMsa-sevI sukhI bhaveti na brUte | na dveShTi tvaM pApAtmA narake pateti nAbhishapati | tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA samAdhiM prati sthitA susthira-praj~nA ucyata ity arthaH ||57||

baladevaH : ya iti sarveShu prANiShu anabhisneha aupAdhika-sneha-shUnyaH | kAruNikatvAn nirupAdhir IShad-snehas tv asty eva | tat tat prasiddhaM shubham uttama-bhojana-srak-candanArpaNa-rUpaM prApya nAbhinandati tad-arpakaM prati dharmiShThas tvaM ciraM jIveti na vadati | ashubham apamAnaM yaShTi-prahArAdikaM ca prApya na dveShTi, pApiShThas tvaM miryasveti nAbhishapati | tasya praj~neti sa sthita-praj~na ity arthaH | atra stuti-nindA-rUpaM vaco na bhAShata iti vyatirekeNa tal lakShaNam ||57||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.58

yadA saMharate cAyaM kUrmo 'N^gAnIva sarvashaH |
indriyANIndriyArthebhyas tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA ||58||

shrIdharaH : kiM ca yadeti | yadA cAyaM yogI indriyArthebhyaH shabdAdibhyaH sakAshAd indriyANi saMharate sarvata evaM j~nAna-niShTha indriyANInidryArthebhyaH sarva-viShayebhyaH upasaMharate | tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA | ity uktArthaM vAkyam ||58|| 

madhusUdanaH : idAnIM kim AsIteti prashnasyottaraM vaktum Arabhate bhagavAn ShaDbhiH shlokaiH | tatra prArabdha-karma-vashAd vyutthAnena vikShiptAnIndriyANi punar upasaMhR^itya samAdhy-artham eva sthita-praj~nasyopaveshanam iti darshayitum Aha yadeti | ayaM vyutthitaH sarvashaH sarvANIndriyArthebhyaH shabdAdibhyaH sarvebhyaH | caH punar-arthe | yadA saMharate punar upasaMharati saN^kocayati | tatra dR^iShTAntaH kUrmo 'N^gAnIva | tadA tasya praj~nAH pratiShThiteti spaShTam | pUrva-shlokAbhyAM vyutthAna-dashAyAm api sakala-tAmasa-vR^itty-abhAva uktaH | adhunA tu punaH samAdhy-avasthAyAM sakala-vR^itty-abhAva iti visheShaH ||58||

vishvanAthaH : kim AsItety asyottaram Aha yadeti | indriyArthebhyaH shabdAdibhya indriyANi shrotrAdIni saMharate | svAdhInAnAm indriyANAM bAhya-viShayeShu calanaM niShidhyAntareva nishcalatayA sthApanaM sthita-praj~nasyAsanam ity arthaH | tatra dR^iShTAntaH | kUrmo 'N^gAni mukha-netrAdIni yathA svAntar eva svecchayA sthApayati ||58||

baladevaH : atha kim AsItety asyottaram Aha yadety AdibhiH ShaDbhir | ayaM yogI yadA cendriyArthebhyaH shabdAdibhyaH svAdhInAnIndriyANi shrotrAdIny anAyAsena saMharati samAkarShati tadA tasya praj~nA pratiShThitety anvayaH | atra dR^iShTAntaH kUrmo 'N^gAnIveti | mukha-kara-caraNAni yathAnAyasena kamaThaH saMharati tadvat viShayebhyaH samAkR^iShTendriyANAm antaH-sthApanaM sthita-praj~nasyAsanam ||58||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.59

viShayA vinivartante nirAhArasya dehinaH |
rasa-varjaM raso 'py asya paraM dR^iShTvA nivartate ||59||

shrIdharaH : nanu nendriyANAM viShayeShv apravR^ittir sthita-praj~nasya lakShaNaM bhavitum arhati | jaDAnAm AturANAm upavAsa-parANAM ca viShayeShv pravR^itter avisheShAt | tatrAha viShayA iti | indriyAir viShayANAm AharaNaM grahaNam AhAraH | nirAhArasya indriyAir viShaya-grahaNam akurvato dehino dehAbhimAnino 'j~nasya rAgo 'bhilAShas tad-varjaM | abhilAShasya na nivartata ity arthaH | yad vA nirAhArasya upavAsa-parasya viShayAH prAyasho nivartante kShudhA-santaptasya shabda-sparshAdy-apekShAbhAvAt, kintu rasa-varjaM rasApekShA tu na nivartata ity arthaH | sheShaM samAnam ||59|| 

madhusUdanaH : nanu mUDhasyApi rogAdi-vashAd viShayebhya indriyANAm upasaMharaNaM bhavati tat kathaM tasya praj~nA pratiShThitety uktam ? ata Aha viShayA iti | nirAhArasya indriyAir indriyAir viShayAn anAharato dehino dehAbhimAnavato mUDhasyApi rogiNaH kAShTha-tapasvino vA viShayAH shabdAdayo vinivartante kintu rasa-varjaM rasa-tR^iShNA taM varjayitvA | aj~nasya viShayA nivartante tad-viShayo rAgas tu na nivartata ity arthaH | asya tu sthita-praj~nasya paraM puruShArthaM dR^iShTvA tad evAham asmIti sAkShAtkR^itya sthitasya raso 'pi kShudra-sukha-rAgo 'pi nivartate | api-shabdAd viShayAsh ca | tathA ca yAvAn artha ity Adau vyAkhyAtam | evaM ca sa-rAga-viShaya-nivR^ittiH sthita-praj~na-lakShaNam iti na mUDhe vyabhicAra ity arthaH | yasmAn nAsati paramAtma-samyag-darshane sa-rAga-viShayocchedas tasmAt sa-rAga-viShayocchedikAyAH samyag-darshanAtmikAyAH praj~nAyAH sthairyaM mahatA yatnena sampAdayed ity abhiprAyaH ||59||

vishvanAthaH : mUDhasyApi upavAsato rogAdi-vashAd vendriyANAM viShayeShv acalanaM sambhavet tatrAha viShayA iti | rasa-varjaM raso rAgo 'bhilAShas taM varjayitvA | abhilAShas tu viShayeShu na nivartanta ity arthaH | asya sthita-praj~nasya tu paraM paramAtmAnaM dR^iShTvA viShayeShv abhilASho nivartata iti na lakShaNa-vyabhicAraH | Atma-sAkShAtkAra-samarthasya tu sAdhakatvam eva, na tu siddhatvam iti bhAvaH ||59||

baladevaH : nanu mUDhasyAmaya-grastasya viShayeShv indriyApravR^itti-dR^iShTA tat katham etat sthita-praj~nasya lakShaNaM tatrAha viShayA iti | nirAhArasya roga-bhayAd bhojanAdIny akurvato mUDhasyApi dehino janasya viShayAs tad-anubhavA vinivartante | kintu raso rAga-tR^iShNA tad-varjaM viShaya-tR^iShNA tu na nivartata ity arthaH | asya sthita-praj~nasya tu raso 'pi viShaya-rAgo 'pi viShayebhyaH paraM sva-prakAshAnandam AtmAnaM dR^iShTvAnubhUya nivartate vinashyatIti sa-rAga-viShaya-nivR^ittis tasya lakShaNam iti na vyabhicAraH ||59||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.60

yatato hy api kaunteya puruShasya vipashcitaH |
indriyANi pramAthIni haranti prasabhaM manaH ||60||

shrIdharaH : indriya-saMyamaM vinA sthita-praj~natA na sambhavati | ataH sAdhakAvasthAyAM tatra mahAn prayatnaH kartavya ity Aha yatato hy apIti dvAbhyAm | yatato mokShArthaM prayatamAnasya | vipashcito vivekino 'pi | mana indriyANi prasabhaM balAd haranti | yataH pramAthIni pramathana-shIlAni kShobhakAnIty arthaH ||60||

madhusUdanaH : tatra praj~nA-sthairye bAhyendriya-nigraho mano-nigrahash cAsAdhAraNaM kAraNaM tad-ubhayAbhAve praj~nA-nAsha-darshanAd iti vaktuM bAhyendriya-nigrahAbhAve prathamaM doSham Aha yatata iti | he kaunteya ! 

yatato bhUyo bhUyo viShaya-doSha-darshanAtmakaM yatnaM kurvato 'pi, cakShiÇo Çitva-karaNAd anudAtteto 'nAvashyakam Atmanepadam iti j~nApanAt parasmaipadam aviruddham | vipashcito 'tyanta-vivekino 'pi puruShasya manaH kShaNa-mAtraM nirvikAraM kR^itam apIndriyANi haranti vikAraM prApayanti | 

nanu virodhinI viveke sati kuto vikAra-prAptis tatrAha pramAthIni pramathana-shIlAni atibalIyastvAd vivekopamardana-kShamANi | ataH prasabhaM prasahya balAtkAreNa pashyaty eva vipashciti svAmini viveke ca rakShake sati sarva-pramAthItvAd evendriyANi vivekaja-praj~nAyAM praviShTaM manas tataH pracyAvya sva-viShayAviShTatvena harantIty arthaH | hi-shabdaH prasiddhiM dyotayati | prasiddho hy ayam artho loke yathA pramAthino dasyavaH prasabham eva dhaninaM dhana-rakShakaM cAbhibhUya tayoH pashyator eva dhanaM haranti tathendriyANy api viShaya-sannidhAne mano harantIti ||60||

vishvanAthaH : sAdhakAvasthAyAM tu yatna eva mahAn, na tv indriyANi parAvartayituM sarvathA shaktir ity Aha yatata iti | pramAthIni pramathana-shIlAni kShobhakAnIty arthaH ||60||

baladevaH : athAsyA j~nAna-niShThayA daurlabhyam Aha yatato hIti | vipashcito viShayAtma-svarUpa-vivekaj~nasya tata indriya-jaye prayatamAnasyApi puruShasya indriyANi shrotrAdIni kartÌNi manaH parasabhaM balAd iva haranti | hR^itvA viShaya-pravaNaM kurvantIty arthaH | nanu virodhini viveka-j~nAne sthite kathaM haranti tatrAha pramAthInIti ati-baliShThatvAt taj-j~nAnopamardana-kShamANIty arthaH | tasmAt caurebhyo mahA-nidher ivendriyebhyo j~nAna-niShThAyAH saMrakShaNaM sthita-praj~nasyAsanam iti ||60||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.61

tAni sarvANi saMyamya yukta AsIta mat-paraH |
vashe hi yasyendriyANi tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA ||61||

shrIdharaH : yasmAd evaM tasmAt tAnIti | yukto yogI tAni indriyANi saMyamya mat-paraH sann AsIta | yasya vashe vashavartinIndriyANi | etena ca katham AsIteti prashnasya vashIkR^itendriyaH sann AsIteti ||61||

madhusUdanaH : evaM tarhi tatra kaH pratIkAra ity ata Aha tAnIti | tAnIndriyANi sarvANi j~nAna-karma-sAdhana-bhUtAni saMyamya vashIkR^itya yuktaH samAhito nigR^ihIta-manAH sann AsIta nirvApAras tiShThet | pramAthinAM kathaM sva-vashIkaraNam iti cet tatrAha mat-para iti | ahaM sarvAtmA vAsudeva eva para utkR^iShTa upAdeyo yasya sa mat-para ekAnta-mad-bhakta ity arthaH | tathA coktam na vAsudeva-bhaktAnAm ashubhaM vidyate kvacit iti | yathA hi loke balavantaM rAjAnam Ashritya dasyavo nigR^ihyante rAjAshrito 'yam iti j~nAtvA ca svayam eva tad-vashyA bhavanti tathaiva bhagavantaM sarvAntaryAminam Ashritya tat-prabhAveNaiva duShTAnIndriyANi nigrAhyANi punash ca bhagavad-Ashrito 'yam iti matvA tAni tad-vashyAny eva bhavantIti bhAvaH | yathA ca bhagavad-bhakter mahA-prabhAvatvaM tathA vistareNAgre vyAkhyAsyAmaH | indriya-vashIkAre phalam Aha vashe hIti | spaShTam | tad etad vashIkR^itendriyaH sann AsIteti kim AsIteti prashnasyottaram uktaM bhavati ||61||

vishvanAthaH : mat-paro mad-bhakta iti | mad-bhaktiM vinA naivendriya-jaya ity agrima-granthe 'pi sarvatra draShTavyam | yad uktam uddhavena - 

prAyashaH puNDarIkAkSha yu¤janto yogino manaH |
viShIdanty asamAdhAnAn mano-nigraha-karshitAH |
athAta Ananda-dughaM padAmbujaM haMsAH shrayeran || [BhP 11.29.1-2] iti |

vashe hIti sthita-praj~nasyendriyANi vashIbhUtAni bhavantIti sAdhakAd visheSha uktaH ||61||

baladevaH : nanu nirjitendriyANAm apy AtmAnubhavo na pratItas tatra ko 'bhyupAya iti cet tatrAha tAnIti | tAni sarvANi saMyamya mat-paro man-niShThaH san yuktaH kR^itAma-samAdhir AsIta tiShTheta | mad-bhakti-prabhAvena sarvendriya-vijaya-pUrvikA svAtma-dR^iShTiH sulabheti bhAvaH | evaM smaranti -

yathAgnir uddhata-shikhaH kakShaM dahati sAnilaH | 
tathA citta-sthito viShNur yoginAM sarva-kilbiSham || [ViP 6.7.74] ity Adi | 

vashe hIti spaShTam | itthaM ca vashIkR^itendriyatayAvasthitiH kim AsItety asyottaram uktam ||61||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.62-63

dhyAyato viShayAn puMsaH saN^gas teShUpajAyate |
saN^gAt saJNjAyate kAmaH kAmAt krodho 'bhijAyate ||62||
krodhAd bhavati saMmohaH saMmohAt smR^iti-vibhramaH |
smR^iti-bhraMshAd buddhi-nAsho buddhi-nAshAt praNashyati ||63||

shrIdharaH : bAhyendriya-saMyamAbhAve doSham uktvA manaH-saMyamAbhAve doSham Aha dhyAyata iti dvAbhyAm | guNa-buddhyA viShayAn dhyAyataH puMsaH teShu saN^ga Asaktir bhavati | AsaktyA ca teShu adhikaH kAmo bhavati | kAmAc ca kenacit pratihatAt krodho bhavati | kiM ca, krodhAd iti | krodhAt saMmohaH kAryAkArya-vivekAbhAvaH | tataH shAstrAcAryopadiShTa-smR^iter vibhramo vicalanaM bhraMshaH | tato buddhesh cetanAyA nAshaH | vR^ikShAdiShv ivAbhibhavaH | tataH praNashyati mR^ita-tulyo bhavati ||62-63||

madhusUdanaH : nigR^ihIta-bAhyendriyasyApi shabdAdInviShayAn dhyAyato manasA punaH punash cintayataH puMsas teShu viShayeShu saN^ga AsaN^go mamAtyantaM sukha-hetava eta ity evaM shobhanAdhyAsa-lakShaNaH prIti-visheSha upajAyate saN^gAt sukha-hetutva-j~nAna-lakShaNAt saJNjAyate kAmo mamaite bhavantv iti tR^iShNA-visheShaH | tasmAt kAmAt kutashcit pratihanyamAnAt tat-pratighAta-viShayaH krodho 'bhijvalanAtmAbhijAyate | krodhAd bhavati saMmohaH kAryAkArya-vivekAbhAva-rUpaH | saMmohAt smR^iti-vibhramaH smR^iteH shAstrAcAryopadiShTArthAnusandhAnasya vibhramo vicalanaM vibhraMshaH | tasmAc ca smR^iti-bhraMshAd buddher aikAtmyAkAra-mano-vR^itter nAsho viparIta-bhAvanopacaya-doSheNa pratibandhAd anutpattir utpannAyAsh ca phalAyogyatvena vilayaH | buddhi-nAshAt praNashyati tasyAsh ca phala-bhUtAyA buddher vilopAt praNashyati sarva-puruShArthAyogyo bhavati | yo hi puruShArthAyogyo jAtaH sa mR^ita eveti loke vyavahriyate | ataH praNashyatIty uktam | yasmAd evaM manaso nigrahAbhAve nigR^ihIta-bAhyendriyasyApi paramAnartha-prAptis taramAn mahatA prayatnena mano nigR^ihNIyAd ity abhiprAyaH | ato yuktam uktaM tAni sarvANi saMyamya yukta AsIteti ||62-63||

vishvanAthaH : sthita-praj~nasya mano-vashIkAra eva bAhyendriya-vashIkAra-kAraNaM sarvathA mano-vashIkArAbhAve tu yat syAt tat shR^iNv ity Aha dhyAyata iti | saN^ga AsaktiH | AsaktyA ca teShv adhikaH kAmo 'bhilAShaH | kAmAc ca kenacit pratihatAt krodhaH | krodhAt saMmohaH kAryAkArya-vivekAbhAvaH | tasmAc ca shAstropadiShTa-svArthasya smR^iti-nAshaH | tasmAc ca buddheH sad-vyavasAyasya nAshaH | tataH praNashyati saMsAra-kUpe patati ||62-63||

baladevaH : vijitendriyasyApi mayy aniveshita-manasaH punar anartho durvAra ity Aha dhyAyata iti dvyAbhyAm | viShayAn shabdAdIn sukha-hetutva-buddhyA dhyAyataH punaH punash cintayato yoginas teShu saN^ga Asaktir bhavati | saN^gAd dhetos teShu kAma-tR^iShNA jAyate | kAmAc ca kenacit pratihatAt krodhash citta-jvAlas tat-pratighAtako bhavati | krodhAt saMmohaH kAryAkArya-viveka-vij~nAna-vilopaH | saMmohAt smR^iter indriya-vijayAdi-prayatnAnusandher vibhramo vibhraMshaH | smR^iti-bhraMshAd buddher Atma-j~nAnArthakasyAdhyavasAyasya nAshaH | buddhi-nAshAt praNashyati punar viShaya-bhoga-nimagno bhavati saMsaratIty arthaH | madanAshrayaNAd durbalaM manas tAni sva-viShayair yojayantIti bhAvaH | tathA ca mano-vijigIShuNA mad-upAsanaM vidheyam ||62-63||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.64

rAga-dveSha-viyuktais tu viShayAn indriyaish caran |
Atma-vashyair vidheyAtmA prasAdam adhigacchati ||64||

shrIdharaH : nanv indriyANAM viShaya-pravaNa-svabhAvAnAM niroddhum ashakyatvAd ayaM doSho duShparihara iti sthita-praj~natvaM kathaM syAt ? ity AshaN^kyAha rAga-dveSha iti dvAbhyAm | rAga-dveSha-rahitaiH vigata-darpair indriyaiH viShayAMsh carann upabhu¤jAno 'pi prasAdaM shAntiM prApnoti | rAga-dveSha-rAhityam evAha Atmeti | Atmano manasaH vashyair indriyaiH vidheyo vashavartI AtmA mano yasyeti | anenaiva kathaM vrajetety asya caturtha-prashnasya svAdhInair indriyair viShayAn gacchatIty uttaram uktaM bhavati ||64||
