madhusUdanaH : manasi nigR^ihIte tu bAhyendriya-nigrahAbhAve 'pi na doSha iti vadan kiM vrajetety asyottaram AhAShTabhiH | yo 'samAhita-cetAH sa bAhyendriyANi nigR^ihyApi rAga-dveSha-duShTena manasA viShayAMsh cintayan puruShArthAd bhraShTo bhavati | vidheyAtmA tu tu-shabdhaH pUrvasmAd vyatirekArthaH | vashIkR^itAntaH-karaNas tu Atma-vashyair mano 'dhInaiH svAdhInair iti vA rAga-dveShAbhyAM viyuktair virahitair indriyaiH shrotrAdibhir viShayAn shabdAdIn aniShiddhAMsh carann upalabhamAnaH prasAdaM prasannAtAM cittasya svacchatAM paramAtma-sAkShAtkAra-yogyatAm adhigacchati | rAga-dveSha-prayuktAnIndriyANi doSha-hetutAM pratipadyante | manasi sva-vashe tu na rAga-dveShau | tayor abhAve ca na tad-adhInendriya-pravR^ittiH | avarjanIyatayA tu viShayopalambho na doSham AvahatIti na shuddhi-vyAghAta iti bhAvaH |

etena viShayANAM smaraNam api ced anartha-kAraNaM sutarAM tarhi bhogas tena jIvanArthaM viShayAn bhu¤jAnaH katham anarthaM na pratipadyeteti shaN^kA nirastA | svAdhInair indriyair viShayAn prApnotIti ca kiM vrajeteti prashnasyottaram uktaM bhavati ||64||

vishvanAthaH : mAnasa-viShaya-grahaNAbhAve sati sva-vashyair indriyair viShaya-grahaNe 'pi na doSha iti vadan sthita-praj~no vrajeta kim ity asyottaram Aha rAgeti | vidheyo vacane sthta AtmA mano yasya saH | 

     vidheyo vinaya-grAhI vacane sthita AshravaH |
     vashyaH praNayo nibhR^ita-vinIta-prashritAH || ity amaraH |

prasAdam adhigacchatIty etAdR^ishasyAdhikAriNo viShaya-grahaNam api na doSha iti kiM vaktavyam ? pratyuta guNa eveti | sthita-praj~nasya viShaya-tyAga-svIkArAv eva Asana-vrajane te ubhe api tasya bhadre iti bhAvaH ||64||

baladevaH : manasi nirjite shrotrAdi-nirjayAbhAvo 'pi na doSha iti bruvan vrajeta kim ity asottaram Aha rAgeti Adibhir aShTabhiH | vijita-bahir-indriyo 'pi mad-anarpita-manAH paramArthAd vicyuta ity uktam | yo vidheyAtmA svAdhIna-manA mad-arpita-manAs tata eva nidagdha-rAgAdi-mano-malaH sa tv Atma-vashyair mano 'dhInair ata eva rAga-dveShAbhyAM viyuktair indriyaiH shrotrAdyair viShayAn niShiddhAn shabdAdIMsh caran bhu¤jAno 'pi prasAdaM viShayAsakty-Adi-malAnAgamAd vimala-manas tam adhigacchatIty prApnotIty arthaH ||64||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.65

prasAde sarva-duHkhAnAM hAnir asyopajAyate |
prasanna-cetaso hy Ashu buddhiH paryavatiShThate ||65||

shrIdharaH : prasAde sati kiM syAd ity atrAha prasAda iti | prasAde sati sarva-duHkha-nAshaH | tatash ca prasanna-cetaso buddhiH pratiShThitA bhavatIty arthaH ||65||

madhusUdanaH : prasAdam adhigacchatIty uktaM tatra prasAde sati kiM syAd ity ucyate prasAda iti | cittasya prasAde svacchatva-rUpe sati sarva-duHkhAnAm AdhyAtmikAdInAm aj~nAna-vilasitAnAM hAnir vinAsho 'sya yater upajAyate | hi yasmAt prasanna-cetaso yater Ashu shIghram eva buddhir brahmAtmaikyAkArA paryavatiShThate pari samantAd avatiShThate sthirA bhavati viparIta-bhAvanAdi-pratibandhAbhAvAt | tatash ca prasAde sati buddhi-paryavasthAnaM tatas tad-virodhy-aj~nAna-nivR^ittiH | tatas tat-kArya-sakala-duHkha-hAnir iti krame 'pi prasAde yatrAdhikyAya sarva-duHkha-hAni-karatva-kathanam iti na virodhaH ||65||

vishvanAthaH : buddhiH paryavatiShThate sarvato-bhAvena svAbhIShTaMprati sthirI-bhavatIti viShaya-grahaNAbhAvAd api samucita-viShaya-grahaNaM tasya sukham iti bhAvaH | prasanna-cetaso iti citta-prasAdo bhaktyaiveti j~neyam | tayA vinA tu na citta-prasAda iti prathama-skandha eva prapa¤citam | kR^ita-vedAnta-shAstrasyApi vyAsasyAprasanna-cittasya shrI-nAradopadiShTayA bhaktyaiva citta-prasAda-dR^iShTeH ||65||

baladevaH : prasAde sati kiM syAd ity Aha asya yogino manaH prasAde sati sarveShAM prakR^iti-saMsarga-kR^itAnAM duHkhAnAM hAnir upajAyate | prasanna-cetasaH svAtma-yAthAtmya-viShayA buddhiH paryavatiShThate sthirA bhavati ||65||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.66

nAsti buddhir ayuktasya na cAyuktasya bhAvanA |
na cAbhAvayataH shAntir ashAntasya kutaH sukham ||66||

shrIdharaH : indriya-nigrahasya sthita-praj~natA-sAdhanatvaM vyatireka-mukhenopapAdayati nAstIti | ayuktasya avashI-kR^itendriyasya nAsti buddhiH | shAstrAcAryopadeshAbhyAm Atma-viShayA buddhiH praj~naiva notpadyate | kutas tasyAH pratiShThA-vArtA | kuta ity atrAha na ceti | na cAyuktasya bhAvanA dhyAnam | bhAvanayA hi buddher Atmani pratiShThA bhavati, sA ca ayuktasya yato nAsti | na cAbhAvayataH Atma-dhyAnam akurvataH shAntiH Atmani cittoparamaH | ashAntasya kutaH sukham mokShAnanda ity arthaH ||66||

madhusUdanaH : imam evArthaM vyatireka-mukhena draDhayati nAstIti | ayuktasyAjita-cittasya buddhir Atma-viShayA shravaNa-mananAkhya-vedAnta-vicAra-janyA nAsti notpadyate | tad-buddhy-abhAve na cAyuktasya bhAvanA nididhyAsanAtmikA vijAtIya-pratyayAnantaritasajAtIya-pratyaya-pravAha-rUpA | sarvatra na¤o 'stIty anenAnvayaH | na cAbhAvayata AtmAnaM shAntiH sakAryAvidyA-nivR^itti-rUpA vedAnta-vAkya-janyA brahmAtmaikya-sAkShAt-kR^itiH | ashAntasyAtma-sAkShAtkAra-shUnyasya kutaH sukhaM mokShAnanda ity arthaH ||66||

vishvanAthaH : uktam arthaM vyatireka-mukhena draDhayati nAstIti | ayuktasyAvashIkR^ita-manaso buddhir Atma-viShayiNI praj~nA nAsti | ayuktasya tAdR^isha-praj~nA-rahitasya bhAvanA parameshvara-dhyAnaM ca | abhAvayato 'kR^ita-dhyAnasya shAntir viShayoparamo nAsti | ashAntasya sukham AtmAnandaH ||66||

baladevaH : pUrvoktam arthaM vyatireka-mukhenAha ayuktasyAyogino mad-aniveshita-manaso buddhir ukta-lakShaNA nAsti na bhavati | ataeva tasya bhAvanA tAdR^ig-Atma-cintApi nAsti | tAdR^isham AtmAnam abhAvayataH shAntir viShaya-tR^iShNA-nivR^ittir nAsti | ashAntasya tat-tR^iShNAkulasya sukham sva-prakAshAnandAtmAnubhava-lakShaNaM kutaH syAt ||66||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.67

indriyANAM hi caratAM yan mano 'nuvidhIyate |
tad asya harati praj~nAM vAyur nAvam ivAmbhasi ||67||

shrIdharaH : nAsti buddhir ayuktasya [GItA 2.66] ity atra hetum Aha indriyANAm iti | indriyANAm avashIkR^itAnAM svairaM viShayeShu caratAM madhye yadaivaikam indriyaM mano 'nuvidhIyate |vashIkR^itaM sad-indriyeNa saha gacchati, tadaivaikam indriyasya manasaH puruShasya vA praj~nAM buddhiM harati viShaya-vikShiptAM karoti | kim uta vaktavyaM bahUni praj~nAM harantIti | yathA pramattasya karNadhArasya nAvaM vAyuH sarvataH paribhramayati tadvad iti ||67||

madhusUdanaH : ayuktasya kuto nAsti buddhir ity ata Aha indriyANAm iti | caratAM sva-viShayeShu sva-sva-viShayeShu pravartamAnAnAm avashIkR^itAnAm indriyANAM madhye yad ekam apIndriyam anulakShyIkR^itya mano vidhIyate preryate pravartate iti yAvat | karma-kartari la-kAraH | tat indriyam ekam api manasAnusR^itam asya sAdhakasya manaso vA praj~nAm Atma-viShayAM shAstrIyAM harati apanayati manasas tad-viShayAviShTatvAt | yadaikam apIndriyaM praj~nAM harati tadA sarvANi harantIti kim u vaktavyam ity arthaH | 

dR^iShTAntas tu spaShTaH | abhyasyeti vAyor naukA-haraNa-sAmarthyaM na bhuvIti sUcayitum ambhasIty uktam | evaM dArShTAntike 'py ambhaH-sthAnIye manash cA¤calye saty eva praj~nA-haraNa-sAmarthyam indriyasya na tu bhU-sthAnIye manaH-sthairya iti sUcitam ||67||

vishvanAthaH : ayuktasya buddhir nAstIty upapAdayati indriyANAM sva-sva-viShayeShu caratAM madhye yan mama ekam indriyam anuvidhIyate | puMsAM sarvendriyAnuvartiH kriyate, tad eva mano 'sya praj~nAM buddhiM harati | yathAmbhasi nIyamAnAM nAvaM pratikUlo vAyuH ||67||

baladevaH : man-niveshita-manaskatayeindriya-niyamanAbhAve doSham Aha indriyANAm iti | viShayeShu caratAm avijitAnAm indriyANAM madhye yad ekaM shrotraM vA cakShur vAnulakShyIkR^itya mano vidhIyate pravartate, tad ekam evendriyaM manasAnugatam asya pravartakasya praj~nAM viviktAtma-viShayAM haraty apanayati manasasas tad-viShayAkR^iShTatvAt | kiM punaH ? sarvANi tAnIti | pratikUlo vAyur yathAmbhasi nIyamAnAM nAvaM tadvat ||67||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.68

tasmAd yasya mahAbAho nigR^ihItAni sarvashaH |
indriyANIndriyArthebhyas tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA ||68||

shrIdharaH : indriya-saMyamasya sthita-praj~natve sAdhanatvaM coktam upasaMharati tasmAd iti | sAdhanatvopasaMhAre tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA j~nAtavyety arthaH | mahAbAho ! iti sambodhayan vairi-nigrahe samarthasya tavAtrApi sAmarthyaM bhaved iti sUcayati ||68||

madhusUdanaH : hi yasmAd evaM tasmAd iti | sarvashaH sarvANi samanaskAni | he mahAbAho iti sambodhayan sarva-shatru-nivAraNa-kShamatvAd indriya-shatru-nivAraNe 'pi tvaM kShamo 'sIti sUcayati | spaShTam anyat | tasyeti siddhasya sAdhakasya ca parAmarshaH | indriya-saMyamasya sthita-praj~naM prati lakShaNatvasya mumukShuM prati praj~nA-sAdhanatvasya copasaMharaNIyatvAt ||68||

vishvanAthaH : yasya nigR^ihIta-manasaH | he mahA-bAho ! iti yathA shatrUn nigR^ihNAsi, tathA mano 'pi nigR^ihANeti bhAvaH ||68||

baladevaH : tasmAd iti | yasya man-niShTha-manasaH pratiShThitAtma-niShThA bhavati | he mahAbAho iti yathA ripUn nigR^ihNAsi tathendriyANi nigR^ihANety arthaH | ebhiH shlokair bhagavan-niviShTatayendriya-vijayaH sthita-praj~nasya siddhasya svAbhAvikaH | sAdhakasya tu sAdhana-bhUta iti bodhyam ||68||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.69

yA nishA sarva-bhUtAnAM tasyAM jAgarti saMyamI |
yasyAM jAgrati bhUtAni sA nishA pashyato muneH ||69||

shrIdharaH : nanu na kashcid api prasupta iva darshanAdi-vyApAra-shUnyaH sarvAtmanA nigR^ihItendriyo loke dR^ishyate | ato 'saktAvitam idaM lakShaNam ity AshaN^kyAha yA nisheti | sarveShAM bhUtAnAM yA nishA | nisheva nishA Atma-niShThA | aj~nAna-dhvAntAvR^ita-matInAM tasyAM darshanAdi-vyApArAbhAvAt | tasyAM Atma-niShThAyAM saMyamI nigR^ihItendriyo jAgrati prabudhyante | sAtma-tattvaM pashyato muner nishA | tasyAM darshanAdi-vyApAras tasya nAsti ity arthaH | etad uktaM bhavati - yathA divAndhAnAm ulukAdInAM rAtrAv eva darshanaM na tu divase | evaM brahmaj~nasyonmIlitAkShasyApi brahmaNy eva dR^iShTiH | na tu viShayeShu | ato nAsambhAvitam idaM lakShaNam iti ||69||

madhusUdanaH : tad evaM mumukShuNA praj~nA-sthairyAya prayatna-pUrvakam indriya-saMyamaH kartavya ity uktaM sthita-praj~nasya tu svataH siddha eva sarvendriya-saMyama ity Aha yA nisheti | yA vedAnta-vAkya-janita-sAkShAtkAra-rUpAhaM brahmAsmIti  praj~nA sarva-bhUtAnAm aj~nAnAM nisheva nishA tAn praty aprakAsha-rUpatvAt | tasyAM brahma-vidyA-lakShaNAyAM sarva-bhUta-nishAyAM jAgarti aj~nAna-nidrAyAH prabuddhaH san sAvadhAno vartate saMyamIndriya-saMyamavAn sthita-praj~na ity arthaH | yasyAM tu dvaita-darshana-lakShaNAyAm avidyA-nidrAyAM prasuptAny eva bhUtAni jAgrati svapnavad vyavaharanti sA nishA na prakAshata Atma-tattvaM pashyato 'parokShatayA muneH sthita-praj~nasya | yAvad dhi na prabudhyate tAvad eva svapna-darshanaM bodhya-paryantatvAd bhramasya tattva-j~nAna-kAle tu na bhrama-nimittaH kashcid vyavahAraH | tad uktaM vArtika-kAraiH -

kAraka-vyavahAre hi shuddhaM vastu na vIkShyante |
shuddhe vastuni siddhe ca kAraka-vyApR^itis tathA ||
kAkolUka-nishevAyaM saMsAro 'j~nAtma-vedinoH |
yA nishA sarva-bhUtAnAm ity avocat svayaM hariH || iti |

tathA ca yasya viparIta-darshanaM tasya na vastu-darshanaM viparIta-darshanasya vastv-adarshana-janyatvAt | yasya ca vastu-darshanaM tasya na viparIta-darshanaM viparIta-darshana-kAraNasya vastv-adarshanasya vastu-darshanena bAdhitatvAt | tathA ca shrutiH - yatra vA anyad iva syAt tatrAnyo 'nyat pashyet | yatra svasya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet || iti vidyAvidyayor vyavasthAm Aha | yathA kAkasya rAtry-andhasya dinam ulUkasya divAndhasya nishA rAtrau pashyatash colUkasya yad dinaM rAtrir eva sA kAkasyeti mahad Ashcaryam etat | atas tattva-darshibhiH katham Avidyaka-kriyA-kArakAdi-vyavahAraH syAd iti svataH siddha eva tasyendriya-saMyama ity arthaH ||69||

vishvanAthaH : sthita-praj~nasya tu svataH-siddha eva sarvendriya-nigraha ity Aha yeti | buddhir hi dvividhA bhavati Atma-pravaNA viShaya-pravaNA ca | tatra yA Atma-pravaNA buddhiH sA sarva-bhUtAnAM nishA | nishAyAM kiM kiM syAd iti tasyAM svapanto janA yathA na jAnanti, tathaiva Atma-pravaNa-buddhau prApyamANaM vastu sarva-bhUtAni na jAnanti | kintu tasyAM saMyamI sthita-praj~no jAgarti | na tu svapiti | ata Atma-buddhi-niShTham AnandaM sAkShAd anubhavati | yasyAM viShaya-pravaNAyAM buddhau bhUtAni jAgrati, tan-niShThaM viShaya-sukha-shoka-mohAdikaM sAkShAd anubhavanti na tu tatra svapanti | sA muneH sthita-praj~nasya nishA tan-niShThaM kim api nAnubhavati ity arthaH | kintu pashyataH sAMsArikAnAM sukha-duHkha-pradAn viShayAn tatraudAsInyenAvalokayataH svabhogyAn viShayAn api yathocitaM nirlepam AdadAnasyety arthaH ||69||

baladevaH : sAdhakAvasthasya sthita-praj~nasyendriya-saMyamaH prayatna-sAdhya ity uktam | siddhAvasthasya tu tasya tan-niyamaH svAbhAvika ity Aha yA nisheti | viviktAtma-niShThA viShaya-niShThA ceti buddhir dvividhA | yAtma-niShThA buddhiH sarva-bhUtAnAM nishA-rUpakeNopamAtra vyajyate rAtri-tulyA tadvad aprakAshikA | rAtrAv ivAtma-niShThAyAM buddhau svapanto janAs tal-labhyam AtmAnaM sarve nAnubhavantIty arthaH | saMyamI jitendriyas tu tasyAM jAgarti na tu svapiti | tayA labhyam AtmAnam anubhavatIty arthaH | yasyAM viShya-niShThAyAM buddhau bhUtAnio jAgrati viShaya-bhogAn anubhavanti na tu tatra svapanti sA muneH sthita-praj~nasya nishA | tasya viShaya-bhogAprakAshikety arthaH | kIdR^ishasyety Aha pashyata iti | AtmAnaM sAkShAd anubhavataH prArabdhaAkR^iShTAn viShayAn apy audAsInyena bhu¤jAnasya cety arthaH | nartakI-mUrdha-ghaTAvadhAna-nyAyenAtma-dR^iShTer na tad-anya-rasa-graha iti bhAvaH | 

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.70

ApUryamANam acala-pratiShThaM
samudram ApaH pravishanti yadvat |
tadvat kAmA yaM pravishanti sarve
sa shAntim Apnoti na kAma-kAmI ||70||

shrIdharaH : nanu viShayeShu dR^iShTy-abhAve katham asau tAn bhuN^kte ity apekShAyAm Aha ApUryamANam iti | nAnA-nada-nadInbhir ApUryamANam api acala-pratiShTham anatikrAnta-maryAdam eva samudraM punar api anyA Apo yathA pravishanti tathA kAmA viShayA yaM munim antar-dR^iShTiM bhogair avikriyamANam eva prArabdha-karmabhir AkShiptAH santaH pravishanti sa shAntim kaivalyaM prApnoti | na tu kAma-kAmI bhoga-kAmanA-shIlaH ||70||

madhusUdanaH : etAdR^ishasya sthita-praj~nasya sarva-vikShepa-shAntir apy artha-siddheti sa-dR^iShTAntam Aha ApUryamANam iti | sarvAbhir nadIbhir ApUryamANaM santaM vR^iShTy-Adi-prabhavA api sarvA ApaH samudraM pravishanti | kIdR^isham acala-pratiShTham anatikrAnta-maryAdam | acalAnAM mainAkAdInAM pratiShThA yasminn iti vA gAmbhIryAtishaya uktaH | yadvad yena prakAreNa nirvikAratvena tadvat tenaiva nirvikAratva-prakAreNa yaM sthita-praj~naM nirvikAram eva santaM kAmA aj~nair lokaiH kAmyamAnAH shabdAdyAH sarve viShayA avarjanIyatayA prArabdha-karma-vashAt pravishanti na tu vikartuM shaknuvanti sa mahA-samudra-sthAnIyaH sthita-praj~naH shAntiM sarva-laukikAlaukika-karma-vikShepa-nivR^ittiM bAdhitAnuvR^ittAvidyA-kArya-nivR^ittiM cApnoti j~nAna-balena | na kAma-kAmI kAmAn viShayAn kAmayituM shIlaM yasya sa kAma-kAmy aj~naH shAntiM samAkhyAtAM nApnoti | api tu sarvadA laukikAlaukika-karma-vikShepeNa mahati kleshArNave magno bhavatIti vAkyArthaH | etena j~nAnina eva phala-bhUto vidvat-saMnyAsas tasyaiva ca sarva-vikShepa-nivR^itti-rUpA jIvan-muktir daivAddhnIna-viShaya-bhoge 'pi nirvikAratety-Adikam uktaM veditavyam ||70||

vishvanAthaH : viShaya-grahaNe kShobha-rAhityam eva nirlepety Aha ApUryamANam iti | yathA varShAsu itas tataH nAdeyA ApaH samudraM pravishanti kIdR^isham | A IShad api ApUryamANam tAvatIbhir apy adbhiH pUrayituM na shakyam | acala-pratiShTham anatikrAnta-maryAdaM tadvad eva kAmA viShayA yaM pravishanti bhogyatvenAyAnti | yathA apAM praveshe apraveshe vA samudro na kam api visheSham Apadyate | evam eva yaH kAmAnAM bhoge abhoge ca kShobha-rahita eva syAt sa sthita-praj~naH | shAntiM j~nAnam ||70||

baladevaH : uktaM bhAvaM sphuTayann Aha ApUryeti | svarUpeNaivApUryamANaM tathApy acala-pratiShTham anullaN^ghita-velaM samudraM yathApo 'nyA varShodbhavA nadyaH pravishanti, na tu tatra ki¤cid visheShaM shaknuvanti kartuM, tadvat sarve kAmAH prArabdhAkR^iShTA viShayA yaM pravishanti na tu vikartuM prabhavanti sa shAntim Apnoti | shabdAdiShu tad indriya-gocareShv api sat svAtmAnandAnubhava-tR^iptair vikAra-lesham apy avindan sthita-praj~na ity arthaH | yaH kAma-kAmI viShaya-lipsuH sa tUkta-lakShaNAM shAntiM nApnoti ||70||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.71

vihAya kAmAn yaH sarvAn pumAMsh carati niHspR^ihaH |
nirmamo nirahaMkAraH sa shAntim adhigacchati ||71||

shrIdharaH : yasmAd evaM tasmAt vihAyeti | prAptAn kAmAn vihAya tyaktvopekShya aprApteShu ca niHspR^ihaH yato nirahaN^kAro 'taeva tad-bhoga-sAdhaneShu nirmamaH sann antar-dR^iShTir bhUtvA yash carati prArabdha-vashena bhogAn bhuN^kte | yatra kutrApi gacchati vA | sa shAntim prApnoti ||71||

madhusUdanaH : yasmAd evaM tasmAt vihAyeti | prAptAn api sarvAn bAhyAn gR^iha-kShetrAdInAntarAn manorAjya-rUpAn vAsanA-mAtra-rUpAMsh ca pathi gacchaMs tR^iNa-sparsha-rUpAn kAmAMs trividhAn vihAyopekShya sharIra-jIvana-mAtre 'pi nispR^ihaH san | yato nirahaN^kAra sharIrendriyAdAv ayam aham ity abhimAna-shUnyaH | vidyAvattvAdi-nimittAtma-sambhAvanA-rahita iti vA | ato nirmamaH sharIra-yAtrA-mAtrArthe 'pi prArabdha-karmAkShipte kaupInAcchAdanAdau mamedam ity abhimAna-varjitaH san yaH pumAMsh carati prArabdha-karma-vashena bhogAn bhuN^kte yAdR^icchikatayA yatra kvApi gacchatIti vA | sa evaMbhUtaH sthita-praj~naH shAntiM sarva-saMsAra-duHkhoparama-lakShaNAm avidyA-tat-kArya-nivR^ittim adhigacchati j~nAna-balena prApnoti | tad etad IdR^ishaM vrajanaM sthita-praj~nasyeti caturtha-prashnasyottaraM parisamAptam ||71||

vishvanAthaH : kashcit tu kAmeShu avishvasan naiva tAn bhuN^kte ity Aha | vihAyeti nirahaN^kAro nirmama iti deha-daihikeShu ahaMtA-mamatA-shUnyaH ||71||

baladevaH : vihAyeti | prAptAn kAmAn viShayAn sarvAn vihAya sharIropajIvana-mAtre 'pi nirmamo mamtA-shUnyaH nirahaN^kAro 'nAtmani sharIre AtmAbhimAna-shUnyash carati tad-upajIvana-mAtraM bhakShayati yatra kvApi gacchati vA sa shAntiM labhate iti vrajeta kim ity asyottaram ||71||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 2.72

eShA brAhmI sthitiH pArtha nainAM prApya vimuhyati |
sthitvAsyAm anta-kAle 'pi brahma-nirvANam R^icchati ||72||

shrIdharaH : uktAM j~nAna-niShThAM stuvann upasaMharati eSheti | brAhmI sthitir brahma-j~nAna-niShThA | eShaivaMvidhA | enAM parameshvarArAdhanena vishuddhAntaHkaraNaH pumAn prApya na vimuhyati | punaH saMsAra-mohaM na prApnoti | yato 'nta-kAle mR^ityu-samaye 'py asyAM lakSha-mAtram api sthitvA brahma-nirvANam brahmaNi nirvANaM layam R^icchati prApnoti | kiM punar vaktavyaM bAlyam Arabhya sthitvA prApnotIti ||72||

shoka-paN^ka-nimagnaM yaH sAN^khya-yogopadeshataH |
ujjahArArjunaM bhaktaM sa kR^iShNa-sharaNaM mama ||

iti shrI-shrIdhara-svAmikR^itAyAM bhagavad-gItA-TIkAyAM subodhinyAM 
dvitIyo 'dhyAyaH 
||2||

madhusUdanaH : tad evaM caturNAM prashnAnAm uttara-vyAjena sarvANi sthita-praj~na-lakShaNAni mumukShu-kartavyatayA kathitAni | samprati karma-yoga-phala-bhUtAM sAN^khya-niShThAM stuvann upasaMharati eSheti | eShA sthita-praj~na-lakShaNa-vyAjena kathitA | eShA te 'bhihitA sAN^khye buddhir iti ca prAg uktA sthitir niShThA sarva-karma-saMnyAsa-pUrvaka-paramAtma-j~nAna-lakShaNA brAhmI brahma-viShayA | he pArtha ! enAM sthitiM prApya yaH kashcid api pnar na vimuhyati | na hi j~nAna-bAdhitasyAj~nAnasya punaH sambhavo 'sti anAditvenotpatty-asambhavAt | asyAM sthitAv anta-kAle 'pi antye 'pi vaayasi sthitvA brahma-nirvANaM brahmaNi nirvANaM nirvR^ittiM brahma-rUpaM nirvANam iti vA | R^icchati gacchaty abhedena | kim u vaktavyaM yo bramacaryAd eva saMnyasya yAvaj-jIvam asyAM brAhmyAM sthitAv avatiShThate sa brahma-nirvANam R^icchatIty api-shabdArthaH ||72||

iti shrImat-paramahaMsa-parivrAjakAcArya-shrI-vishveshvara-sarasvatI-pAda-shiShya-shrI-madhusUdana-sarasvatI-viracitAyAM shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-gUDhArtha-dIpikAyAm sarva-gItArtha-sUtraNaM nAma 
dvitIyo 'dhyAyaH ||2||

vishvanAthaH : upasaMharati eSheti | brAhmI brahma-prApikA | anta-kAle mR^ityu-samaye 'pi | kiM punar AbAlyam ||72||

j~nAnaM karma ca vispaShTam aspaShTaM bhaktim uktavAn |
ataevAyam adhyAyaH shrI-gItA-sUtram ucyate ||
iti sArArtha-varShiNyAM harShiNyAM bhakta-cetasAm |
shrI-gItAsu dvitIyo 'yaM saN^gataH saN^gataH satAm ||2||

baladevaH : sthita-praj~natAM stauti eSheti | brAhmI brahma-prApikA | anta-kAle carame vayasi | kiM punar AkaumAraM brahma R^icchati labhate | nirvANam amR^ita-rUpaM tat pradam ity arthaH | nanu tasyAM sthitaH kathaM brahma prApnoti | tat-prAptes tad-bhakti-hetukatvAd iti ced ucyate | tasyAs tad-bhakti-hetukatvAt tad-bhakti-hetutvAc ca tat-prApakateti ||72||
niShkAma-karmabhir j~nAnI harim eva smaran bhavet |
anyathA vighna eveti dvitIyo 'dhyAya-nirNayaH ||

iti shrImad-bhagavad-gItopaniShad-bhAShye dvitIyo 'dhyAyaH |
||2||




[*ENDNOTE] Only found in Manu.
[*ENDNOTE] This is a reference to chapter 11.25. See VCT to 18.28.
